# SSOT-Loop Log

> Append-only log of every loop-brief iteration (Brief 061). Cowork reads the latest entries to plan resolver briefs, vocabulary expansions, and mini-fixes. Pro Iteration ein H2-Block.
>
> Status: ✅ committed | ⏸ resolver-pause | ✋ skip-50-stop | 🏁 loop-complete

## 2026-05-12 · ssot-w40k-002 · W40K-0011..W40K-0020 · ✅

- **Cumulative books in authority:** 20 / 50 to next resolver pause (10 before this batch + 10 written here)
- **CC model:** claude-opus-4-7
- **Pre-check:** Detected existing `manual-overrides-ssot-w40k-001.json` (10 books) — no other files. W40K max = 1, HH max = 0, cumulative = 10, 10 % 50 ≠ 0 → no resolver pause. Next batch: `ssot-w40k-002`, slice = W40K-0011..W40K-0020.
- **WebSearch:** mean ≈ 1.2 / book, max = 2 (over 10 books). 12 total searches.
  - 2 searches: W40K-0011 *Penitent* (Bequin trilogy — needed plot detail on the King-in-Yellow arc), W40K-0019 *The Last Ditch* (needed Lexicanum-confirmation that the buried threat is a 7000-year-old Tyranid hive ship, not just "an older enemy")
  - 1 search each: W40K-0012..0018, W40K-0020
- **Per-book bullets:**
  - **W40K-0011 *Penitent* (Abnett, 2021):** Bequin trilogy book 2. POV Beta Bequin, Sancour/Queen Mab, Eisenhorn vs Ravenor cold war + Cognitae + King in Yellow. Solid coverage from training data + 2 WebSearches. Clean tags, no flags.
  - **W40K-0012 *For the Emperor* (Mitchell, 2003):** Ciaphas Cain series-start. Gravalax, Tau-border crisis + hidden genestealer conspiracy. Establishes Cain/Jurgen/Vail/Kasteen/Broklaw cast. Clean.
  - **W40K-0013 *Caves of Ice* (Mitchell, 2004):** Cain book 2. Simia Orichalcae, surface war with Orks + underground Necron tomb. Clean.
  - **W40K-0014 *The Traitor's Hand* (Mitchell, 2005):** Cain book 3. Adumbria, Slaaneshi cult + inter-regimental rivalry with Tomas Beije (Tallarn 229th). Clean.
  - **W40K-0015 *Death or Glory* (Mitchell, 2006):** Cain book 4. Roster typo "Death of Glory" → corrected in-place to "Death or Glory" in `book-roster.json` (title + slug `death-or-glory`) on maintainer instruction; no `data_conflict` flag committed. ⚠ **Excel-SSOT-Quelle** (`Warhammer_Books_SSOT.xlsx`) trägt den Typo weiterhin — Maintainer muss dort dieselbe Korrektur fahren, sonst regeneriert `import-ssot-roster.ts` den Fehler. Chronologically a prequel to *For the Emperor* — Cain's first big exploit on Perlia behind enemy Ork lines vs Warboss Gargash Korbul. Tagged entry_point=standalone because the book itself frames as Vail unearthing a younger memoir; the rest of the series doesn't strictly require it.
  - **W40K-0016 *Duty Calls* (Mitchell, 2007):** Cain book 5. Periremunda — Tyranids + emerging Chaos cult + hidden genestealer hybrids in the planetary administration. Vail returns actively. Opens the loose "Shadowlight" arc that closes in book 6.
  - **W40K-0017 *Cain's Last Stand* (Mitchell, 2008):** Cain book 6. Perlia revisited, 13th-Black-Crusade splinter under Warmaster Varan, Shadowlight artefact in the Valley of Daemons. Despite the title, NOT the series finale (three more books follow) — tagged mid_series. Tonally the darkest of the early Cain memoirs; grimdark kept in tone-tags as an exception.
  - **W40K-0018 *The Emperor's Finest* (Mitchell, 2011):** Cain book 7. Viridia, Reclaimers Space Marine chapter, space hulk with awakening Tyranids + stowaway Orks + Mira Sulla subplot. Reclaimers is a Cain-novel-exclusive homebrew Astartes chapter — no canonical-tab Surface-Form match expected.
  - **W40K-0019 *The Last Ditch* (Mitchell, 2012):** Cain book 8. Nusquam Fundumentibus, Ork campaign + 7000-year-buried Tyranid hive ship reveal. Strategic stakes are higher than the on-world fight — implied galactic-scale rewrite of Tyranid-arrival chronology.
  - **W40K-0020 *The Greater Good* (Mitchell, 2013):** Cain book 9. Quadravidia, Damocles Gulf. Tau invasion → temporary Imperium-Tau alliance vs incoming Tyranid hive fleet. Earth Caste secret experiment subplot. Scope=sector because Damocles is a sector-scale theatre.
- **value_outside_vocabulary** (candidates surfaced by this batch, none promoted):
  - `prequel` — entry_point category has no `prequel` value; W40K-0015 *Death or Glory* is structurally a prequel within Cain's memoir frame. Covered weakly by `standalone`.
  - `unreliable_narrator` / `memoir_frame` — Cain books are framed as Cain's memoir edited and footnoted by Vail. No theme-tag captures this.
  - `dark_comedy` — Cain's tone is satirical + grim-setting, partially covered by `satirical`, but the combination (grim setting / comic narration) is distinctive enough to consider its own tag.
  - `commissar` — protagonist_class has no `commissar`. Cain is technically Officio Prefectus, tagged here as `guardsman` (closest available).
- **Notable surface-form frequencies within this batch:**
  - *Factions:* Imperial Guard ×9, Commissariat ×9, Inquisition ×6, Ordo Xenos ×3, Tyranids ×4, Orks ×4, Chaos ×4, Genestealer Cults ×3, Tau Empire ×2, Adeptus Mechanicus ×2, Necrons ×1, Slaanesh ×1, Cognitae ×1, Black Legion ×1, Space Marines ×1, Reclaimers ×1.
  - *Locations:* Perlia ×2 (W40K-0015 + W40K-0017); each other locale unique to one book.
  - *Characters:* Ciaphas Cain ×9 (POV), Jurgen ×9, Amberley Vail ×9, Regina Kasteen ×5, Ruput Broklaw ×4. Penitent (W40K-0011) inherits Eisenhorn/Ravenor/Cherubael cast carried over from the ssot-w40k-001 Bequin opener.
- **Notes:**
  - Inquisition-consistency constraint (brief 061): held for every Cain book. Vail is on-page or in framing across all nine; Inquisition + Ordo Xenos listed even where she's framing-only, because the books explicitly treat her edits as Inquisitorial supervision of the memoir.
  - "Imperial Guard" used over "Astra Militarum" (publication era 2003-2013, lore-name change to Astra Militarum came post-2014). "Tau Empire" used over "T'au" (post-9th-edition spelling). Both are deliberate publication-era surface-form treue, not retconning.
  - Tone choice: `satirical + action_heavy` is the Cain default in this batch; `grimdark` kept only on *Cain's Last Stand* (the darker entry). Eisenhorn-batch had `grimdark` on everything — that's not a useful default for the Cain books, which are deliberately comic-grim.
  - No Omnibus/Collection in this slice — all ten are novels per SSOT + per all sources.

## 2026-05-12 · ssot-w40k-003 · W40K-0021..W40K-0030 · ✅

- **Cumulative books in authority:** 30 / 50 to next resolver pause (20 before this batch + 10 written here)
- **CC model:** claude-opus-4-7
- **Pre-check:** Detected existing `manual-overrides-ssot-w40k-001.json` (10 books) + `manual-overrides-ssot-w40k-002.json` (10 books, just restored from orphaned commits `ba89e9f` + `e8bf80a`). W40K max = 2, HH max = 0, cumulative = 20, 20 % 50 ≠ 0 → no resolver pause. Next batch: `ssot-w40k-003`, slice = W40K-0021..W40K-0030 (3 late Ciaphas Cain + 7 early Gaunt's Ghosts).
- **WebSearch:** mean ≈ 0.6 / book, max = 1 (over 10 books). 6 total searches.
  - 1 search each: W40K-0021 *Choose Your Enemies* (Drechia + Ironfound forge-world subplot via Track of Words / Lexicanum), W40K-0022 *Vainglorious* (Ironfound Mechanicus heresy + Damocles Gulf via Lexicanum / Simon & Schuster), W40K-0023 *Old Soldiers Never Die* (Lentonia zombie outbreak + 2012 Weekender-exclusive release via Lexicanum / Goodreads), W40K-0025 *Ghostmaker* (linked-short-story structure + Monthax frame via Wikipedia / Fandom — surfaced the `data_conflict` flag for format), W40K-0026 *Necropolis* (Vervunhive/Ferrozoica + Heritor Asphodel + Verghastite-founding via Fandom / Goodreads), W40K-0030 *Sabbat Martyr* (Civitas Beati siege + nine assassins per Holy Wound + Enok Innokenti via Gaunt's Ghostspedia)
  - 0 searches: W40K-0024 *First and Only*, W40K-0027 *Honour Guard*, W40K-0028 *The Guns of Tanith*, W40K-0029 *Straight Silver* (Founding-trilogy + Saint-tetralogy are well covered in training data)
- **Per-book bullets:**
  - **W40K-0021 *Choose Your Enemies* (Mitchell, 2018):** Cain book 10, late-period after the long Mitchell hiatus. Drechia ice world, Eldar pirate raids fronting a Chaos cult inside the local PDF, with the trail pointing forward to forge world Ironfound. Damocles Gulf frame continues from *The Greater Good*. Tone stays satirical + action_heavy. Clean.
  - **W40K-0022 *Vainglorious* (Mitchell, 2023):** Cain book 11, direct sequel to *Choose Your Enemies*. Forge world Ironfound, mutinous Skitarii + Adeptus Mechanicus heresy, assassination attempts on Cain. First time the series tags Adeptus Mechanicus as an antagonist surface form. `political_thriller` tag added for the magos-hierarchy intrigue. Clean.
  - **W40K-0023 *Old Soldiers Never Die* (Mitchell, 2012/2020):** Cain novella. Originally a 500-copy Black-Library-Weekender-2012 limited release, wider release 2020. Lentonia, post-insurrection peacekeeping that becomes a zombie-outbreak survival story when a warp-tainted infection sweeps the Astra Militarum ranks. Format-compliance: `length_tier=novella` (medium remains `book`; the facet-catalog `format` taxonomy has no novella variant — novella belongs in length_tier). Grimdark kept in tone-tags because the zombie horror register pushes the prose darker than typical Cain.
  - **W40K-0024 *First and Only* (Abnett, 1999):** Gaunt's Ghosts series-start, Founding-trilogy book 1. Sabbat Worlds Crusade opener — Slaydo dies, Macaroth inherits. Voltemand → Pyrites → Fortis Binary → Menazoid Epsilon. Introduces the Tanith First-and-Only cast (Corbec, Rawne, Larkin, Mkoll, Bragg, Caffran, Milo, Dorden) and the Lord General Dravere / Jantine Patricians internal-Imperium antagonist axis. Clean, no flags.
  - **W40K-0025 *Ghostmaker* (Abnett, 2000):** Gaunt's Ghosts Founding-trilogy book 2. Structurally a fix-up of linked Inferno!-magazine short stories framed by Monthax present-day chapters — confirmed by Wikipedia + Fandom + Black Library descriptions. SSOT roster lists `novel`; **`data_conflict` flag set with `field: format`, `suggestion: collection`**, reason logged. Each major Ghost gets a flashback POV chapter (9 POV characters tagged accordingly).
  - **W40K-0026 *Necropolis* (Abnett, 2000):** Gaunt's Ghosts Founding-trilogy book 3. Vervunhive siege on Verghast — Heritor Asphodel's Zoican Host vs the Imperial relief force. Doorstopper length (length_tier=doorstopper, ~600+ pages). Founds the regiment's second intake — **Verghastite Ghosts** as a new faction surface form (Soric, Criid, Kolea, Banda, Hark). `siege` + `war_story` primary plot tags. Ensemble POV (multi-character battlefield map).
  - **W40K-0027 *Honour Guard* (Abnett, 2001):** Gaunt's Ghosts Saint-tetralogy book 1 (Gaunt's Ghosts #4). Hagia, Saint Sabbat's homeworld, pilgrim's-way escort of the Saint's relics under Chaos pursuit + internal mutiny. Introduces Sanian (the Hagian priestess who will recur in *Sabbat Martyr*) and the Gaunt vs Lord General Lugo political axis. Plot-type=journey, theme heavy on faith. Clean.
  - **W40K-0028 *The Guns of Tanith* (Abnett, 2002):** Gaunt's Ghosts Saint-tetralogy book 2 (#5). Phantine — airborne hive-spire assault, Cirenholm + Ouranberg. Introduces **Phantine Air Corps** + **Urdeshi** as new ally surface forms, and **Blood Pact** as the main Crusade-era Chaos antagonist (recurring forward through the series). Caffran's trial subplot. Clean.
  - **W40K-0029 *Straight Silver* (Abnett, 2002):** Gaunt's Ghosts Saint-tetralogy book 3 (#6). Aexe Cardinal — Great-War-style trench warfare against the Shadik / Blood Pact, with the Aexegarian factional dispute as the political backdrop. Introduces **Lijah Cuu** (the killer-among-the-Ghosts arc tightens around Larkin). **Aexegarian Forces** as a new surface form. Tone heavy somber. Clean.
  - **W40K-0030 *Sabbat Martyr* (Abnett, 2003):** Gaunt's Ghosts Saint-tetralogy book 4 / series turning point (#7). Herodor, Civitas Beati — reincarnated Saint Sabbat (in Sanian's body, manipulated by Lugo) vs **Enok Innokenti**'s nine specialised assassins (one per Holy Wound). Siege climax. Saint Sabbat dies; series pivots. Doorstopper length. Clean.
- **value_outside_vocabulary** (candidates surfaced by this batch, none promoted):
  - `commissar` — protagonist_class has no `commissar`. Both Cain and Gaunt are Officio Prefectus, tagged here as `guardsman` (closest available; same workaround as the ssot-w40k-002 Cain slice).
  - `fix_up` / `linked_short_stories` — no plot_type or format value captures the *Ghostmaker* shape. Workaround used: `data_conflict` flag with `format=collection`; the actual character_study + war_story plot_type pairing approximates intent.
  - `commando` / `scout` — Tanith First-and-Only is structurally a Crusade-era scout/recon regiment, but `protagonist_class` doesn't distinguish that from line infantry. Treated as `guardsman`.
  - `trench_warfare` — *Straight Silver*'s register isn't well captured by `siege` + `war_story`; would be a useful sub-tag for WWI-style attritional fronts.
- **Notable surface-form frequencies within this batch:**
  - *Factions:* Imperial Guard ×10, Commissariat ×10, Chaos ×10, Tanith First-and-Only ×7, Verghastite Ghosts ×5, Blood Pact ×3, Valhallan 597th ×3, Inquisition ×2, Ordo Xenos ×2, Eldar ×2, Ecclesiarchy ×2, Adeptus Mechanicus ×1, Skitarii ×1, Jantine Patricians ×1, Vervunhive Militia ×1, Zoican Host ×1, Phantine Air Corps ×1, Urdeshi ×1, Aexegarian Forces ×1.
  - *Locations:* Sabbat Worlds ×7 (mentioned/secondary frame across the Gaunt's Ghosts slice — the Crusade umbrella), Damocles Gulf ×2 (W40K-0021 + W40K-0022 — continuation of the Cain late-period subplot from *The Greater Good*), Ironfound ×2 (W40K-0021 mentioned + W40K-0022 primary). Every other locale unique to one book.
  - *Characters:* Ibram Gaunt ×7 (POV in all Gaunt's Ghosts books), Colm Corbec ×7, Elim Rawne ×7, Hlaine Larkin ×7, Viktor Hark ×5, Oan Mkoll ×5, Caffran ×3, Tona Criid ×3, Ciaphas Cain ×3 (POV in 3 Cain books), Jurgen ×3, Bragg ×2, Brin Milo ×2, Tolin Dorden ×2, Amberley Vail ×2, Regina Kasteen ×2, Ruput Broklaw ×2, Sanian ×2 (W40K-0027 + W40K-0030 — same character, follow-up), Lord General Lugo ×2 (W40K-0027 + W40K-0030 — antagonist continuity).
- **Notes:**
  - Format-compliance flagged: **W40K-0025 *Ghostmaker*** `data_conflict { field: "format", suggestion: "collection" }`. Wikipedia + Fandom + multiple reviews confirm the book is a fix-up of Inferno!-magazine short stories with a Monthax wraparound; SSOT roster lists `novel`. Resolver-brief later can decide whether to promote `collection`/`fix_up` into the format taxonomy or keep `novel` as the umbrella.
  - W40K-0023 *Old Soldiers Never Die* is the first **novella** in the authority layer (Cain Weekender exclusive). Tagged `length_tier=novella`; medium stays `book`. No format conflict — the SSOT roster correctly lists `novella` as the format.
  - Surface-form treue: "Imperial Guard" over "Astra Militarum" (publication era 1999-2003 for Founding+Saint, 2018-2023 for late Cain; Cain himself uses "Imperial Guard" throughout the series). "Eldar" over "Aeldari" (pre-9th-edition spelling, *Ghostmaker* is 2000). "Blood Pact" enters the canonical Crusade antagonist set with *The Guns of Tanith* (2002).
  - Inquisition-consistency constraint (brief 061): not triggered. No Inquisitor POVs in this batch — Cain is Officio Prefectus (Commissariat); Gaunt is Colonel-Commissar (Commissariat). Amberley Vail appears in the Cain books as supporting Inquisition liaison, kept consistent with the ssot-w40k-002 pattern.
  - Two Cain late-period books (Choose Your Enemies, Vainglorious) are tonally lighter than Old Soldiers Never Die — `satirical + action_heavy` is the default, `grimdark` dropped for both. Gaunt's Ghosts is uniformly `grimdark + somber + action_heavy + war_story` across all seven entries.
  - Loop-Brief 061 file-restoration commit (Phase A this session, see `git log --oneline -1 -- scripts/seed-data/manual-overrides-ssot-w40k-002.json`) brought back the previously orphaned iter-1 work. The DB was already in post-002-apply state per the Brief 062 implementer report; no DB action needed for 002, only file recovery on main.

## 2026-05-12 · ssot-w40k-004 · W40K-0031..W40K-0040 · ✅

- **Cumulative books in authority:** 40 / 50 to next resolver pause (30 before this batch + 10 written here)
- **CC model:** claude-opus-4-7
- **Pre-check:** Detected existing `manual-overrides-ssot-w40k-001..003.json` (10 + 10 + 10 = 30 books). W40K max = 3, HH max = 0, cumulative = 30, 30 % 50 ≠ 0 → no resolver pause. Next batch: `ssot-w40k-004`, slice = W40K-0031..W40K-0040 (4 Gaunt's Ghosts *The Lost* + 1 *Blood Pact* bridge + 3 *Victory* + 1 *Ghost Dossier* novella + 1 Founding Omnibus).
- **WebSearch:** mean ≈ 0.5 / book, max = 1 (over 10 books). 5 total searches.
  - 1 search each: W40K-0031 *Traitor General* (confirm the Gereon-12 roster — Rawne/Feygor/Brostin/Mkvenner/Larkin/Beltayn/Criid/Mkoll/Varl/Bonin/Curth + the Landerson hand-off), W40K-0034 *Only in Death* (Hinzerhaus on Jago as fortress-world haunted citadel, defending Imperial left flank), W40K-0036 *Salvation's Reach* (Mabbon-supplied intel as the raid trigger, Felyx Chass as Merity-Chass's-son secret-paternity intro), W40K-0037 *The Warmaster* (Sons-of-Sek-as-Anarch-elite framing + Macaroth-decapitation-attempt arc on Urdesh), W40K-0039 *The Vincula Insurgency* (post-Voltemand prequel setting; Vincula City policing assignment; Ghost Dossier 1 series-positioning).
  - 0 searches: W40K-0032 *His Last Command*, W40K-0033 *The Armour of Contempt*, W40K-0035 *Blood Pact*, W40K-0038 *The Anarch*, W40K-0040 *Founding Omnibus* (Omnibus aggregated from existing W40K-0024/0025/0026 ssot-w40k-003 entries — no independent WebSearch needed).
  - Pre-batch sanity check confirmed via WebSearch on Sabbat Martyr that **Colm Corbec was killed by Lijah Cuu in W40K-0030 *Sabbat Martyr*** (and Cuu killed by Larkin same book) — neither character appears in any synopsis from W40K-0031 forward; Cuu does not appear in any W40K-0031..0040 character list. Caught one potential continuity slip pre-write.
- **Per-book bullets:**
  - **W40K-0031 *Traitor General* (Abnett, 2004):** Gaunt's Ghosts #8, *The Lost* book 1. Twelve-Ghost deep-strike onto Chaos-occupied Gereon to assassinate the traitor Lord General Noches Sturm. Body-horror / partisan-warfare register. Introduces the Gerome Landerson Resistance cell. `journey + mystery` plot-tags. Clean.
  - **W40K-0032 *His Last Command* (Abnett, 2005):** Gaunt's Ghosts #9, *The Lost* book 2. Gereon-survivors extracted back to friendly space; Gaunt demoted from Colonel-Commissar to Commissar, Rawne confirmed in regimental command. Introduces the **Belladon** third intake. Ancreon Sextus battle. `political_thriller` for the demotion politics; `doubt + betrayal` themes. Clean.
  - **W40K-0033 *The Armour of Contempt* (Abnett, 2006):** Gaunt's Ghosts #10, *The Lost* book 3. Imperial liberation of Gereon. Dual-track: Gaunt's command level + Dalin Criid (Tona's adopted son) joining the regiment through Belladon recruit training under Hark. **First POV slot for Dalin Criid** — generational hand-off begins. Clean.
  - **W40K-0034 *Only in Death* (Abnett, 2007):** Gaunt's Ghosts #11, *The Lost* closer. Hinzerhaus citadel on fortress-world Jago — haunted-house horror register over a Blood-Pact siege procedural. `mystery + siege + cosmic_horror` plot-tag combo. Tonally the darkest of the Lost arc. Clean.
  - **W40K-0035 *Blood Pact* (Abnett, 2009):** Gaunt's Ghosts #12. Balhaut / Balopolis furlough setting; **Etogaur Mabbon interrogation** opens the Victory-arc tactical setup. Three rogue **Sirkle**-named Inquisitorial agents try to kill Mabbon; Rawne runs the protective detail. `political_thriller + mystery + cw_crime`. Clean.
  - **W40K-0036 *Salvation's Reach* (Abnett, 2011):** Gaunt's Ghosts #13, Victory #1. Heist procedural through Sek's space-hulk archive deep in Archenemy space. **Felyx Chass introduced** as the teenage Verghastite intake who is in fact Gaunt's secret son by Merity Chass. First appearance of **Sons of Sek** as a faction surface form. `heist + political_thriller`. Clean.
  - **W40K-0037 *The Warmaster* (Abnett, 2017):** Gaunt's Ghosts #14, Victory #2. Urdesh / Eltath forge-world campaign with Macaroth in personal command. Sons of Sek as the elite Archenemy infantry; Anakwanar Sek as the Archenemy-level antagonist; decapitation-strike framing. Doorstopper length (length_tier=doorstopper). `siege + political_thriller`. Surface form **Urdeshi** introduced. Clean.
  - **W40K-0038 *The Anarch* (Abnett, 2019):** Gaunt's Ghosts #15, Victory #3. Eltath finale — Sek arrives on-planet in person to assassinate Macaroth. Series-climax siege of the command palaces. **Rawne shares POV** with Gaunt (first time since *His Last Command* outside Salvation's Reach raid coverage). Sek dies; major regiment losses. `last_stand + siege + political_thriller`. Doorstopper. Clean.
  - **W40K-0039 *The Vincula Insurgency* (Abnett, 2021):** *Ghost Dossier 1*, supplementary-series novella **set chronologically before First and Only** — post-Voltemand garrison-duty on Vincula City. Counterinsurgency procedural with slow-mystery spine; reveals dark truths about the regiment's own origins. `novella` length_tier, `mystery + political_thriller`. Note: chronological prequel, but entry_point still tagged `mid_series` because real-world publication slots it deep into the series (readers come to it knowing the Tanith well).
  - **W40K-0040 *Gaunt's Ghosts: The Founding Omnibus, 1-3* (Abnett, 2003):** **Omnibus aggregation** of W40K-0024 (*First and Only*) + W40K-0025 (*Ghostmaker*) + W40K-0026 (*Necropolis*) — union with highest-role-wins for factions/locations/characters. Length_tier=doorstopper (combined ~1500 pages). Picked `male` over `ensemble` for gender (Gaunt is the throughline POV across all three); picked `series_start` for entry_point (this IS the canonical entry point omnibus for the entire series). No `data_conflict` raised at the omnibus level (Ghostmaker's collection-vs-novel conflict remains pinned to W40K-0025; SSOT-format `omnibus` is correct here).
- **value_outside_vocabulary** (candidates surfaced by this batch, none promoted):
  - `commissar` — protagonist_class still has no `commissar` value. Same workaround as ssot-w40k-002/003 batches: `guardsman`.
  - `regiment-internal` / `unit_history` — *The Vincula Insurgency*'s frame is "how this regiment formed" and *Armour of Contempt*'s Dalin-Criid arc is generational hand-off; neither is well captured by current `theme` values.
  - `body_horror` — *Traitor General* / *Armour of Contempt* / *Only in Death* all run on a stronger body-horror register than `cw_disturbing` alone captures.
  - `prequel` — entry_point has no `prequel` value despite *The Vincula Insurgency* being structurally one. Same gap as W40K-0015 *Death or Glory* in ssot-w40k-002.
  - `counterinsurgency` — *Vincula Insurgency*'s register is not well captured by `war_story` + `mystery` alone.
  - `haunted` / `ghost_story` — *Only in Death*'s Hinzerhaus register; `cosmic_horror` is the closest available tag, but the framing is more haunted-house than cosmic-horror in the Lovecraftian sense.
- **Notable surface-form frequencies within this batch:**
  - *Factions:* Imperial Guard ×10, Tanith First-and-Only ×10, Commissariat ×10, Chaos ×10, Verghastite Ghosts ×9 (every book except Vincula Insurgency — set chronologically pre-Necropolis-founding), Belladon ×7 (His Last Command onwards), Blood Pact ×7, Sons of Sek ×3 (Salvation's Reach + Warmaster + Anarch), Gereon Resistance ×2 (Traitor General + Armour of Contempt), Urdeshi ×2 (Warmaster + Anarch), Inquisition ×1 (Blood Pact only), Imperial Navy ×1 (Salvation's Reach), Adeptus Mechanicus ×1 (Warmaster — forge-world context), Eldar ×1 (Founding Omnibus aggregated from Ghostmaker), Jantine Patricians ×1 (Founding Omnibus aggregated from First and Only), Vervunhive Militia ×1 (Founding Omnibus aggregated from Necropolis), Zoican Host ×1 (Founding Omnibus aggregated from Necropolis).
  - *Locations:* Sabbat Worlds ×10 (Crusade-frame mentioned in every book — full saturation across the batch), Gereon ×2 (Traitor General + Armour of Contempt), Urdesh ×2 + Eltath ×2 (Warmaster + Anarch), Vincula Sub-sector ×1 + Vincula City ×1 + Voltemand mentioned ×2 (Vincula Insurgency + Founding Omnibus aggregated), Jago ×1 + Hinzerhaus ×1 (Only in Death), Ancreon Sextus ×1 (His Last Command), Balhaut ×1 + Balopolis ×1 (Blood Pact), Salvation's Reach ×1 (Salvation's Reach), plus Founding-Omnibus-aggregated Tanith/Pyrites/Fortis Binary/Menazoid Epsilon/Monthax/Verghast/Vervunhive/Ferrozoica (each ×1).
  - *Characters:* Ibram Gaunt ×10 (POV in all 10), Elim Rawne ×9 (supporting × 8, POV × 1 — *The Anarch*), Oan Mkoll ×9, Hlaine Larkin ×9, Viktor Hark ×7, Ban Daur ×6, Tona Criid ×4, Mabbon Etogaur ×4 (Blood Pact + Salvation's Reach + Warmaster + Anarch), Felyx Chass ×3 (Salvation's Reach + Warmaster + Anarch), Ana Curth ×4, Caffran ×3, Dalin Criid ×2 (Armour of Contempt POV + Only in Death supporting), Anakwanar Sek ×2 (Warmaster + Anarch — Archenemy-level antagonist), Macaroth ×2, Gerome Landerson ×2 (Traitor General + Armour of Contempt), Brin Milo ×2 (Vincula Insurgency + Founding Omnibus), Tolin Dorden ×2, Bragg ×2, Colm Corbec ×2 (Vincula Insurgency + Founding Omnibus — Corbec is killed in W40K-0030 *Sabbat Martyr*, so he only appears in books set chronologically before that death). - **Notes:**
  - Inquisition-consistency constraint (Brief 061): triggered only on W40K-0035 *Blood Pact* (Sirkle rogue-Inquisitorial agents as a supporting Inquisition presence). No Inquisitor POVs in this batch. Constraint quietly held.

"Eldar" over "Aeldari" (only relevant in the Founding-Omnibus aggregation from *Ghostmaker* 2000). "Sons of Sek" introduced as a faction at *Salvation's Reach* (2011), distinct from "Blood Pact" — kept separate per Brief 061 surface-form discipline.

  - W40K-0039 *The Vincula Insurgency* entry_point: tagged `mid_series` because the publication ordering makes it a deep-in-series read. The work is *chronologically* a prequel (pre-First-and-Only), but the **Ghost Dossier** supplementary-series framing assumes Crusade-veteran reader familiarity — this is the same tension as W40K-0015 *Death or Glory* in ssot-w40k-002.

Abnett bookends with *Of Their Lives in the Ruins of Their Cities* (Tanith First, post-Necropolis) and *The Iron Star* (Inquisition piece). Mitchell's *A Good Man* is a Cain-tonally-lighter Imperial Guard study. McNeill's *Apostle's Creed* foregrounds an Adepta Sororitas confessor — first Sororitas surface form in the authority layer. SSOT format=anthology, correct → no data_conflict raised. POV is ensemble across multi-author short fiction; gender tag = ensemble.
  - **W40K-0044 *Sabbat Crusade* (anthology, ed. Abnett, 2014):** Second Sabbat anthology. Abnett contributes four Ghosts shorts (*Family* / *You Never Know* / *Ghosts and Bad Shadows* / *A Ghost Return*); French's *Son of Sek* + Dembski-Bowden's *Arnogaur* foreground the rising Sek faction and the Blood Pact officer corps; Annandale's *The Deeper Wounds*, Kyme's *Tempest*, Vincent's *Viduity* run smaller-scale Crusade threads. Sirkle-style internal-Imperium conspiracy + Sek/Innokenti split as recurring framing — political_thriller added to facetIds.

Smallest of the four Gaunt's Ghosts omnibuses in this batch (2 books vs. 3 or 4), but still length_tier=doorstopper because the combined page-count crosses ~600 pages and the omnibus framing carries Mabbon Etogaur's recruitment-to-deep-strike arc and the Felyx Chass paternity reveal across both constituents.
  - **W40K-0046 *Sabbat War* (anthology, ed. Abnett, 2021):** Third Sabbat anthology, ten stories. Post-Anarch finale framing — Sek is dead, the Crusade reorients. Abnett bookends with *This is What Victory Feels Like (Forever the Same)* and *From There to Here*. Rachel Harrison's *Indomitable Spirit* is a Severina-Raine-style Commissar piece; Justin D. Hill's *The Tomb of Vichres* + Robert Rath's *Glory Flight* (Phantine Air Corps) + John French's *Armaduke* (named for Gaunt's strike-cruiser flagship) thread the wider Crusade. doubt tag added to facetIds (post-victory-meaning umbrella frame). No new factions vs. 0044.
  - **W40K-0047 *Nightbringer* (McNeill, 2002):** Ultramarines #1 — Uriel Ventris series debut. Pavonis mercantile-world setting; seven Cardinal Houses political-intrigue layer; awakening C'tan-Nightbringer beneath Eldar-exile prison structure; Inquisitor Ario Barzano partnership; tactical Eldar farseer alliance. Captain Idaeus death framing (pre-novel). POV=Uriel Ventris, scope=company (4th Company deployment). entry_point=series_start. **First Necron antagonist faction** and **first C'tan named antagonist** in the authority layer.
  - **W40K-0048 *Warriors of the Ultramar* (McNeill, 2003):** Ultramarines #2 — Tarsis Ultra Tyranid-hive-fleet defence. Mortifactors Chapter crossover under Chaplain Astador (death-cult-oriented Astartes brotherhood). Adeptus Mechanicus contingent + Inquisitor Barzano return. The Vespasian-class biological-weapon Codex-violation precipitates Ventris's death-oath. **First Mortifactors surface form** and **first Tyranid major-antagonist** since the Cain books in 002. scope=planetary.
  - **W40K-0049 *Dead Sky, Black Sun* (McNeill, 2004):** Ultramarines #3 — death-oath aftermath. Ventris + Pasanius to Medrengard (Iron Warriors daemon-forge-world in the Eye of Terror); Daemonculaba-sample mission; Warsmith Honsou as long-arc personal antagonist; Ardaric Vaanes + Lords of the Unholy Host as supporting fallen-Astartes band. cosmic_horror added to facetIds (corrupted-flesh / daemon-machinery register). scope=squad (two-Astartes-on-foot mission). **First Iron Warriors major antagonist** and **first Honsou appearance** in the authority layer.
  - **W40K-0050 *The Ultramarines Omnibus* (McNeill, 2006):** Omnibus aggregation of W40K-0047 + W40K-0048 + W40K-0049 from within this batch — first intra-batch omnibus aggregation in the loop (previous omnibuses aggregated from preceding batches). Union/highest-role-wins. entry_point=series_start (canonical entry-point omnibus for the Ventris saga). length_tier=doorstopper.
- **value_outside_vocabulary** (candidates surfaced by this batch, none promoted):
  - `anthology` / `collection` — `format` facet only carries media values (book, audiobook, animation, etc.); the SSOT-roster's `anthology` and `omnibus` structural-format values live outside the facet vocabulary. Three anthology entries (0043, 0044, 0046) tag `book` for medium and rely on SSOT-roster `format=anthology` for the structural call.
  - `multi_author` — a `creator_role` ensemble dimension for multi-author works would help anthologies cleanly. Currently no facet captures "the contributor list is N>1 distinct authors".
  - `space_marine_company` — `scope=company` exists, but `space_marine_company` as a distinct scope (vs. Imperial Guard company) would be useful for differentiating Astartes-detachment-scale stories from Guard-detachment-scale stories of nominally the same headcount.
  - `prison_world` / `daemon_world` / `forge_world` — Medrengard (W40K-0049) and Iron Warriors infrastructure don't have specific tags beyond `location`-level surface forms.
  - `codex_violation` / `death_oath` — Ventris-arc-specific concepts. `doubt` + `hubris` approximate the moral-stakes weight, but the Codex-versus-pragmatism axis is a recurring Ultramarines-saga theme that the current `theme` taxonomy doesn't cleanly capture.

  - **W40K-0059 *Death Knell* (Kelly, 2018):** Novella tied to the Space Marine Heroes miniature line. Ultramarines tactical squad under Sergeant Sevastus vs the **Crimson Slaughter** Heretic Astartes renegade chapter on the Isle of St Capilene; daemonic bell driving the mortal population to madness while silencing the renegades' internal voices. Captain Thassarius leads the initial mass-assault that fails; Sevastus's stealth squad finishes the job. **First Crimson Slaughter surface form** + **first explicit Heretic Astartes faction** in the authority layer (previously only Iron Warriors as Chaos Astartes via the McNeill arc). `cosmic_horror` tag for the haunted-cathedral register.
  - **W40K-0060 *Storm of Iron* (McNeill, 2002):** Iron Warriors siege of the Imperial fortress-world of Hydra Cordatus. Warsmith Barban Falk leads (correction from initial Shon'tu draft per WebSearch); Forrix, Kroeger, and the rising half-breed Honsou are the Grand-Company captains; Warsmith Berossus arrives with reinforcements for the final push. Imperial defenders: Imperial Guard regiment + thin Imperial Fists detachment + Magos Naicin guarding the primarch-DNA vault. **Dual POV across both sides** (pov_side=dual; protagonist_gender=ensemble) — first authority-layer entry to carry both. **Foundational Honsou origin novel** — written four years before he appears as Ventris's antagonist in W40K-0049 *Dead Sky, Black Sun*. Iron-Warriors-anchored standalone, accessible without prior series knowledge.
- **value_outside_vocabulary** (candidates surfaced by this batch, none promoted):
  - `primaris` — no facet captures the post-Indomitus Primaris/Firstborn distinction. *The Swords of Calth* is the first authority-layer book to require this differentiation. Resolver/vocab brief later: a Marine-generation facet would be useful.
  - `repackaging` / `re-issue` — the roster carries multiple structurally-identical omnibus rows under different SKUs (W40K-0050 ≡ W40K-0056, W40K-0055 ≡ W40K-0057). No facet captures this. Workaround: `data_conflict { kind: "duplicate_omnibus" }` flag on the later-published rows. Long-term, a `logical_work_id` or `superseded_by` would be cleaner.
  - `body_horror` — *The Killing Ground* Unfleshed register goes beyond `cosmic_horror` + `cw_disturbing`. Same gap as W40K-0034 *Only in Death* (haunted-house horror) noted in the ssot-w40k-004 status entry.
  - `crusade_era` — Primaris/Indomitus framing has no temporal-era facet. Workaround: surface form `Indomitus Crusade` in factions/locations, none in facetIds.
  - `daemonic_artefact` / `cursed_object` — *Death Knell*'s daemonic bell, common pattern across the catalog; not captured by current facet taxonomy.
- **Notable surface-form frequencies within this batch:**
  - *Factions (canonical-resolver match):* Adeptus Astartes ×10 (every entry), Ultramarines ×9 (every entry except Storm of Iron, which is Iron-Warriors-anchored but still mentions Imperial Fists), Iron Warriors ×5 (Killing Ground background + Chapter's Due antagonist + 2 omnibuses + Storm of Iron primary — the second-most-frequent faction in this batch), Chaos ×5 (Chapter's Due + Death Knell + 2 omnibuses + Storm of Iron background), Necrons ×2 (Swords of Calth + Vol. 1 Omnibus aggregating Nightbringer), Tau Empire ×3 (Courage and Honour + 2 omnibuses — *first Tau Empire major antagonist* in the authority layer), Imperial Guard ×4 (Courage and Honour + 2 omnibuses + Storm of Iron), Imperial Fists ×1 (Storm of Iron — *first Imperial Fists* in the authority layer despite being a First Founding loyalist chapter).
  - *Factions (new surface forms in this batch):* **Crimson Slaughter** ×1 (Death Knell — first appearance), **Heretic Astartes** ×1 (Death Knell — first explicit faction surface form; previously only specific Chaos-Astartes legions like Iron Warriors), **Bloodborn** ×3 (Chapter's Due + 2 omnibuses — first appearance), **Unfleshed** ×3 (Killing Ground + 2 omnibuses — first appearance), **Salinas Liberation Front** ×3 (same), **C'tan** ×1 (Vol. 1 Omnibus aggregating Nightbringer — first explicit C'tan-as-faction surface form, distinct from Nightbringer-the-character), **Mortifactors** ×1 (Vol. 1 Omnibus aggregating Warriors of Ultramar), **Lords of the Unholy Host** ×1 (Vol. 1 Omnibus aggregating Dead Sky, Black Sun).
  - *Locations:* Ultramar ×4 (Chapter's Due + 2 omnibuses + Swords of Calth mentioned), Calth ×3 (Chapter's Due + 2 omnibuses), Macragge ×5 (Killing Ground mentioned + Courage and Honour mentioned + Chapter's Due secondary + 2 omnibuses secondary), Pavonis ×4 (Courage and Honour + 2 omnibuses + Vol. 1 Omnibus aggregating Nightbringer), Salinas ×3 + Killing Ground ×3 (Killing Ground + 2 omnibuses), Eye of Terror ×4 (Killing Ground mentioned + 2 omnibuses + Vol. 1 Omnibus aggregating Dead Sky), Medrengard ×2 (Vol. 1 Omnibus aggregating Dead Sky + repackaging), Tarsis Ultra ×1 (Vol. 1 Omnibus aggregating Warriors of Ultramar), Sycorax ×1 (Swords of Calth — first appearance), Black Reach ×1 (Assault on Black Reach — first appearance), Isle of St Capilene ×1 (Death Knell — first appearance), Hydra Cordatus ×1 (Storm of Iron — first appearance, foundational Iron-Warriors-siege locale).
  - *Characters:* Uriel Ventris ×7 (POV in 4 novels + 3 omnibuses), Pasanius Lysane ×7 (supporting in all 7 Ventris entries), Honsou ×6 (mentioned/supporting in Killing Ground + Chapter's Due + 2 omnibuses + Storm of Iron POV + Vol. 1 Omnibus aggregating Dead Sky), Marneus Calgar ×3, Cato Sicarius ×4 (Chapter's Due + 2 omnibuses + Assault on Black Reach), Tigurius ×3, Cassius ×3, Ardaric Vaanes ×3, Leto Barbaden ×3, Daron Nisato ×3, Sylvanus Thayer ×3, Shas'O Or'es'ka'an ×3, Aun'rai ×3, Lord Winterbourne ×3, Mykola Shonai ×4 (Courage and Honour + 2 omnibuses + Vol. 1 Omnibus aggregating Nightbringer), Ario Barzano ×1 (Vol. 1 Omnibus aggregating Nightbringer/Warriors of Ultramar), Chaplain Astador ×1 (Vol. 1 Omnibus aggregating Warriors of Ultramar), Roboute Guilliman ×1 (Swords of Calth mentioned — first appearance), Scipio Vorolanus ×1 (Assault on Black Reach POV — first appearance), Iulus Fennion ×1, Praxor ×1, Telion ×1, Zanzag ×1 (Assault on Black Reach Ork warlord), Sevastus ×1 (Death Knell POV), Thassarius ×1, Aethor ×1, Titus ×1, Forrix ×1 (Storm of Iron POV), Kroeger ×1, Barban Falk ×1 (Storm of Iron Warsmith), Berossus ×1, Magos Naicin ×1, Captain Idaeus ×1 (Vol. 1 Omnibus aggregating Nightbringer — mentioned).
- **Notes:**
  - **Skip-50-stop active.** Maintainer's opening prompt for this iteration ("Lass uns sessions/2026-05-11-061-arch-ssot-loop.md machen — lets go!" plus the implicit "5 runs sind schon durch") matched the brief's permissive interpretation of the skip-marker: resolver was already done (063–069 closed OQ4 + OQ5 for the first 50 books per the 069 implementer report), so the 50er-pause was operationally released before this session opened. Status-block tag set to ✋ rather than ✅ to make the skip-condition visible in the loop log.
  - **Repackaging-pair pattern.** First time the loop encounters structurally-identical omnibuses under different roster rows: W40K-0050 ≡ W40K-0056 (Ventris Vol. 1 ≡ Original Ultramarines Omnibus, books 1-3), W40K-0055 ≡ W40K-0057 (Ventris Vol. 2 ≡ Second Omnibus, books 4-6). Both pairs flagged with `data_conflict { kind: "duplicate_omnibus" }`. Pattern will likely recur for HH-domain Garro / Vulkan / Dark Imperium re-issues — Resolver brief at the next 50er-pause should decide whether to add a `logical_work_id` or `superseded_by` facet, or keep the duplicate-omnibus flag as the canonical workaround.
  - **First Imperial Fists appearance.** Despite being a First Founding loyalist chapter, Imperial Fists do not appear in the authority layer until W40K-0060 *Storm of Iron* (defender detachment). The Cain books and Gaunt's Ghosts arc are Imperial Guard / Commissariat-anchored, the Ventris arc is Ultramarines-anchored. Worth noting for the Resolver brief: the canonical chapter is now in scope.
  - **First dual-POV Imperium-vs-Chaos entry.** W40K-0060 *Storm of Iron* is the first authority-layer book with `pov_side=dual` (Iron Warriors POV alongside Imperial defender POV) and `protagonist_gender=ensemble`. The Cain books were satirical-Imperium-only, Gaunt's Ghosts were Imperial-Guard-only with brief Mabbon-Etogaur POVs in the Victory arc.
  - **First Primaris framing.** W40K-0054 *The Swords of Calth* (2021) is the first authority-layer book that explicitly frames Uriel as Primaris-ascended. The pre-Primaris generation is now distinguishable from the post-Indomitus generation in the catalog. Resolver/vocab brief should consider a Marine-generation facet (Firstborn vs Primaris).
  - **Inquisition-consistency constraint** (Brief 061): not triggered. No Inquisitor POVs in any of the 10 entries. The closest inquisition-presence is Ario Barzano via the Vol. 1 Omnibus aggregating Nightbringer/Warriors of Ultramar — kept as supporting where canonically present.
  - **Surface-form treue compliance.** "Imperial Guard" over "Astra Militarum" across this batch (publication range 2002–2021 spans the 2014 rename, but McNeill's Ventris arc kept the original term through 2010, and the Storm of Iron 2002 entry is firmly pre-rename). "Eldar" over "Aeldari" where it appears (only Vol. 1 Omnibus aggregating Nightbringer, 2002). "Tau Empire" over "T'au" (2009 *Courage and Honour* is firmly pre-9th-edition spelling). "Necrons" both old and new (no rename). "Adeptus Astartes" + "Ultramarines" + "Iron Warriors" + "Imperial Fists" + "Crimson Slaughter" all canonical surface forms.
  - **W40K-0060 *Storm of Iron* protagonist-class anomaly.** The book is space-marine-anchored on both sides (Iron Warriors POV + Imperial Fists defender), so `protagonist_class=space_marine` covers both. The dual nature is captured by `pov_side=dual` + `protagonist_gender=ensemble`, not by a multi-class tag. Acceptable workaround.
  - Lint/typecheck/brain-lint nicht gelaufen — data-only commit (eine JSON + ein Markdown-Append), keine Code-/Brain-Page-Änderungen, alle drei Lint-Targets nicht betroffen. Per Brief-061-Klausel akzeptabel.

## 2026-05-13 · ssot-w40k-007 · W40K-0061..W40K-0070 · ✅

- **Cumulative books in authority:** 70 / 100 to next resolver pause (60 before this batch + 10 written here). No 50er-stop hit; next pause at 100 (= ssot-w40k-010).
- **CC model:** claude-opus-4-7
- **Pre-check:** Detected existing `manual-overrides-ssot-w40k-001..006.json` (6 × 10 = 60 books). W40K max = 6, HH max = 0, cumulative-before = 60, 60 % 50 ≠ 0 → no resolver pause. Next batch: `ssot-w40k-007`, slice = W40K-0061..W40K-0070 (3 Iron Warriors / Honsou entries — the 2012 Omnibus, the 2019 Complete Honsou Omnibus, the 2010 limited-edition novella — plus 7 early-2000s 40K standalones, four of which now sit under Black Library's *Heretic Tomes* label).
- **WebSearch:** mean ≈ 0.8 / book, max = 1 (over 10 books). 8 total searches:
  - 1 search each: W40K-0061 *Iron Warriors: The Omnibus* (confirm constituent stories — Storm of Iron + Iron Warrior novella + six shorts: The Enemy of My Enemy, The Heraclitus Effect, The Skull Harvest, The Iron Without, The Beast of Calth, The Corpse Road), W40K-0062 *The Complete Honsou Omnibus* (confirm content-identical to W40K-0061), W40K-0063 *Iron Warrior* novella (Honsou's star-fort strike + A5 limited edition 1,000-copy hand-numbered detail), W40K-0064 *Space Marine* (confirm Imperial Fists chapter + three Necromunda-underhive POVs + Tyranid-bioship climax + Heretic Tomes label), W40K-0065 *Eye of Terror* (Bayley plot — Maynard Rugolo rogue trader + corrupted Great-Crusade-survivor Marine subplot + Bayley New-Wave-SF register + Heretic Tomes label), W40K-0066 *Pawns of Chaos* (Brian Craig = Brian Stableford pseudonym, Sigmatus medieval-tech setting, cultist-POV summoning narrative, Heretic Tomes), W40K-0067 *Farseer* (William King — Janus Darke rogue trader + Eldar Farseer Auric + Slaanesh Daemon-Prince soul-hunt + Heretic Tomes), W40K-0068 *Daemon World* (Torvendis cast — Lady Charybdia / Golgoth / Kron / Word Bearers Captain Amakyre / traitor Karnulon).
  - 0 searches: W40K-0069 *Angels of Darkness* (Astelan interrogation by Boreas + parallel Piscina IV Ork war + Master Belial — foundational Dark-Angels-Fallen text, training-data-dense), W40K-0070 *Fire Warrior* (had enough on Spurrier / Kais / Dolumar IV / Ko'vash / Tarkh'ax / Webway-prison after the omnibus + Heretic-Tomes-cluster searches; the WebSearch result for W40K-0070 came back as part of an earlier batched call).
- **Per-book bullets:**
  - **W40K-0061 *Iron Warriors: The Omnibus* (McNeill, 2012):** First Black-Library omnibus of the Iron Warriors thread — collects *Storm of Iron* (W40K-0060, prior batch) + the limited-edition novella *Iron Warrior* (W40K-0063, this batch) + six Honsou-arc shorts (*The Enemy of My Enemy*, *The Heraclitus Effect*, *The Skull Harvest*, *The Iron Without*, *The Beast of Calth*, *The Corpse Road*). Strictly chaos-POV, Honsou-anchored. **`data_conflict { kind: duplicate_omnibus }`** flag set against W40K-0062 (identical contents under a different SKU). `entry_point=standalone` because Storm of Iron itself stands alone and the omnibus is the canonical entry into the Iron-Warriors-side reading order.
  - **W40K-0062 *Iron Warriors: The Complete Honsou Omnibus* (McNeill, 2019):** 2019 repackaging of W40K-0061 under the "Complete Honsou" title. **Identical eight constituents — second repackaging-pair in the authority layer** (after W40K-0050 ≡ W40K-0056 and W40K-0055 ≡ W40K-0057 from ssot-w40k-006). `data_conflict { kind: duplicate_omnibus }` flag set against W40K-0061. Pattern recurring: roster carries logically-identical omnibus rows under different ISBNs / cover art / publication decades; resolver should merge for recommendation but keep separate for catalogue completeness.
  - **W40K-0063 *Iron Warrior* (McNeill, 2010 novella):** Honsou's near-impossible strike at a heavily-defended Ultramarines star fort that conceals "a secret at its very core"; Black Library's first A5 limited-edition novella (1,000 hand-numbered, author-signed copies). Strictly chaos-POV. `entry_point=requires_context` because the vendetta-against-Ventris frame requires the Ventris saga (or Storm of Iron + Dead Sky context). Surface-forms cautious — I did not invent secondary characters (e.g. internal-cell figures) that the search summary didn't surface; Honsou + Ventris + Ardaric Vaanes only. **First authority-layer novella that is purely chaos-POV** (Death Knell from ssot-w40k-006 was Ultramarines vs Crimson Slaughter, imperium-POV).
  - **W40K-0064 *Space Marine* (Watson, 1993):** The third 40K novel ever published, structurally a Bildungsroman in three POVs (Lexandro d'Arquebus / Yeremi Valance / Biff Tundrish) following Necromunda underhive recruits through Imperial Fists gene-seed implantation, scout-stage, ascension to battle-brother, and a First Company Tyranid-bioship boarding action. **First authority-layer entry now under Black Library's *Heretic Tomes* label** for canonicity drift — flag set with `kind=data_conflict, field=canonicity, suggestion=heretic_tomes_label`. The Squat sub-faction (now removed from the setting) features in the lore and is preserved as a faction surface form for fidelity, even though it has no current canonical home.
  - **W40K-0065 *Eye of Terror* (Bayley, 1999):** British-New-Wave-SF-register chaos novel — Rogue Trader Maynard Rugolo on the eve of a Black Crusade plus a parallel Astartes-corruption subplot. `pov_side=dual` (Imperium rogue-trader + chaos / corrupted-Marine views), `protagonist_class=multi`. Heretic Tomes flag set. **Second `low_confidence` flag** set on characters: beyond Rugolo, the two Marine-subplot protagonists and the named-mad Navigator are described in summary but their personal names are not consistently surfaced across review sources — deliberately left unenumerated rather than invented (Brief 061 plot-halluzinations-disziplin). First authority-layer entry where `multi` is used as protagonist_class anchor; first "philosophical" tone-tag in the authority layer (the catalogue carries it; this is the first use).
  - **W40K-0066 *Pawns of Chaos* (Brian Craig / Brian Stableford pseudonym, 2001):** Medieval-tech world Sigmatus, indigenous cultist-POV daemon-summoning against the Imperial occupier. `protagonist_class=civilian` (rebel cultists), `pov_side=chaos`. Heretic Tomes flag set. **Pseudonym note** logged in the canonicity-flag reasoning: "Brian Craig" is the Black-Library pseudonym for the British SF author Brian Stableford — useful when the resolver auto-creates the persons-table row. **First authority-layer entry with `protagonist_class=civilian` as primary anchor** (Eisenhorn's was inquisitor-anchored; the cultist civilian role is structurally new here). Characters left empty: cultist-side ensemble cast across the rebel cell without consistent secondary-source character naming — `low_confidence` flag set on characters.
  - **W40K-0067 *Farseer* (King, 2002):** Rogue Trader Janus Darke + Eldar Farseer Auric alliance into the Eye of Terror, hunting a Slaanesh Daemon-Prince that's hunting Darke's soul. `protagonist_class=multi`, `pov_side=imperium` (Janus is the human POV anchor; Auric is supporting). Heretic Tomes flag set. **First authority-layer Eldar-Farseer-POV-supporting entry** — Auric is supporting-tier (not pov) but on-page Eldar-perspective material is rare in the early 2000s catalogue and worth flagging for the resolver. (Note: an actual Eldar-POV-primary entry would arrive later in the W40K thread.)
  - **W40K-0068 *Daemon World* (Counter, 2003):** Torvendis as the canvas — Slaaneshi ruler Lady Charybdia, Word Bearers Captain Amakyre hunting the traitor Karnulon, tribal warlord Golgoth pushing for his own holding, the fugitive sorcerer Kron threading every faction. **First explicit *Word Bearers* surface form** in the authority layer (previously only generic Heretic Astartes via Death Knell or Iron-Warriors-specific via the McNeill arc). **First explicit *Violators* warband** (Charybdia's Heretic-Astartes enforcers). All four Chaos powers (Slaanesh / Khorne / Tzeentch / Nurgle) on stage. **`cw_sex` content-warning added** for the Slaaneshi register — first authority-layer book to carry that tag (the Eisenhorn / Ravenor / Cain / Gaunt's Ghosts / Ventris arcs were all violence-anchored without sexual content of note). Ensemble POV (4 of the 5 named characters tagged pov).
  - **W40K-0069 *Angels of Darkness* (Thorpe, 2003):** **Foundational Dark-Angels / Fallen-Angels text.** Alternating-chapter structure: Astelan-the-Fallen interrogation by Interrogator-Chaplain Boreas + parallel Piscina IV Ork war under Master Belial. Astelan's claim — that the Lion himself was the traitor and the Fallen the loyalists — is the moral wrench the novel hands the chapter (and the reader). **First explicit *Dark Angels* faction surface form** in the authority layer. **First explicit *Fallen Angels* faction** — separate from Dark Angels, since the chapter's whole identity is structured around hunting them. `political_thriller` tag justified by Astelan's argument being political-in-the-Astartes-sense (a successor-chapter heresy claim).
  - **W40K-0070 *Fire Warrior* (Spurrier, 2003):** **First Tau-POV-anchored entry** in the authority layer (previously Tau Empire appeared only as antagonist via *Courage and Honour* / *The Greater Good*). Shas'la T'au Kais on Dolumar IV, rescuing the Ethereal Aun'el Ko'vash from an Imperial-held desert world while a Chaos cult tries to use Ko'vash as a soul-substance battery to free the Greater Daemon Tarkh'ax from a Webway warp-prison. `protagonist_class=pc_xenos` (the catalog's `pc_` prefix disambiguating it from pov_side.xenos — same workaround as the catalog's design intent). `pov_side=xenos`. **First authority-layer entry with `protagonist_gender=male` + `protagonist_class=pc_xenos` + `pov_side=xenos`** — the Tau-side anchor is structurally new. Tie-in novelisation of THQ's 2003 *Fire Warrior* PlayStation 2 game (Marc Gascoigne plotted, Spurrier wrote).
- **value_outside_vocabulary** (candidates surfaced by this batch, none promoted):
  - `heretic_tomes` / `canonicity_drift` — four entries in this batch (W40K-0064, W40K-0065, W40K-0066, W40K-0067) sit under Black Library's *Heretic Tomes* label for cumulative canonicity drift. No facet captures this; workaround is `data_conflict { kind: canonicity, suggestion: heretic_tomes_label }`. Long-term, a canonicity / canonicity-status facet would make the recommender's job cleaner — it would let Ask-the-Archive down-rank or contextualise Heretic-Tomes entries when the user's question implies "current-canon recommendation".
  - `bildungsroman` / `coming_of_age` — Watson's *Space Marine* is structurally a Bildungsroman across three POVs. No plot_type captures this; workaround used: `war_story + journey + character_study`.
  - `recruitment_arc` — same gap for *Space Marine*: there's no facet specifically for the "boy → Astartes" arc structure that Watson originated and that later catalog entries (e.g. various Space Marines Battles tie-ins, James Swallow's Blood Angels Deus Encarmine arc) descend from.
  - `pseudonym` — the *Pawns of Chaos* author Brian Craig is the Black-Library pseudonym for the British SF author Brian Stableford. No facet captures author-pseudonym attribution; the persons-table will need a `pseudonym_of` column or similar when the resolver auto-creates Brian Craig as an author row. Logged in the W40K-0066 canonicity-flag reasoning for resolver pickup.
  - `webway` — first time the Webway appears as a location in the authority layer (W40K-0070, where the Tarkh'ax prison is buried within a fragment of it). No faction-or-location-meta-tag captures the Webway's structural role (Eldar / Drukhari infrastructure used as a chaos-warp-prison substrate); treated as a normal location surface form.
  - `four_chaos_powers` / `chaos_pantheon` — *Daemon World* is the first authority-layer entry where all four Chaos gods (Slaanesh / Khorne / Tzeentch / Nurgle) are on stage in named tension; *The Killing Ground* and *The Chapter's Due* leaned heavily on Khorne via the Bloodborn, and Eisenhorn / Cain leaned heavily on Slaanesh + Chaos Undivided. A `chaos_pantheon=multi` or similar facet would be useful for the resolver.
- **Notable surface-form frequencies within this batch:**
  - *Factions (canonical-resolver match):* Chaos ×8 (every entry except Space Marine and the Tau-anchored Fire Warrior — though Fire Warrior carries Chaos as primary antagonist), Adeptus Astartes ×8 (every Iron Warriors entry, Space Marine, Eye of Terror, Angels of Darkness, Fire Warrior as antagonist), Iron Warriors ×3 (Omnibus + Complete Honsou Omnibus + Iron Warrior novella — the McNeill chaos-arc continues from ssot-w40k-006's Storm of Iron), Ultramarines ×3 (antagonist in Iron Warriors entries), Heretic Astartes ×4 (Iron Warriors entries + Eye of Terror + Daemon World — the Violators), Daemons ×5 (Iron Warriors entries background + Pawns of Chaos + Farseer + Daemon World + Fire Warrior), Imperial Guard ×5 (Iron Warriors entries + Pawns of Chaos + Angels of Darkness + Fire Warrior), Inquisition ×2 (Farseer + Fire Warrior — both as supporting/antagonist).
  - *Factions (new surface forms in this batch):* **Word Bearers** ×1 (Daemon World — first explicit appearance), **Violators** ×1 (Daemon World — Charybdia's Heretic Astartes warband), **Dark Angels** ×1 (Angels of Darkness — first explicit appearance, despite being a First Founding loyalist chapter), **Fallen Angels** ×1 (Angels of Darkness — distinct faction from Dark Angels by the novel's design), **Tau Empire** ×1 (Fire Warrior — first as primary-protagonist faction; previously antagonist in ssot-w40k-006 and ssot-w40k-002 batches), **Fire Caste** ×1 (Fire Warrior — first Tau-internal-caste surface form), **Ethereal Caste** ×1 (same), **Cult of Chaos** ×2 (Pawns of Chaos + Fire Warrior), **Squats** ×1 (Space Marine — first appearance of the now-removed sub-faction in the authority layer; preserved for surface-form fidelity), **Rogue Traders** ×2 (Eye of Terror + Farseer — first dedicated Rogue-Trader-faction surface forms), **Navis Nobilite** ×1 (Eye of Terror), **Adeptus Arbites** ×1 (Pawns of Chaos), **Slaanesh** ×2 (Farseer + Daemon World — first as standalone faction surface form; previously implicit in Daemonculaba / Crimson Slaughter framing), **Tzeentch** ×1 (Daemon World), **Nurgle** ×1 (same), **Khorne** ×2 (Eye of Terror + Daemon World — second appearance after Chapter's Due / Bloodborn in ssot-w40k-006), **Eldar** ×1 (Farseer — first Eldar surface form in the authority layer).
  - *Locations:* Medrengard ×3 (Iron Warriors entries — recurring from ssot-w40k-006), Hydra Cordatus ×2 (Iron Warriors omnibuses, via Storm of Iron), Ultramar ×3 (Iron Warriors entries), Eye of Terror ×3 (Iron Warriors entries mentioned + Eye of Terror primary + Farseer primary), Maelstrom ×1 (Daemon World — first appearance, distinct from Eye of Terror), Calth ×1 (Iron Warriors entries mentioned), Macragge ×1 (same). New first-appearance characters: Lexandro d'Arquebus / Yeremi Valance / Biff Tundrish (Space Marine), Maynard Rugolo (Eye of Terror), Janus Darke + Auric (Farseer), Lady Charybdia / Golgoth / Kron / Amakyre / Karnulon (Daemon World), Boreas + Astelan + Belial (Angels of Darkness — Astelan in particular is the load-bearing first-Fallen-Angel surface form for resolver purposes), Shas'la T'au Kais + Aun'el Ko'vash + Tarkh'ax (Fire Warrior — first Tau-named characters in the authority layer).
- **Notes:**
  - **Repackaging-pair pattern continues.** Second consecutive batch with a repackaging-pair flag set — W40K-0061 ≡ W40K-0062 (Iron Warriors omnibuses, 2012 + 2019). The post-ssot-w40k-006 prediction held: the loop is encountering structurally-identical omnibus rows under different SKUs, and the workaround pattern is now stable (`data_conflict { kind: duplicate_omnibus }` cross-referenced both ways). Resolver brief at the next 50er-pause (cumulative=100 = `ssot-w40k-010`) should formalise the duplicate-omnibus handling — `logical_work_id`, `superseded_by`, or a `repackaging_of` field would all clean this up.
  - **Heretic Tomes cluster.** Four of the ten books in this slice — W40K-0064 *Space Marine*, W40K-0065 *Eye of Terror*, W40K-0066 *Pawns of Chaos*, W40K-0067 *Farseer* — are currently sold by Black Library under the *Heretic Tomes* label for cumulative canonicity drift. This is the loop's first dense Heretic-Tomes cluster; the early 2000s 40K standalone catalogue is the era most affected by retcons (Squats, pre-9th-edition Eldar / T'au spellings and politics, pre-Cawl Marine recruitment lore, pre-Indomitus Eye-of-Terror geopolitics). Workaround: `data_conflict { kind: canonicity, suggestion: heretic_tomes_label }`. The recommender should consider a canonicity-status facet so Ask-the-Archive can down-rank or contextualise Heretic-Tomes entries when the user's question implies "current-canon recommendation".
  - **First Tau-POV-anchored entry.** W40K-0070 *Fire Warrior* is the authority layer's first entry where the POV character is Tau (`protagonist_class=pc_xenos`, `pov_side=xenos`). Previous authority-layer Tau presence was antagonist-only (Shas'O Or'es'ka'an + Aun'rai in *Courage and Honour* via ssot-w40k-006). The Tau-internal-caste surface forms (`Fire Caste`, `Ethereal Caste`) enter the resolver dictionary here.
  - **First Word Bearers + Dark Angels + Fallen Angels appearance.** W40K-0068 *Daemon World* introduces the Word Bearers as a primary faction (and the Violators as a Heretic-Astartes warband), W40K-0069 *Angels of Darkness* introduces both the Dark Angels and the Fallen Angels as distinct factions. Three of the major loyalist + traitor First Founding Astartes legions / chapters that weren't yet in the authority layer enter together — useful for the Resolver brief because all three have well-established canonical surface forms.
  - **`protagonist_class=civilian` + `protagonist_class=multi` first uses.** W40K-0066 *Pawns of Chaos* (cultist-POV) is the first civilian-anchored authority-layer entry. W40K-0065 *Eye of Terror* (rogue trader + Marine subplot dual frame) and W40K-0067 *Farseer* (rogue trader + Farseer alliance) are the first `multi`-class entries. These structural slots were always in the catalog but unused until this batch.
  - **`philosophical` tone tag first use.** Bayley's *Eye of Terror* and Stableford's *Pawns of Chaos* both inherit a philosophical-SF register from their authors' wider careers, distinct from the standard 40K register; tagged `philosophical` for the first time in the authority layer (the tag was always available; this is the first surface use).
  - **`cw_sex` content-warning first use.** W40K-0068 *Daemon World* — the Slaaneshi register pushes the prose into explicitly sexual content in places (Charybdia's court, the Violators' courtly excess). Tag added for first time in the authority layer; future Slaaneshi-heavy entries will likely pick it up too.
  - **`low_confidence` flags.** Two entries — W40K-0065 *Eye of Terror* (characters beyond Rugolo) and W40K-0066 *Pawns of Chaos* (cultist ensemble names) — carry `low_confidence` flags on the characters array because secondary-source coverage doesn't consistently surface those names, and Brief 061's plot-halluzinations-disziplin says "leer lassen oder low_confidence-Flag setzen" is the correct move when WebSearch coverage is thin. Better to under-name and over-flag than to invent.
  - **Inquisition-consistency constraint** (Brief 061): not strictly triggered. No Inquisitor POVs in any of the 10 entries. The closest inquisition-presence is W40K-0067 *Farseer* (Inquisition agents converging on Darke + Auric inside the Eye of Terror) and W40K-0070 *Fire Warrior* (Inquisition strike-team pursuing the Chaos cult on Dolumar IV); both kept as supporting/antagonist where canonically present, not promoted to primary.
  - **Surface-form treue compliance.** "Imperial Guard" over "Astra Militarum" across the batch (publication range 1993–2019; the 2014 rename does not retroactively change pre-rename surface forms, and the 2019 Complete Honsou Omnibus is a repackaging of pre-rename material). "Eldar" over "Aeldari" in *Farseer* (2002 publication, pre-9th-edition spelling). "Tau Empire" + "Shas'la T'au Kais" + "Aun'el Ko'vash" over "T'au" spellings (2003 *Fire Warrior* is firmly pre-9th-edition). "Word Bearers" + "Violators" + "Dark Angels" + "Fallen Angels" all canonical surface forms. "Squats" preserved as a surface form for W40K-0064 even though the sub-faction has been removed from current canon — fidelity to the 1993 text matters more than retroactive consistency.
  - Lint/typecheck/brain-lint nicht gelaufen — data-only commit (eine JSON + ein Markdown-Append), keine Code-/Brain-Page-Änderungen, alle drei Lint-Targets nicht betroffen. Per Brief-061-Klausel akzeptabel.

## 2026-05-13 · ssot-w40k-008 · W40K-0071..W40K-0080 · ✅

- **Cumulative books in authority:** 80 / 100 to next resolver pause (70 before this batch + 10 written here). No 50er-stop hit (80 % 50 ≠ 0); next pause at 100 = `ssot-w40k-010`.
- **CC model:** claude-opus-4-7
- **Pre-check:** Detected existing `manual-overrides-ssot-w40k-001..007.json` (7 × 10 = 70 books). W40K max = 7, HH max = 0, cumulative-before = 70, 70 % 50 ≠ 0 → no resolver pause. Next batch: `ssot-w40k-008`, slice = W40K-0071..W40K-0080 (mixed late-2000s/early-2010s 40K standalones — one Sabbat-Worlds-aviation novel, one Iron Hands quest, one Night Lords noir, one Iron Snakes fix-up, one Goto Eldar novel, one Imperial-Navy class-war thriller, one Adeptus-Titanicus ensemble piece, one Imperial-Fists recruitment novel, one Inquisitor-Czevak Webway novel, one Grey-Knights first-person novel).
- **WebSearch:** mean ≈ 1.0 / book, max = 1 (over 10 books). 10 total searches:
  - 1 search each: W40K-0071 *Double Eagle* (confirm Bree Jagdea + Khrel Kas Obarkon as the Imperium and Chaos POV anchors + Phantine-XX framing on Enothis), W40K-0072 *Iron Hands* (confirm Iron-Father Gdolkin + Medusa + 13th-Black-Crusade frame + Ferrus-Manus relic quest), W40K-0073 *Lord of the Night* (confirm Zso Sahaal + Mita Ashyn + Equixus + Acerbus + Corona Nox), W40K-0074 *Brothers of the Snake* (confirm Iron Snakes / Damocles Squad / Priad / Ithaka / Karybdis / seven-story fix-up structure), W40K-0075 *Eldar Prophecy* (confirm craftworld Kaelor + Naois + decadent-civilisation register), W40K-0076 *Relentless* (confirm Captain Becket + First Officer Ward + Eastern-Fringe-cruiser frame + Dark Eldar twist), W40K-0077 *Titanicus* (confirm Orestes + Legio Invicta + Princeps Gearhart + Guido Prinzhorn + Cally Samstag + Tolemy + Mechanicus / Imperium schism), W40K-0078 *Sons of Dorn* (confirm Imperial Fists scout recruits Zatori / du Queste / Taloc + Vernailis + Roaring Blades), W40K-0079 *Atlas Infernal* (confirm Bronislaw Czevak + Atlas Infernal map + Webway + Black Library + Ahzek Ahriman + Harlequins), W40K-0080 *The Emperor's Gift* (confirm Hyperion / Squad Castian first-person POV + Annika Jarlsdottir + First War of Armageddon + Months of Shame vs Space Wolves).
- **Per-book bullets:**
  - **W40K-0071 *Double Eagle* (Abnett, 2002):** Sabbat-Worlds Crusade companion to Gaunt's Ghosts, focused on the Phantine-XX fighter wing on Enothis. Dual POV across the dogfighting line: Bree Jagdea (Phantine commander) on the Imperial side, Khrel Kas Obarkon (Chaos Hell-Talon ace) on the Chaos side. 'Battle of Britain in space' register — sustained aerial attrition, pilot-psychology, strategic stakes of the air corridor over the ground Crusade. First authority-layer entry where the Imperial Navy is the *primary* protagonist faction (previously supporting in Sabbat-anthologies via Phantine Air Corps mentions in ssot-w40k-003/004/005). **First Khrel Kas Obarkon surface form** (Chaos ace antagonist). Clean.
  - **W40K-0072 *Iron Hands* (Green, 2004):** Iron-Father Gdolkin quest novel under the 13th-Black-Crusade frame. Gdolkin's company is pulled off Medusa to honour an old Adeptus-Mechanicus oath; the chase converges on a lost world that may hide both an ancient weapon and the resting place of Ferrus Manus. **First authority-layer entry where Iron Hands is the primary protagonist faction** (previously absent from the catalogue) and **first explicit Ferrus Manus surface form**. Adeptus-Mechanicus-Astartes-machine-theology register; quest / mystery as the primary plot type.
  - **W40K-0073 *Lord of the Night* (Spurrier, 2005):** Night-Lords noir / Inquisitorial-investigation dual frame on the sunless hive-world of Equixus. Zso Sahaal — First Captain of the VIII Legion, ten-thousand-years-exiled since Konrad Curze's death — hunts the Corona Nox to reclaim his legion from his treacherous rival Acerbus; Interrogator Mita Ashyn (with her own growing doubts about Inquisitorial hypocrisy) is on his trail. Dual POV, neither cleanly hero nor villain. **First authority-layer entry where the Night Lords legion is the primary protagonist faction** and **first explicit Zso Sahaal + Mita Ashyn + Acerbus surface forms**. cosmic_horror tag for the VIII-Legion's terror-doctrine register.
  - **W40K-0074 *Brothers of the Snake* (Abnett, 2007):** Episodic Iron-Snakes novel — seven linked Inferno!-magazine short stories under a Brother-Sergeant-Priad / Damocles-Squad spine over roughly twelve years on the Reef Stars front. Greek-coded chapter culture (home-world Ithaka, fortress moon Karybdis, oath/hospitality/kin-debt ethics). **`data_conflict` flag set** (`field: format, current: novel, suggestion: collection`) — same pattern as W40K-0025 *Ghostmaker* in ssot-w40k-003. **First authority-layer entry where the Iron Snakes chapter is the primary protagonist faction**; **first Reef-Stars sector / Ithaka / Karybdis surface forms**.
  - **W40K-0075 *Eldar Prophecy* (Goto, 2007):** Standalone Eldar-anchored novel on the isolated craftworld Kaelor, with the young warrior Naois at the centre of a prophecy that may be Slaaneshi manipulation rather than guidance. Quasi-feudal House politics + Aspect Temples withdrawn from public life + decadent-civilisation register. **`low_confidence` flag set on characters/locations** — secondary-source coverage is thin and inconsistent on House lords, Farseer cast, and craftworld-internal locales beyond Kaelor itself. Per Brief 061's plot-halluzinations-disziplin, surface forms kept tight to what summary sources consistently surface. **First xenos-POV-primary entry since W40K-0070 *Fire Warrior* in ssot-w40k-007**, and the first Eldar-craftworld-internal-POV entry in the authority layer.
  - **W40K-0076 *Relentless* (Williams, 2008):** Imperial-Navy class-war / political-thriller aboard the cruiser *Relentless* on patrol in the Eastern Fringe. First Officer Ward has the ship running on illicit trade-tithes; new captain Becket tightens the reins, an assassination drops Becket into his own Conscript decks, and Becket has to work his way back up the ship to confront Ward while a Dark-Eldar raider intercept turns the conspiracy into a survival fight. Ship-class scope (regiment-tier in the facet vocabulary). **First Imperial-Navy-cruiser-internal sociology piece** in the authority layer — *Double Eagle* in this same batch is the Navy aviation register, while *Relentless* is the lower-deck class-war register.
  - **W40K-0077 *Titanicus* (Abnett, 2008):** Adeptus-Titanicus ensemble doorstopper on the forge-world of Orestes when a Chaos titan legion makes planetfall. Multi-POV across Princeps Gearhart (Legio Invicta commander), Guido Prinzhorn (Legio Tempestus drafted in to crew the Dominatus Victrix after Eldar-engagement losses), Cally Samstag (Orestes PDF Activated 26th, unlikely junior leader), Moderati Zane Tarses (sole survivor of the original Dominatus Victrix crew), and Tolemy (archivist driving the Mechanicus / Imperium theological schism subplot). War-story + political-thriller in roughly equal weight; Mechanicus-vs-Imperium Omnissiah theology is the *internal* fault-line that the Chaos invasion exploits. **First authority-layer entry for the Adeptus Titanicus / Legio-level register** and **first explicit Legio Invicta + Legio Tempestus surface forms**.
  - **W40K-0078 *Sons of Dorn* (Roberson, 2010):** Imperial-Fists recruitment-and-training novel — three rival-nation Neophytes (Zatori, du Queste, Taloc) on a backwater civil-war-era planet are abducted into the chapter alongside ~2000 other candidates, survive the chapter's brutal recruitment regime, progress together through the Scout stage, and deploy to Vernailis against the Roaring Blades Traitor Guard. Coming-of-age / Bildungsroman across three POV recruits; opens what was projected as an Imperial-Fists Scout-trilogy. **First authority-layer entry where the Imperial Fists chapter is the primary protagonist faction** (previously only an off-page detachment in W40K-0060 *Storm of Iron*); **first Astartes-recruitment register** in the authority layer (closest prior parallel is W40K-0064 *Space Marine* Imperial-Fists-Bildungsroman in ssot-w40k-007).
  - **W40K-0079 *Atlas Infernal* (Sanders, 2011):** Standalone Inquisitor-Czevak novel compressing four crucial decades of High Inquisitor Bronislaw Czevak's life into a Webway-scale chase. Czevak has stolen the Atlas Infernal — a living map of the Webway — from the Eldar's Black Library and is now hunted simultaneously by Eldar Harlequins, Inquisition rivals, and his deadliest foe, Thousand Sons arch-sorcerer Ahzek Ahriman. Webway-scale journey + cat-and-mouse pursuit. **First authority-layer entry where the Ordo Xenos is the primary protagonist faction** (previously supporting/secondary only) and **first explicit Harlequins surface form** + **first Black-Library-the-place surface form** + **first explicit Eldrad Ulthran mention** + **first Ahzek-Ahriman-as-active-antagonist surface form** (vs. previous Thousand Sons appearances at the faction level only).
  - **W40K-0080 *The Emperor's Gift* (Dembski-Bowden, 2012):** First-person Grey-Knights novel narrated in retrospect by Hyperion of Squad Castian, covering the chapter's role around the First War of Armageddon and the subsequent intra-Imperium fallout — the Months of Shame — when the Grey Knights and the Inquisition's handling of Armageddon survivors put the chapter on a collision course with Logan Grimnar's Space Wolves. Inquisitor Annika Jarlsdottir (Fenrisian) holds the Inquisition end and the moral-tension hinge. Somber + reflective register; the Grey Knights are presented as incorruptible but not infallible, with the moral cost of daemon-banishment work and witness-handling as the load-bearing spine. **First authority-layer entry where Grey Knights is the primary protagonist faction**, **first authority-layer Space-Wolves surface form** (in antagonist register — Months-of-Shame frame), **first explicit Ordo Malleus surface form**, **first explicit Logan Grimnar surface form**, and **first First-War-of-Armageddon framing** in the authority layer.
- **value_outside_vocabulary** (candidates surfaced by this batch, none promoted):
  - `aerial_combat` / `fighter_pilot` — *Double Eagle*'s register isn't well captured by `war_story` + `action_heavy` alone; an aviation / fighter-ace sub-tag would distinguish dog-fighting attrition from Astartes-line ground combat. The Phantine Air Corps and Imperial-Navy-aviation surface forms come without a corresponding facet shape.
  - `recruitment_arc` / `bildungsroman` — same gap as W40K-0064 *Space Marine* in ssot-w40k-007; *Sons of Dorn* is structurally the same shape (three-POV-recruit progression from civilian → scout → Neophyte → first deployment). Workaround used: `war_story + character_study + journey`.
  - `class_warfare` / `lower_deck` — *Relentless* lives in a ship-internal-sociology register (Conscript decks vs officer deck) that no current facet captures. Workaround: `political_thriller + cw_abuse`.
  - `theological_schism` — *Titanicus*'s Mechanicus-vs-Imperium Omnissiah debate isn't captured by `political_thriller` alone; a religion / theology axis would add useful texture for Mechanicus-anchored entries.
  - `noir` / `detective` — *Lord of the Night*'s Mita-Ashyn-investigation thread is closer to noir-detective than to either `mystery` or `political_thriller` standalone. `mystery + character_study` is the workaround.
  - `meta_canon` / `non_current_canon` — *Eldar Prophecy*'s reception within Black Library readership is widely critical of the lore handling, which puts it in a structural neighbourhood with the ssot-w40k-007 Heretic-Tomes cluster (W40K-0064..0067) — but Black Library has not labelled the Goto Eldar trilogy under the *Heretic Tomes* imprint as far as my evidence goes, so I did NOT set a canonicity-flag in this batch. A `canonicity` facet (suggested earlier in ssot-w40k-007 notes) would let the recommender handle both the Heretic-Tomes-labelled and the merely-critically-questioned entries cleanly.
- **Notable surface-form frequencies within this batch:**
  - *Factions (canonical-resolver match):* Adeptus Astartes ×8 (every Astartes-anchored entry), Chaos ×8 (every entry except *Eldar Prophecy* and *Relentless* — Eldar-only and Navy-vs-Dark-Eldar respectively), Heretic Astartes ×4 (Double Eagle + Iron Hands + Lord of the Night + Titanicus), Imperial Guard ×7 (supporting / mentioned across most Imperium-side entries), Inquisition ×3 (Lord of the Night + Atlas Infernal + Emperor's Gift), Imperial Navy ×2 (Double Eagle + Relentless — the two Navy-anchored entries in the batch), Adeptus Mechanicus ×2 (Iron Hands + Titanicus), Dark Eldar ×2 (Brothers of the Snake + Relentless), Daemons ×1 (Emperor's Gift).

- **Notes:**
  - **Heavy first-appearance density.** This batch carries the highest "first-X" surface-form count of any batch so far: six Astartes chapters as primary protagonist faction (Iron Hands, Night Lords, Iron Snakes, Imperial Fists, Grey Knights — plus Space Wolves as first antagonist appearance), two new Eldar factions (Eldar as primary protagonist, Harlequins), three new Inquisition Ordos (Ordo Xenos as primary, Ordo Malleus, the rivals-within-Inquisition antagonist-as-faction shape in Atlas Infernal), two new Titan Legions (Invicta, Tempestus) + Adeptus Titanicus itself, and one new Chaos-Imperial-Guard Traitor-Guard surface form (Roaring Blades, distinct from Bloodborn / Blood Pact / Sons of Sek). Resolver brief at the next 50er-pause (cumulative=100 = `ssot-w40k-010`) will have a dense pile of new canonical chapter / legion / Ordo surface forms to fold into the reference data.
  - **Format-compliance flag.** W40K-0074 *Brothers of the Snake* `data_conflict { field: "format", suggestion: "collection" }` — seven linked Inferno!-magazine shorts under a Priad / Damocles-Squad-progression spine. Same pattern as W40K-0025 *Ghostmaker* (ssot-w40k-003) and the workaround used for it. Both books are structurally fix-ups with a continuity-of-cast frame; the format-compliance question (`fix_up` / `collection` as a new value, or `novel` as umbrella) is a Resolver / vocabulary call.
  - **`low_confidence` flag.** W40K-0075 *Eldar Prophecy* (characters/locations beyond Naois + Kaelor). Goto's Eldar trilogy is widely criticised within Black Library readership for lore-handling, and secondary-source summaries are inconsistent on the House-lord cast, Farseer figures, and craftworld-internal locales. Per Brief 061's plot-halluzinations-disziplin, kept tight to what summaries consistently surface; under-name + flag rather than invent.
  - **No canonicity flag set despite ssot-w40k-007 precedent.** I considered setting a `canonicity_drift / heretic_tomes_label` flag on *Eldar Prophecy* analogous to the four-entry Heretic-Tomes cluster in ssot-w40k-007 (W40K-0064..0067), but as far as my evidence goes, Black Library has not labelled the Goto Eldar trilogy under the *Heretic Tomes* imprint specifically — the criticism is reader-community-level, not Black-Library-imprint-level. Skipped the flag to avoid overstating; resolver / vocab brief can revisit if Black Library's canonicity scheme tightens to include reader-community-level non-canon entries.
  - **Inquisition-consistency constraint** (Brief 061): triggered cleanly for three of the ten entries — W40K-0073 *Lord of the Night* (Mita Ashyn as Inquisitorial Interrogator POV → Inquisition primary), W40K-0079 *Atlas Infernal* (Bronislaw Czevak as Ordo Xenos High Inquisitor POV → Inquisition + Ordo Xenos both primary), W40K-0080 *The Emperor's Gift* (Annika Jarlsdottir as Inquisitor + Hyperion's Grey-Knights / Inquisition partnership → Inquisition + Ordo Malleus both primary). Constraint held in all three: where an Inquisitor is on-page POV / supporting, the relevant Ordo is at least supporting-tier.
  - **Surface-form treue compliance.** "Imperial Guard" over "Astra Militarum" across the batch (publication range 2002–2012; the 2014 rename is post-publication for every entry). "Eldar" over "Aeldari" across the batch (publication range pre-9th-edition). "Dark Eldar" over "Drukhari" (Brothers of the Snake 2007 + Relentless 2008 pre-rename). "Night Lords" + "Iron Snakes" + "Iron Hands" + "Grey Knights" + "Space Wolves" + "Harlequins" all canonical surface forms.
  - **Synopsis-length elasticity.** W40K-0077 *Titanicus* (1201 chars) and W40K-0080 *The Emperor's Gift* (1300 chars) sit just over the 1200-char soft cap. Justified by ensemble register (Titanicus has 5 POVs to introduce + the Mechanicus / Imperium schism subplot) and by *Emperor's Gift*'s tri-faction moral frame (Grey Knights + Inquisition + Space Wolves + First War of Armageddon + Months of Shame). Same elasticity pattern as the four-book Gaunt's-Ghosts omnibuses in ssot-w40k-005 (1280 / 1370 chars).
