- **WebSearch:** mean ≈ 1.1 / book, max = 2 (over 10 books). 11 total searches:
  - 2 searches: W40K-0081 *Fire Caste* (first confirm Iverson + Phaedra + Tau-stalemate frame; second confirm dual-Imperial POV with Colonel Cutler vs solo Iverson POV — confirmed dual Imperial-side POV, not Iverson-vs-Tau dual).
  - 1 search each: W40K-0082 *Seventh Retribution* (confirm protagonist is Imperial-Fists Lysander on Opis with Iron-Warriors trauma frame and Chaos-cult antagonist, NOT Black-Templars-vs-Word-Bearers as my initial mental model had it), W40K-0083 *Valedor* (confirm Yriel + Iyanden + Biel-Tan + Commorragh Dark-Eldar alliance vs Hive-Fleets Leviathan + Kraken at Battle of Duriel — NO Iron Hands despite my initial mental model), W40K-0084 *Dark Hunters: Umbra Sumus* (confirm Jonah Kerne + Mortai + Phobian homeworld + Ras Hanem campaign + Punishers warband, and that Dark Hunters are White-Scars-successors NOT Raven-Guard-successors), W40K-0085 *Assassinorum: Execution Force* (confirm Severin Drask + Crimson Slaughter + Temple of Shades ritual), W40K-0086 *Silver Skulls: Portents* (confirm Sergeant Gileas Ur'ten + Valoria Quintus + Prognosticar / Inquisition manipulation subplot), W40K-0087 *Curse of the Wulfen* (confirm Harald Deathwolf + returning 13th-Company Wulfen + Magnus-glyph + Grey-Knights uneasy truce), W40K-0088 *Warlord: Fury of the God Machine* (confirm Krezoc / Pallidus Mor + Syagrius / Imperial Hunters + Warlord Titans *Gloria Vastator* and *Augustus Secutor*), W40K-0089 *Calgar's Fury* (confirm space hulk *Fury* + agri-world Iax in M41.812 + 1st/5th/7th/9th/10th companies + Inquisition + Mechanicus allies), W40K-0090 *Lucius: The Faultless Blade* (confirm Lucius vs World Eaters + Fabius Bile's Emperor's Children rival cabal + Dark Eldar Webway).
- **Per-book bullets:**
  - **W40K-0081 *Fire Caste* (Fehervari, 2013):** Imperial-Guard / Commissariat Tau-stalemate novel on jungle-death-world Phaedra. Dual Imperial POV — Commissar Holt Iverson (decade-on-Phaedra-corroded private-vendetta arc) and Colonel Ensor Cutler (regimental command). 19th Arkan Confederates as the deployed regiment, still carrying trauma from their home-world's recent rebellion. Phaedra as antagonist-by-environment (Heart-of-Darkness / Apocalypse-Now register, warp leaking through the canopy). Opens Fehervari's loose *Dark Coil* continuity (weird-40K standalones with shared cosmic-horror undercurrent, never explicitly cross-referenced). **First authority-layer Arkan-Confederates regiment surface form** and **first Phaedra surface form**; **first Fehervari Dark-Coil entry**.
  - **W40K-0082 *Seventh Retribution* (Counter, 2013):** Imperial-Fists novel built around Captain Darnath Lysander + 1st Company on civil-war Opis. Chaos cult inside the Opisian aristocracy reveals itself across the campaign; Lysander's Iron-Warriors-imprisonment trauma (carried over from *Iron Warriors* series) braids into the present war as the cult-master's nature becomes clear. Officio-Assassinorum support in the late-novel push. **First authority-layer Imperial-Fists *Lysander* surface form** (Lysander is a chapter-iconic character but had not appeared as POV in the authority layer before; W40K-0078 *Sons of Dorn* in ssot-w40k-008 was Imperial-Fists scout-recruitment register without Lysander).
  - **W40K-0083 *Valedor* (Haley, 2014):** Eldar-anchored Apocalypse-scale novel covering the Battle of Duriel. Prince Yriel of Iyanden hunts a Kraken-fragment that his farseers had previously diverted into the warp and that is now on a collision course with Hive Fleet Leviathan; the gene-exchange a merge would produce is unsurvivable. Three-way uneasy alliance — Iyanden, Biel-Tan (Aspect-Warrior bias), and Commorragh Dark Eldar. Somber-cosmic register. **First authority-layer entry where Eldar craftworlds *Iyanden* + *Biel-Tan* + Dark-Eldar craftworld *Commorragh* are all primary surface forms simultaneously**, and **first explicit Hive Fleet Leviathan + Hive Fleet Kraken surface forms** (vs. previous generic *Tyranids* faction-level mentions). **First Yriel surface form.**
  - **W40K-0084 *Dark Hunters: Umbra Sumus* (Kearney, 2015):** Series-start Dark-Hunters chapter novel. White-Scars-successor (NOT Raven-Guard-successor) whose silent-hunting doctrine comes from the Sahrmatae of homeworld Phobian (silent-hunters avoiding deadly Phobian Bats). Captain Jonah Kerne + Mortai Company defend Phobian against a feint Chaos raid, then pursue the Punishers warband to Ras Hanem for a slow-burn pursuit-into-decapitation campaign. **First authority-layer Dark-Hunters chapter surface form** (second White-Scars-successor entry in the authority layer this iteration, alongside Silver Skulls in this same batch); **first Phobian + Ras Hanem surface forms**.
  - **W40K-0085 *Assassinorum: Execution Force* (Parrino, 2015):** Officio-Assassinorum novella tied to the GW board-game box-set. Four assassins — Vindicare + Eversor + Callidus + Culexus — vs Severin Drask of the Crimson Slaughter at the Temple of Shades. Cooperation tension between the four temples is the structural spine as much as the Chaos opposition. **First authority-layer entries for Officio Assassinorum + Vindicare / Eversor / Callidus / Culexus temples** (all five new surface forms) and **first Crimson Slaughter Chaos-warband surface form**. Length_tier=short (novella-length tie-in, slightly above true novella).
  - **W40K-0086 *Silver Skulls: Portents* (Cawkwell, 2014):** Silver-Skulls chapter novel (sequel to *The Gildar Rift*, same continuity). White-Scars-successor whose Prognosticars (prophetic psyker-priests) decree the chapter's deployments. Sergeant Gileas Ur'ten + his squad to Valoria Quintus to crush a Prognosticar-foreseen-easy insurrection that turns out to be Inquisition-steered against the chapter itself. Slow-burn political-thriller / mystery wrapped around a war-story spine. **First authority-layer Silver-Skulls chapter surface form** (third White-Scars-successor chapter in the authority layer total, after the Cain crossover and the Dark Hunters in this same batch — recall White Scars themselves not yet entered as primary-protagonist faction). **First Prognosticars surface form.**
  - **W40K-0087 *Curse of the Wulfen* (Annandale, 2016):** War-Zone-Fenris / Gathering-Storm tie-in. Returning 13th-Company Wulfen (lost since the burning of Prospero ten thousand years prior) reappear across Fenris in scattered packs; Wolf-Lord Harald Deathwolf anchors the chapter response. The Wulfen turn out warp-tainted (chapter-brothers begin turning Wulfen on contact); scattered cult activity across the Fenris system resolves into Magnus's glyph; Grey Knights demand the Wulfen for the Ordo Malleus, uneasy truce brokered. **First authority-layer Wulfen sub-faction surface form** and **first Magnus the Red active-antagonist surface form** (vs. W40K-0067 *Farseer* / W40K-0080 *Emperor's Gift* mentions). Entry_point=requires_context (Gathering-Storm-event tie-in; standalone reading is possible but loses the long-arc framing). **Inquisition-consistency constraint** held — Ordo Malleus + Grey Knights both surface as supporting in the truce subplot.
  - **W40K-0088 *Warlord: Fury of the God-Machine* (Annandale, 2016):** Adeptus-Titanicus dual-legio ensemble. Pallidus Mor demi-legio (stoic / duty-bound, Tyranid-recovering) and Imperial Hunters legio (aristocratic / glory-seeking) forced to fight together against Chaos titans on a Chaos-overrun forge world. Dual princeps POV across the legio-friction line: Princeps Ferantha Krezoc (Warlord *Gloria Vastator*, Pallidus Mor) and Princeps Adrel Syagrius (Warlord *Augustus Secutor*, Imperial Hunters). **Second authority-layer Adeptus-Titanicus entry** (after W40K-0077 *Titanicus* in ssot-w40k-008); **first Pallidus Mor + Imperial Hunters Titan-Legio surface forms** (joining Invicta + Tempestus from *Titanicus*). Forge world is unnamed in summary sources I checked; `locations: []` rather than inventing a name per Brief 061's hallu-disziplin.
  - **W40K-0089 *Calgar's Fury* (Kearney, 2016):** Standalone Ultramarines space-hulk novel. Marneus Calgar + Ultramarines 1st/5th/7th/9th/10th companies vs the hulk *Fury* near agri-world Iax in M41.812. Inquisition + Adeptus Mechanicus detachments embedded under their own command + their own agendas; novel deliberately blurs Imperium-faction lines. Tyranid + Genestealer + Chaos defenders on the hulk. **First authority-layer Ultramarines chapter as primary-protagonist surface form** (Ultramarines were primary-mentioned in earlier batches but never as the lead chapter); **first Marneus Calgar surface form** and **first Iax + Ultramar surface forms**. Macragge stays mentioned-only (not the campaign theatre). Morally-murky register kept tight to summary sources.
  - **W40K-0090 *Lucius: The Faultless Blade* (St. Martin, 2016):** Series-start Lucius-the-Eternal trilogy book 1. Lucius — Soulthief, Slaaneshi reincarnation curse — gathers his exhausted Cohort to confront converging pressures: a World-Eaters Khornate champion pursuing him for decades, a rival Fabius-Bile-aligned Emperor's-Children cabal, and a Dark-Eldar Kabal that has tracked him into the Webway. Servitor-POV intervals around the chapters frame Lucius from outside his narcissism. Themes: loss / addiction / decay / mortality-impossibility. **First authority-layer Emperor's Children as primary-protagonist surface form** (previous Emperor's Children appearances were Heretic-Astartes-level only); **first Lucius the Eternal POV surface form** and **first Fabius Bile antagonist surface form**. POV side = chaos (first chaos-POV-primary entry in the authority layer since the Iron-Warriors / Honsou omnibus arc in ssot-w40k-007).
- **value_outside_vocabulary** (candidates surfaced by this batch, none promoted):
  - `commissar` — protagonist_class still has no `commissar` value. Same workaround as ssot-w40k-002/003/004 batches: `guardsman`.
  - `princeps` / `titan_commander` — protagonist_class has no `princeps` value. *Warlord* and the earlier *Titanicus* (W40K-0077) workaround used `multi`. A `princeps` value (or `tech_priest` reuse via the Collegia-Titanica framing) would tighten this register.
  - `assassin` / `imperial_assassin` — protagonist_class has no `assassin` value. *Assassinorum: Execution Force* workaround used `multi` (four-temple ensemble), but a single `assassin` value would map the temple-vocation cleanly.
  - `dark_coil` / `weird_40k` / `cosmic_taint` — *Fire Caste*'s register isn't well captured by `grimdark + cosmic_horror + somber + philosophical` alone; Fehervari's Dark-Coil continuity is a distinctive sub-mode that the recommender could surface as its own theme/tone facet. Considered + skipped without facet-catalog promotion.
  - `space_hulk_expedition` / `hulk_recon` — *Calgar's Fury*'s shape (chapter-master-leading-deep-recon-into-hulk) is shared with several earlier Space Marine Battles entries but no facet captures the procedural-into-hulk arc. Workaround used: `journey + mystery + siege + cosmic_horror`.
  - `prophecy_subversion` / `psyker_manipulation` — *Silver Skulls: Portents*'s slow-burn ("the Prognosticars themselves are the operation's target") isn't well captured by `mystery + political_thriller` alone; a `prophecy` or `psyker_subversion` sub-tag would add useful texture.
  - `apocalypse_scale` — *Valedor*'s Apocalypse-scale battle-scale isn't captured by `last_stand + siege + war_story` plus `scope=sector`; a sub-tag denoting Apocalypse-style massed engagements (super-heavy and Wraith-construct levels) would help.
- **Notable surface-form frequencies within this batch:**
  - *Factions (canonical-resolver match):* Adeptus Astartes ×7 (every Astartes-anchored entry except Fire Caste and Valedor + Assassinorum: Execution Force), Chaos ×9 (every entry except Valedor — Valedor's antagonist is Tyranids), Heretic Astartes ×6 (Seventh Retribution + Dark Hunters: Umbra Sumus + Assassinorum + Silver Skulls + Curse of the Wulfen + Lucius), Imperial Guard ×4 (Fire Caste + Dark Hunters + Silver Skulls + Warlord — supporting in the Astartes-anchored entries, primary in Fire Caste), Inquisition ×4 (Seventh Retribution + Silver Skulls + Curse of the Wulfen + Calgar's Fury), Adeptus Mechanicus ×2 (Warlord + Calgar's Fury), Tyranids ×2 (Valedor + Calgar's Fury), Dark Eldar ×2 (Valedor + Lucius).
  - *Factions (new surface forms in this batch):* **Arkan Confederates** ×1 (Fire Caste — first appearance, distinct from the Tanith / Phantine / Valhallan / Mordian regiments in earlier batches), **Tau Empire** ×1 antagonist-role (Fire Caste — second authority-layer appearance after W40K-0070 *Fire Warrior* in ssot-w40k-007, this time as antagonist-not-protagonist), **Iron Warriors** ×1 antagonist-role (Seventh Retribution — first authority-layer antagonist-tier appearance since the W40K-0058/0059/0060 Iron-Warriors-protagonist omnibus arc in ssot-w40k-006/007), **Iyanden** ×1 primary-role (Valedor — first explicit craftworld-faction surface form, distinct from generic Eldar), **Biel-Tan** ×1 primary-role (Valedor — second explicit craftworld-faction surface form), **Hive Fleet Leviathan** ×1 antagonist (Valedor — first explicit hive-fleet surface form), **Hive Fleet Kraken** ×1 antagonist (Valedor — second explicit hive-fleet surface form), **Dark Hunters** ×1 primary-role (Dark Hunters: Umbra Sumus — first appearance), **Punishers** ×1 antagonist (Dark Hunters: Umbra Sumus — first Chaos-warband surface form distinct from prior Bloodborn / Blood Pact / Sons of Sek / Roaring Blades shapes), **Officio Assassinorum** primary ×1 (Assassinorum: Execution Force — first appearance), **Vindicare Temple** + **Eversor Temple** + **Callidus Temple** + **Culexus Temple** ×1 each primary-role (Assassinorum — four first-appearances), **Crimson Slaughter** ×1 antagonist (Assassinorum — first Chaos-warband surface form), **Silver Skulls** ×1 primary-role (Silver Skulls: Portents — first appearance), **Wulfen** ×1 primary-role (Curse of the Wulfen — first appearance as distinct sub-faction; previously only Space-Wolves at chapter level), **Thousand Sons** ×1 antagonist (Curse of the Wulfen — second authority-layer appearance after W40K-0079 *Atlas Infernal* in ssot-w40k-008, this time as primary antagonist driving the campaign), **Tzeentch** ×1 antagonist (Curse of the Wulfen — first authority-layer Chaos God surface form distinct from the umbrella *Chaos* faction; prior batches had Slaanesh and Khorne implicit in Cain / Lucius arcs), **Pallidus Mor** ×1 primary-role (Warlord — first Titan-Legio surface form distinct from Invicta + Tempestus from ssot-w40k-008), **Imperial Hunters** ×1 primary-role (Warlord — second new Titan-Legio surface form this batch), **Ultramarines** ×1 primary-role (Calgar's Fury — first authority-layer Ultramarines-as-primary surface form), **Genestealer Cults** ×1 antagonist (Calgar's Fury — second authority-layer appearance after the W40K-0012/0016 Cain-arc supporting mentions in ssot-w40k-002), **Emperor's Children** ×1 primary-role (Lucius — first appearance as primary protagonist faction), **Slaanesh** ×1 primary-role (Lucius — second authority-layer Chaos God surface form), **World Eaters** ×1 antagonist (Lucius — first appearance), **Khorne** ×1 antagonist (Lucius — third authority-layer Chaos God surface form), **Fabius Bile's Coterie** ×1 antagonist (Lucius — first Bile-faction surface form).

- **Notes:**
  - **Continued first-appearance density.** Following the ssot-w40k-008 surge, this batch carries another heavy first-X density: five new Astartes chapters as primary protagonist faction (Imperial Fists is technically a return-to-primary via Lysander rather than first-appearance, since Sons of Dorn (W40K-0078) was Imperial-Fists scout-recruitment register; Dark Hunters + Silver Skulls + Wulfen-sub-faction + Ultramarines + Emperor's Children are clean first-primaries), two new Eldar craftworlds (Iyanden + Biel-Tan as primary surface forms distinct from generic Eldar), two new hive fleets (Leviathan + Kraken), Officio Assassinorum + its four temples (five new surface forms), the Crimson Slaughter + Punishers + Fabius Bile's Coterie Chaos warbands, two new Titan Legios (Pallidus Mor + Imperial Hunters), and three Chaos God surface forms (Tzeentch + Slaanesh + Khorne — promoted from generic *Chaos* umbrella). Resolver brief at cumulative=100 (`ssot-w40k-010`) will have a very dense pile of canonical chapter / legion / Ordo / Chaos-God / warband / craftworld / hive-fleet / Inquisition-temple surface forms to fold into reference data.
  - **No format-compliance or low-confidence flags this iteration.** Mid-2010s Black-Library entries are uniformly well-documented in summary sources (Lexicanum / Fandom / Goodreads / Track-of-Words / publisher product pages); secondary-source coverage was strong enough across all ten entries that no `data_conflict { field: format }` or `low_confidence { field: characters }` flags were warranted. This contrasts with the ssot-w40k-008 batch which carried one of each (W40K-0074 *Brothers of the Snake* fix-up flag + W40K-0075 *Eldar Prophecy* low-coverage flag).
  - **Warlord: Fury of the God-Machine `locations: []`.** Forge world was not explicitly named in the summary sources I checked. Per Brief 061's hallu-disziplin (lieber knapp und korrekt als breit und erfunden), left empty rather than invent. The factions cover the relevant context (Pallidus Mor + Imperial Hunters + Adeptus Titanicus + Adeptus Mechanicus); resolver / vocabulary brief later can surface the forge-world name if needed.
  - **Inquisition-consistency constraint** (Brief 061): triggered cleanly for one entry — W40K-0087 *Curse of the Wulfen* (Grey Knights demanding the Wulfen for the Ordo Malleus → Grey Knights + Ordo Malleus + Inquisition all supporting-tier). W40K-0089 *Calgar's Fury* has Inquisition presence but no on-page Inquisitor POV — kept supporting; W40K-0086 *Silver Skulls: Portents* has Inquisition as the manipulation-revealing supporting tier but no on-page named Inquisitor — kept supporting. W40K-0082 *Seventh Retribution* has Officio-Assassinorum-not-Inquisition as the late-novel Imperial-special-operation support — Officio Assassinorum is a separate surface form from Inquisition.
  - **Surface-form treue compliance.** "Imperial Guard" over "Astra Militarum" across the batch (publication range 2013-2016, all on the boundary of the 2014 rename; W40K-0081 *Fire Caste* is March-2013 pre-rename, others are post-rename but the books' own surface forms remained "Imperial Guard" in-text). "Eldar" over "Aeldari" across the Valedor entry (2014 publication, pre-9th-edition spelling). "Dark Eldar" over "Drukhari" (Valedor + Lucius both pre-rename). "Crimson Slaughter" + "Punishers" + "Wulfen" + "Pallidus Mor" + "Imperial Hunters" + "Fabius Bile's Coterie" all canonical Black-Library surface forms.
  - **Synopsis-length elasticity.** Three entries (W40K-0083 *Valedor* at 1180, W40K-0087 *Curse of the Wulfen* at 1295, W40K-0090 *Lucius* at 1246) sit just over the 1200-char soft cap. Justified by ensemble register: Valedor has three-Eldar-faction tri-alliance + two hive fleets to introduce; Curse of the Wulfen has Wulfen-return + Magnus-glyph + Grey-Knights-truce + Thousand-Sons-revenge to introduce simultaneously; Lucius has converging-pressures structure (World Eaters + Fabius Bile + Dark Eldar) plus the Soulthief / reincarnation-curse framing. Same elasticity pattern as ssot-w40k-008 W40K-0077 + W40K-0080.

Maintainer kann via `skip-50-stop`-Marker bei Bedarf überschreiben, aber Cowork-Tendenz aus Brief 061: lieber Resolver-Pass sofort nach erster Pause.

- **Per-book bullets:**
  - **W40K-0091 *Shroud of Night* (Clark, 2017):** Alpha-Legion-Chaos-anchored novel on oceanic hive-world Tsadrekha during the Noctis Aeterna. Strike-Captain Kassar + the Unsung warband (stranded-since-Scouring) infiltrate to seize/corrupt the planetary Astropathic beacon; Khârn the Betrayer leads a frontal World-Eaters assault on the same target; Khornate / Slaaneshi / Tzeentchian / rival Alpha-Legion warbands all converge. Imperial defenders: an Imperial Saint, Tsadrekhan Guardsmen, Adepta Sororitas, Imperial Fists. **First authority-layer entry where Alpha Legion is the primary protagonist faction** and **first Khârn the Betrayer + Kassar + Tsadrekha + Unsung surface forms**. The Imperial Saint in the defence may or may not be Saint Celestine in continuity with W40K-0100 — left unnamed in the synopsis per Brief-061 hallu-disziplin (Andy Clark wrote both novels and has stated they share thematic furniture without direct continuation, per the search evidence for *Celestine*).
  - **W40K-0092 *The Last Hunt* (MacNiven, 2017):** White-Scars 4th Company novel on steppe-Honour-World Darkand under Joghaten Khan, post-Great-Rift / early-Gathering-Storm window. Hive-Fleet-Leviathan splinter + Genestealer-Cult-PDF-compromise as the primary antagonist axis, then triangulates with an Aeldari Craftworld force and a Drukhari Kabal offering uneasy alliance. **First authority-layer entry where White Scars is the primary protagonist faction** (previously absent), **first Darkand surface form**, and **first authority-layer use of 'Aeldari' / 'Drukhari' surface forms** (post-rename 8th-edition vocabulary, distinct from the 'Eldar' / 'Dark Eldar' pre-rename surface forms in ssot-w40k-007/008/009 entries).
  - **W40K-0093 *Sons of the Hydra* (Sanders, 2017):** Alpha-Legion warband novel (loose follow-up to *Shroud of Night* but stands alone). Occam the Untrue + the Redacted warband (mixed-Astartes-and-renegade) operating out of the Maelstrom under Inquisition pursuit, with a layered infiltration arc culminating at the cold heart of the galaxy. **Second authority-layer Alpha-Legion entry this iteration** — Shroud-of-Night is the frontal-siege-with-twists register, Sons-of-the-Hydra is the long-range-infiltration-onion register. **First Occam the Untrue + Redacted surface forms.**
  - **W40K-0094 *Lukas the Trickster* (Reynolds, 2018):** Space-Wolves trickster-duel novel on Fenris during Helwinter. Lukas the Strifeson / Jackalwolf (Blood Claw, chapter-iconic prankster) is reassigned by Wolf-Priest Galerunner to Wolf-Lord Kjarl Grimblood's Great Company; Drukhari raid under Duke Traevelliath Sliscus / Serpent of Commorragh lands; trickster-vs-trickster escalating-ambush duel ensues with surviving Fenrisian tribes joining. **First authority-layer entry where the *Drukhari* (post-rename) surface form appears as a primary antagonist faction**; **first Lukas the Strifeson + Duke Sliscus + Kjarl Grimblood + Galerunner surface forms**.
  - **W40K-0095 *Imperator: Wrath of the Omnissiah* (Thorpe, 2018):** Adeptus-Titanicus Imperator-class-titan novel. Legio Metalica's *Casus Belli* + Magos Exasus deployed onto forge-world Nicomedua to crush a tech-priest-led secession under the Cicatrix Maledictum's cover; while the Titans engage corrupted-Knight + traitor-Titan + Dark-Mechanicum + cultist-horde opposition in city-scale war, Exasus runs a saboteur-hunt inside the *Casus Belli*'s own crew-hierarchy. 'Hunt for Red October with an Imperator Titan' (Thorpe's own pitch). **Third authority-layer Adeptus-Titanicus entry** (after W40K-0077 *Titanicus* in ssot-w40k-008 + W40K-0088 *Warlord* in ssot-w40k-009); **first Imperator-class-titan + Legio Metalica + Nicomedua + *Casus Belli* + Magos Exasus + Dark Mechanicum surface forms**.
  - **W40K-0096 *Legacy of Dorn* (Lee, 2018):** Crimson-Fists chapter novel set during the ork invasion of Rynn's World (same WAAAGH! as Parker's *Rynn's World*). Veteran-Sergeant Sandor Galleas's Sternguard squad + battered human-survivor band running guerrilla warfare through the wasteland and ruined-city terrain after the chapter's fortress-monastery Arx Tyrannus is destroyed. **First authority-layer entry where the Crimson Fists is the primary protagonist faction** (Imperial-Fists-successor register distinct from W40K-0078 *Sons of Dorn*'s parent-chapter register in ssot-w40k-008); **first Sandor Galleas + Rynn's World + Arx Tyrannus surface forms**.
  - **W40K-0097 *Blood of Iax* (MacNiven, 2018):** Primaris-only Ultramarines novel on ork-held mining world Ikara IX during the Dark-Imperium era. Strike Force Fulminata under brothers Chaplain Kastor + Apothecary Polixis vs WAAAGH! under Warlord Urgork, with the apothecary-targeted-not-chapter-master twist as the structural spine. Multi-POV chapters include other Fulminata Astartes (notably Reivers as a Primaris-only terror-spec register), an Astra-Militarum Lieutenant on Ikara, and ork POVs. **First authority-layer Primaris-Astartes-anchored novel**; **first Strike Force Fulminata + Kastor + Polixis + Urgork + Ikara IX + Reivers surface forms**. Note: the title's *Iax* (Ultramar agri-world from W40K-0089 *Calgar's Fury* in ssot-w40k-009) is metaphorical — refers to the Ultramarines gene-line, not the campaign's actual setting.
  - **W40K-0098 *The Lords of Silence* (Wraight, 2018):** Death-Guard warband novel built around First-Captain Vorx (Heresy-era legionnaire, Mortarion-pre-fall-Barbarus tenure, numerologically-obsessed). Their grand cruiser *Solace*, part of Abaddon's 13th-Black-Crusade fleet aimed at Ultramar, is thrown off-course into deep warp; the book runs three parallel investigations — geographic (where are we?), strategic (how do we rejoin?), and forensic (which of our own caused the jump?) — with a Word-Bearers vessel alliance for the rejoin. **First authority-layer entry where Death Guard is the primary protagonist faction**, **first Nurgle Chaos-God surface form** (vs prior generic *Chaos* faction), **first Word Bearers + Vorx + Slert + Philemon + *Solace* + Abaddon the Despoiler + 13th Black Crusade surface forms**. Detailed plague-monks-meets-Hercule-Poirot register; structural payoff is patience-as-Astartes-tactical-doctrine.
  - **W40K-0099 *Spear of the Emperor* (Dembski-Bowden, 2018):** Memoir-framed first-person Astartes novel narrated decades-after-the-events by helot Anuradha. POV chain: Anuradha → Lieutenant Amadeus Kaias Incarius of the Mentors chapter, sent across the Great Rift into Elara's Veil nebula in Imperium Nihilus to assess the survival of three frontier-protector chapters (Star Scorpions / Celestial Lions / Emperor's Spears). Spine: Amadeus's gradual transition from observer-diplomat to fighting-brother of the Spears under the realisation that there's no way back through the Rift. **First authority-layer entry where the Emperor's Spears chapter is the primary protagonist faction**, **first explicit Mentors / Mentor Legion surface form**, **first Star Scorpions + Celestial Lions surface forms**, **first Anuradha + Amadeus Kaias Incarius + Elara's Veil surface forms**, and **first long-form helot-POV register** in the authority layer.
  - **W40K-0100 *Celestine* (Clark, 2019):** Standalone short novel (Lexicanum + Track-of-Words register: 'short novel' / novella-length). Saint Celestine — Adepta-Sororitas Living Saint — fights a desperate ground battle in Imperium Nihilus on a world the saint manifests on once more, while a parallel inward strand traces her journey through the torment-realm where the cost of her gift is reckoned and where the question of whether *faith itself* is a corrupted thing surfaces as slow philosophical horror. Set in the post-Cadia / Gathering-Storm window. **First authority-layer entry where Adepta Sororitas is the primary protagonist faction** and **first explicit Saint Celestine surface form** (the unnamed Imperial Saint at Tsadrekha in W40K-0091 *Shroud of Night* may be Celestine in continuity but is not confirmed in summary sources). **`data_conflict { field: format, suggestion: short_novel }` flag set** — Lexicanum + Track-of-Words + Black-Library product page consistently characterise this release as 'short novel' / novella-length, closer to the *Assassinorum: Execution Force* register from ssot-w40k-009 than a standard novel.
- **value_outside_vocabulary** (candidates surfaced by this batch, none promoted):
  - `chaos_legion_primary` — Alpha-Legion-as-primary-protagonist + Death-Guard-as-primary-protagonist pair in this batch (W40K-0091 / W40K-0093 / W40K-0098) shares structural shape with the ssot-w40k-007 Iron-Warriors-omnibus arc but with even denser chaos-POV register. A `chaos_legion_focus` or `traitor_legion_pov` sub-tag would tighten this register beyond `pov_side=chaos`.
  - `helot` / `chapter_serf` — *Spear of the Emperor*'s memoir-from-helot register isn't well captured by `multi` protagonist_class + `civilian` workarounds; a `chapter_serf` value would map the household-of-a-Marine vocation cleanly.
  - `living_saint` — *Celestine*'s register isn't well captured by `sister` protagonist_class alone; the Living-Saint frame is qualitatively different from baseline Adepta-Sororitas register (immortality / torment-realm / death-rebirth cycle).
  - `primaris_focus` / `dark_imperium_era` — *Blood of Iax* and *Spear of the Emperor* both anchor in the Dark-Imperium era with Primaris-only / Primaris-emissary registers; a `dark_imperium` or `primaris_register` facet would distinguish these from the pre-Great-Rift Astartes-anchored novels in earlier batches. Workaround: `requires_context` entry_point + explicit Great-Rift mention in synopsis (but neither *Blood of Iax* nor *Spear of the Emperor* used `requires_context` here — both are sufficiently self-contained that `standalone` is the better fit).
  - `mystery_in_chaos_register` — *Lords of Silence*'s whodunnit-inside-Death-Guard-ranks register isn't a clean `mystery + political_thriller` mix; the structural shape (Death-Guard-as-detective) is distinct from prior `mystery`-flagged entries (which lean Inquisition/Astartes-loyalist). A `chaos_internal_mystery` or `traitor_legion_investigation` sub-tag would tighten this.
  - `titan_focus_internal` — *Imperator: Wrath of the Omnissiah*'s 'inside an Imperator-Titan' setting (the Titan as both vehicle and primary location) isn't captured by `Adeptus Titanicus` faction tag + planetary scope alone. The *Casus Belli* functions as a quasi-location-character hybrid (listed in `locations` per W40K-0089 *Calgar's Fury*'s space-hulk-*Fury* precedent).
  - `torment_realm` / `allegorical_strand` — *Celestine*'s dual outer-battle / inner-allegorical-journey structure isn't well captured by `journey + character_study + philosophical` alone. A `dual_strand` or `allegorical_journey` facet would tighten this.
- **Notable surface-form frequencies within this batch:**

- **Notes:**
  - **Continued first-appearance density at the 100-cumulative mark.** This batch carries the same heavy first-X density as ssot-w40k-008 / ssot-w40k-009: eight new Astartes chapters/legions as primary protagonist faction (Alpha Legion ×2, White Scars, Crimson Fists, Death Guard, Emperor's Spears, Mentors, and Ultramarines-second-appearance), Adepta Sororitas as primary protagonist faction (Celestine — first appearance), Nurgle as primary Chaos-God surface form (Lords of Silence — completes the 4-Chaos-Gods set with Tzeentch / Slaanesh / Khorne from ssot-w40k-009), three Mechanicum entries (Legio Metalica + Imperial Knights + Skitarii + Dark Mechanicum from *Imperator*), two post-rename xenos surface forms (Aeldari + Drukhari — distinct from the pre-rename 'Eldar' / 'Dark Eldar' surface forms in prior batches), two named-vessel-as-location surface forms (*Solace* + *Casus Belli*), and three Imperium-Nihilus / Dark-Imperium-era frame surface forms (Imperium Nihilus + Great Rift + Elara's Veil). Resolver brief at cumulative=100 will have a dense pile of new canonical chapter / legion / Chaos-God / Mechanicum / vessel / Dark-Imperium-era surface forms to fold into reference data, including the **first systematic post-rename xenos-vocabulary boundary** (Eldar→Aeldari / Dark Eldar→Drukhari).
  - **One `data_conflict { field: format, suggestion: short_novel }` flag** on W40K-0100 *Celestine*. Lexicanum + Track-of-Words + Black-Library product page consistently characterise this release as 'short novel' / novella-length, closer to the *Assassinorum: Execution Force* register from ssot-w40k-009 (which also had length_tier=short rather than standard) than to a standard novel. The SSOT format=`novel` is plausibly correct (it's marketed as a novel) but the page-count / length-register is closer to novella; flag preserves the question for Maintainer Excel-SSOT-workflow.
  - **No `low_confidence` flags this iteration.** All ten entries have strong post-2017 Black-Library coverage (Lexicanum, Track-of-Words, Goonhammer, Grimdark Magazine, publisher product pages, author blogs — Dembski-Bowden's own blog gives unusually detailed *Spear of the Emperor* context). Mid-2010s and later Black-Library entries are well-documented enough to support full surface-form coverage without flagging.
  - **Inquisition-consistency constraint** (Brief 061): triggered cleanly for one entry — W40K-0099 *Spear of the Emperor* (Inquisition's purge of the Celestial Lions chapter is part of the Imperium-Nihilus-frame backstory → Inquisition antagonist-tier). W40K-0093 *Sons of the Hydra* has Inquisition as the pursuit antagonist but no on-page Inquisitor POV — kept antagonist; constraint doesn't trip without an Inquisitor character. W40K-0091 *Shroud of Night* has Adepta Sororitas as Imperial defenders but no on-page Inquisitor — Adepta Sororitas is a separate surface form from Inquisition.
  - **Surface-form treue compliance.** "Aeldari" + "Drukhari" used for the 2017+ post-rename entries (Last Hunt + Lukas the Trickster) per the search-source register. "Astra Militarum" used for the Dark-Imperium-era entries (Blood of Iax + Celestine — both 2018-2019 set post-Great-Rift, in-text-register confirmed); "Imperial Guard" retained for Last Hunt (2017, on the boundary, in-text-register still 'Imperial Guard' in summaries) + Legacy of Dorn + Shroud of Night (2017-2018, on the boundary). Per-book judgment call; the surface forms are different and the resolver pass will need to either map both to a single canonical Astra-Militarum entry or maintain both as historical-publication-window surface forms. "Drukhari" + "Aeldari" deliberate choice for the post-rename batch, contrast against "Eldar" + "Dark Eldar" in ssot-w40k-007/008/009. "Saint Celestine" canonical, "Khârn the Betrayer" canonical (with the â diacritic from Black Library's own surface form).
  - **Synopsis-length elasticity.** Eight of ten entries sit over the 1200-char soft cap (range 1182–1573; lowest is Imperator at 1182, highest is Spear of the Emperor at 1573). Justified by the density of first-authority-layer surface forms each entry introduces: most entries are introducing a chapter / legion / faction / Chaos God / Dark-Imperium-era frame for the first time in the authority layer, so each synopsis has to do double-duty — set the plot AND establish the surface forms for the resolver pass. Same elasticity pattern as ssot-w40k-008 W40K-0077 + W40K-0080 and ssot-w40k-009 W40K-0083 + W40K-0087 + W40K-0090, but pushed harder here at the cumulative-100 mark.

- **Per-book bullets:**
  - **W40K-0101 *Honourbound* (Harrison, 2019):** Severina-Raine series-opener. Commissar Severina Raine + Eleventh Antari Rifles in the Bale Stars Crusade vs the Sighted Chaos cult. Three-arc structure: present campaign (drop-strike / urban grind / final cult-citadel assault), Schola-Progenium / sister-Lucia flashbacks, intra-Crusade malfeasance subplot. **First authority-layer entry with a Commissar as primary POV** (protagonist_class=`guardsman` per the Cain / Gaunt workaround until a `commissar` value is promoted); **first Antari Rifles + the Sighted + Bale Stars surface forms**.
  - **W40K-0102 *Requiem Infernal* (Fehervari, 2019):** Dark-Coil-continuity standalone. Sister-Hospitaller Asenath Hyades returns to her birthworld Candleworld escorting Astra-Militarum survivors of a xenos encounter; ostensibly investigating heresy in the Order of the Last Candle / Eternal Candle, privately laying her own ghosts. Parallel POV: itinerant preacher Jonah Tythe with his own pilgrimage. Cosmic-horror + mystery + character-study register; faith-and-doubt as plot engine. **First authority-layer Hospitaller-POV novel + first Order of the Last Candle / Candleworld surface forms.**
  - **W40K-0103 *Belisarius Cawl: The Great Work* (Haley, 2019):** Cawl + Tetrarch Felix + Scythes-of-the-Emperor remnants on Sotha (Scythes' Tyranid-ravaged homeworld). Necron tomb-raid under the chapter monastery + Cawl reckoning with 10,000 years of lost/deleted/stolen memories. **First authority-layer entry with an Adeptus-Mechanicus Archmagos as primary POV** (Cawl); **first Sotha + Scythes of the Emperor + Tetrarch Felix surface forms**. Note: Tomb-raiding-Necrons element is on-page Necron-faction antagonist, BUT Trazyn the Infinite does NOT appear in this novel (a recurring training-data conflation with Trazyn's collector-character; verified-absent via Lexicanum product description + Grimdark-Magazine review).
  - **W40K-0104 *Rites of Passage* (Brooks, 2019):** Lady Chettamandey series-start. Frail-elderly-Navigator-widow-and-murderer Lady Chettamandey Brobantis vs warp-cultist Radimir Niklau (fresh from Galimo-Prime ritual, harvesting Navigator warp-eyes on Vorlese). House-Brobantis succession + cult-mystery + court-intrigue register. **First authority-layer entry where the Navis Nobilite + House Brobantis are the primary protagonist faction.** Protagonist_class tagged `civilian` (closest available; Navigators have no own class).
  - **W40K-0105 *Mark of Faith* (Harrison, 2020):** Standalone Sororitas-pilgrimage novel post-Ophelia-VII. Sister Evangeline (Order of Our Martyred Lady) + Inquisitor Ahri Ravara (Ordo Hereticus) cross the Great Rift into Imperium Nihilus to recover the Shield of Saint Katherine. Dual POV: Evangeline's raw-faith arc + Ravara's Thousand-Sons-Sorcerer / Sofika-crippled subplot. Sister Augusta as Evangeline's anchor. **First authority-layer entry where Order of Our Martyred Lady is the primary sub-Order** (prior Sororitas appearances were generic Adepta-Sororitas-faction-level). Inquisition-consistency: Ravara is Ordo Hereticus, Inquisition + Ordo Hereticus both tagged primary.
  - **W40K-0106 *Ephrael Stern: The Heretic Saint* (Annandale, 2020):** Prose-follow-up to the *Daemonifuge* graphic-novel mythology. Stern the Thrice-Born / Daemonifuge / Heretic Saint + Harlequin companion Kyganil 100-year webway pilgrimage; webway meeting with Yvraine, Herald of Ynnead, updates Stern on Imperium-Nihilus / Guilliman's return. **First authority-layer entry with Harlequins + the Ynnari + Yvraine as on-page characters + the Black Library as a sought destination**; **first Ephrael Stern + Kyganil + Daemonifuge / Thrice-Born / Heretic Saint surface forms**. Entry_point=`requires_context` (Daemonifuge mythology reading is genuinely helpful).
  - **W40K-0107 *Brutal Kunnin* (Brooks, 2020):** Goff Big-Mek Ufthak Blackhawk + Mogrot Redtoof + Nizkwik-the-grot vs Adeptus-Mechanicus forge world Hephaesto, with Kaptin Badrukk's Freebooterz already on-planet under Da-Biggest-Big-Mek's "temporary co-operation" order. **First authority-layer entry where Orks are the primary protagonist faction** (protagonist_class=`pc_xenos`, pov_side=`xenos`); tone dropped grimdark for **`satirical + action_heavy`** — Brooks's Ork-prose register is comedy-grim, similar-but-inverted to the Cain-novels exception in ssot-w40k-002.
  - **W40K-0108 *The Infinite and the Divine* (Rath, 2020):** Dual-Necron rivalry between Trazyn the Infinite (Solemnace galleries, artefact-collector) and Orikan the Diviner (Sautekh chronomancer-prophet). Orikan steals from Trazyn's galleries to find the last true Necrontyr Phaeron's tomb on Cepharil / Serenade (formerly Cephris); Triarch Council forces co-op; spans millennia; Genestealer-Cult uprising + Imperial exterminatus climax; Trazyn-escape + Orikan-stranded ending. **First authority-layer entry where Necrons are the sole primary protagonist faction**; **first Trazyn the Infinite + Orikan the Diviner + Solemnace + Cepharil / Serenade + Triarch Council + Sautekh Dynasty surface forms.** Tone: `philosophical + satirical + action_heavy + grimdark` — dual-Necron comedy of antiquated arrogance is a distinctive register.
  - **W40K-0109 *Indomitus* (Thorpe, 2020):** 9th-edition launch novel. Crusade Fleet Quintus's *Ithraca's Vengeance* under Captain Aeschelus + Lts Nemetus + Praxamedes stranded in becalmed-warp inside the Pariah Nexus; Silent Kingdom soul-harvest tech is the antagonist superstructure. Dual-POV with Necron Overlord Simut + Plasmancer Ah-hotep + Skorpekh-Lord Zozar. Last-stand-vs-warn-Guilliman pivot. **First Pariah Nexus + Silent Kingdom + Crusade Fleet Quintus + Ithraca's Vengeance + Aeschelus + Nemetus + Praxamedes + Simut + Ah-hotep + Zozar surface forms.** Pov_side=`dual` (Ultramarines + Necron alternating).
  - **W40K-0110 *Silent Hunters* (Albert, 2021):** Carcharodons-chapter brothers-separated-by-feud novel. Te Kahurangi (the Pale Nomad Librarian, returning from MacNiven's earlier Carcharodons books) + Chaplain Tangata Manu (his brother, ancient feud) pursue a stolen relic into Commorragh / the Dark City; Drukhari antagonist. Chapter-serf POVs: Iraia + Jona. **First authority-layer entry where the Carcharodons / Space Sharks chapter is the primary protagonist faction**; **first Commorragh + Sagaraya + Te Kahurangi + Tangata Manu + Iraia + Jona surface forms.** Training-data conflation caught pre-write: this is Carcharodons, NOT Raven Guard despite both being shadow-operations-oriented chapters; the roster slug `silent-hunters` and author Edoardo Albert hold (only the chapter-assignment in my pre-search mental model was wrong).
- **value_outside_vocabulary** (candidates surfaced by this batch, none promoted):
  - `commissar` — protagonist_class still has no `commissar` value. Same workaround as ssot-w40k-002/003/004 batches: `guardsman`. *Honourbound* re-surfaces this as a high-priority promotion candidate (Severina Raine is a non-comedic Commissar POV — distinct register from the satirical Cain books).
  - `navigator` — protagonist_class has no `navigator` value. *Rites of Passage* workaround used `civilian`. The Navis-Nobilite vocation is sufficiently distinct (psyker-adjacent / non-combatant / hereditary-house-political) that a `navigator` value would map cleanly.
  - `hospitaller` — Sororitas sub-order has no facet representation. *Requiem Infernal*'s Hospitaller register (healing / pastoral / not-Militant) is distinct from the Militant register that has dominated prior Sororitas appearances; a `hospitaller` sub-tag or a more general `medical_pov` facet would tighten this.
  - `living_saint` — re-surfaces as a candidate (raised at ssot-w40k-010 with *Celestine* and *Mark of Faith*'s Saint-Katherine-relic register). Both *Mark of Faith* and *Ephrael Stern* in this batch lean on saint / heretic-saint registers that the `sister` protagonist_class doesn't cover.
  - `webway` / `harlequin_register` — *Ephrael Stern* anchors in the webway with Harlequin Kyganil + Yvraine; the cross-Aeldari-Imperial register isn't well captured by `dual` pov_side alone. A `webway_journey` or `cross_faction_pilgrimage` sub-tag would tighten.
  - `ork_satirical` / `pc_xenos_comic` — *Brutal Kunnin*'s `satirical + action_heavy` register stands at the boundary of the Cain-style `satirical` register; the Ork-side comedy is distinct enough (the joke is *on* the protagonists, not delivered by them) to merit consideration as its own sub-tag.
  - `necron_comedy` / `dual_xenos_pov` — *The Infinite and the Divine*'s `philosophical + satirical` Necron-rivalry register is qualitatively distinct from the *Brutal Kunnin* Ork-satirical register and from prior Necron antagonist registers (which were uniformly cold / inhuman / grimdark). A `necron_personality` or `dual_xenos_buddy_arc` facet would tighten this.
  - `9th_edition_onramp` / `edition_launch_tie_in` — *Indomitus* is structurally an explicit edition-launch on-ramp (analogous to the 8th-edition *Dark Imperium* trilogy starter); `standalone` entry_point covers the readability but loses the "this is the Black-Library-equivalent of the 9th-edition core-book intro" framing. A `core_lore_onramp` sub-tag would help.
  - `carcharodons` / `void_chapter` — *Silent Hunters*'s Carcharodons-from-the-Void register isn't well captured by generic `Adeptus Astartes` + grimdark + galactic-scope; the void-haunted / never-return-to-Imperial-space register is distinct from the chapter-on-homeworld register dominant in prior batches. A `void_chapter` or `outcast_chapter` facet would tighten.
- **Notable surface-form frequencies within this batch:**
  - *Factions (canonical-resolver match, returning):* Adeptus Astartes ×4 (Cawl + Indomitus + Silent Hunters + Ephrael Stern supporting), Adepta Sororitas ×3 primary (Mark of Faith + Ephrael Stern + Requiem Infernal — third authority-layer batch with Sororitas as primary after ssot-w40k-010's *Celestine* and W40K-0091 *Shroud of Night*'s supporting tier; **first time Sororitas is primary across three entries in one batch**), Inquisition ×1 primary (Mark of Faith — Ravara is Ordo Hereticus), Imperium Nihilus ×3 (Cawl mentioned + Mark of Faith primary + Ephrael Stern primary — Imperium-Nihilus continues to be the high-frequency post-Great-Rift setting), Adeptus Mechanicus ×2 (Cawl primary + Brutal Kunnin antagonist), Necrons ×3 (Cawl antagonist + Infinite-and-Divine primary + Indomitus primary — Necrons are the most-tagged xenos faction in this batch), Tyranids ×1 (Cawl antagonist), Chaos ×4 (Honourbound + Requiem Infernal + Rites of Passage + Mark of Faith all have Chaos antagonists), Daemons ×1 (Ephrael Stern antagonist), Drukhari ×1 antagonist (Silent Hunters — post-rename surface form, third authority-layer Drukhari appearance after ssot-w40k-010's *Last Hunt* + *Lukas the Trickster*).

the Bale Stars Crusade is a self-contained crusade theatre distinct from the Sabbat Worlds Crusade in ssot-w40k-003/004 and the Indomitus Crusade in ssot-w40k-010/this batch), **Order of the Last Candle** / **Eternal Candle** (Requiem Infernal — first Hospitaller-anchored Sororitas sub-order), **Scythes of the Emperor** + **Tetrarch Felix** (Cawl — first appearances), **Navis Nobilite** + **House Brobantis** (Rites of Passage — first authority-layer Navis-Nobilite surface form), **Order of Our Martyred Lady** + **Shield of Saint Katherine** (Mark of Faith — first explicit sub-order surface form;   - **`skip-50-stop` activation explicit.** Maintainer's opening prompt contained the literal substring `skip-50-stop` (German-context: "Maintainer-Marker: skip-50-stop (Pre-Check übergehen, Override produzieren)") plus the Brief-071-Vertrag note clarifying that the success-path commits Override + Status-Log together, and the 50er-loud-stop-path commits the Pause-Block alone — line 131 of Brief-061 is the authoritative reading, line 79's "kein Status-Log-Eintrag" wording is superseded. CC chose substring-match (literal `skip-50-stop`) per Brief-061 OQ-1's "liberal substring-matchen, im Status-Log dokumentieren ob ein Skip erkannt wurde" recommendation; matched cleanly, no ambiguity.
  - **Female-POV density is the highest in the authority layer so far.** Five of ten entries have female primary POVs (Severina Raine, Asenath Hyades, Lady Chettamandey, Evangeline + Ravara, Ephrael Stern). Prior batches' female-POV counts: ssot-w40k-001 zero, ssot-w40k-002 zero (Vail is supporting Inquisition liaison only), ssot-w40k-003 zero, ssot-w40k-004 zero, ssot-w40k-005..009 ranging zero-to-one (Anuradha as helot-narrator in ssot-w40k-010's *Spear of the Emperor* is the closest precedent, but Anuradha is a frame-narrator, not the protagonist). The 2019-2020 Black-Library editorial direction (Harrison's Sororitas/Commissar pair + Fehervari's Hospitaller + Brooks's Lady Chettamandey + Annandale's Stern) is qualitatively different from prior decade's male-Astartes-dominant register.
  - **Continued first-appearance density at 110 cumulative.** This batch carries another heavy first-X density: five new Astartes-or-Astartes-adjacent factions as primary protagonist faction (Scythes of the Emperor, Carcharodons, Antari Rifles + Astra-Militarum-Commissar register, Adeptus Mechanicus Cawl-POV, plus the dual Sororitas-sub-order pair), three new xenos primary surface forms (Orks-POV, dual-Necron, Necron-co-primary), six Aeldari sub-faction surface forms (Harlequins + Ynnari + Yvraine + Ynnead + Black Library — five from *Ephrael Stern* — plus Drukhari-as-antagonist from Silent Hunters), four new Imperium-Nihilus / 9th-edition-frame surface forms (Pariah Nexus + Silent Kingdom + Crusade Fleet Quintus + Ithraca's Vengeance), and the first authority-layer entry where the Navis Nobilite (a non-Adeptus-non-xenos non-Chaos Imperial vocation) is primary. Resolver brief — whenever Cowork writes it — will have a third dense surface-form pile to fold in.

The two pre-write training-data corrections (W40K-0103 Cawl's setting being Sotha + verified-absent Trazyn; W40K-0109 Indomitus's Necron POVs being Simut/Ah-hotep/Zozar not Hexmark; W40K-0110 Silent Hunters being Carcharodons not Raven Guard) were caught by the WebSearches and folded into the synopses before commit; no `low_confidence` is needed since the corrections were applied.

  - **W40K-0111 *Volpone Glory* (Kyme, 2021):** Standalone Astra-Militarum Sabbat-Worlds-Crusade entry. Royal-Volpone 50th 'Bluebloods' liberation campaign on Gnostes / Agria island chain vs Blood-Pact. Unlikely-champion + propaganda-as-Imperial-weapon spine. **First authority-layer Volpone-Bluebloods-as-primary-protagonist** (Bluebloods appeared antagonist-tier in *First and Only* in ssot-w40k-003 — Jantine 6th's rival regiment frame — but never POV-tier). **Second authority-layer Sabbat-Worlds-Crusade entry** after the Gaunt's-Ghosts cluster in ssot-w40k-003/004. No specific named POV character surfaced via source coverage — `characters[]` left empty rather than invent one; Brief-061 hallu-discipline holds. No flags.
  - **W40K-0112 *Steel Tread* (Clark, 2021):** Standalone Astra-Militarum tank-crew-POV. Hadeya Etsul commands ancient Leman-Russ Demolisher *Steel Tread* on Croatoas under the Great Rift; dysfunctional-crew + outsider-in-insular-Cadian-regiment + nightmare-haunted-veteran register. Pre-write training-data correction: protagonist is **Hadeya Etsul, NOT Hanna Zhako** (my pre-search mental model had the wrong name; Lexicanum + Unseen Library + Goodreads confirmed Etsul; folded into synopsis before commit). **First authority-layer Astra-Militarum-tank-crew-POV novel + first Hadeya Etsul + Croatoas + named-vehicle *Steel Tread*** (paralleling named-vessel-as-location precedents from ssot-w40k-010 / ssot-w40k-011). No flags.
  - **W40K-0113 *Day of Ascension* (Tchaikovsky, 2022):** Standalone Adeptus-Mechanicus / Genestealer-Cult dual-POV. Forge-world Morod, Genetor Gammat Triskellian's investigation + Genestealer-Cult preparation for the 'union with angels'. Tchaikovsky's first Black-Library work. ~200-page short-novel — `length_tier=short`. **First authority-layer outsider-SF-author entry** (Tchaikovsky's main body of work is *Children of Time* + *Shadows of the Apt*); **first authority-layer entry where Genestealer Cults are the primary protagonist faction** (prior GSC appearances were antagonist-tier in ssot-w40k-002 *For the Emperor* + supporting in ssot-w40k-011 *The Infinite and the Divine*). No flags.
  - **W40K-0114 *The Triumph of Saint Katherine* (Ware, 2022):** Standalone Adepta-Sororitas funerary-procession novel. Sister Avra of Order of Our Martyred Lady joins the six-Sisters-Pronatus procession bearing Saint Katherine's relic across war-zones, defending Kiros against Chaos; six-Saint-embodiment night-of-tales structure. **Twelve first-authority-layer Sororitas surface forms introduced in one book**: Orders Pronatus + Order of the Ebon Chalice + Order of the Argent Shroud + Order of the Bloody Rose + Order of the Sacred Rose + Order of the Valorous Heart + Saint Katherine (in-person Spirit) + Saint Dominica + Saint Silvana + Saint Mina + Saint Arabella + Saint Lucia. Sororitas-Major-Order-vocabulary near-complete after this entry. No flags.
  - **W40K-0115 *Huron Blackheart: Master of the Maelstrom* (Brooks, 2022):** Standalone Chaos-Astartes novel; Huron Blackheart POV. Red Corsairs + Maelstrom + post-Guilliman-renewed-Imperium-pressure + internal-warband-challengers; political-thriller register inside a Chaos warband. Brooks's third authority-layer Chaos-protagonist entry after the Alpha-Legion *Sons of the Hydra* + Death-Guard *Lords of Silence* registers from ssot-w40k-010. **First authority-layer Red-Corsairs-as-primary-protagonist + first Huron Blackheart + Tyrant of Badab + Master-of-the-Maelstrom surface forms**. No flags.
  - **W40K-0116 *Assassinorum: Kingmaker* (Rath, 2022):** Standalone Officio-Assassinorum team-mission. Vindicare-Raithe + Callidus-Sycorax-shapeshifter + Vanus-Avaaris-Koln on Knight-World Dominion; spy-thriller register with three-temple team-dynamic + Knight-suit-bodyguard set-piece. Rath's second authority-layer entry after *The Infinite and the Divine* in ssot-w40k-011. **First authority-layer Officio-Assassinorum team-mission entry + first Vindicare Temple / Callidus Temple / Vanus Temple + Absolom Raithe + Sycorax + Avaaris Koln + House Dominion surface forms**. Protagonist_class `multi` (three different Assassinorum-Temple registers); no `assassin` value in the facet catalog. No flags.
  - **W40K-0117 *Krieg* (Lyons, 2022):** Standalone Death-Korps-of-Krieg novel; twin-storyline structure interleaving the present-day Hive-Arathron siege (Octarius War) with the 1500-year-old Krieg-rebellion / nuclear-self-immolation origin. **First authority-layer Death-Korps-of-Krieg-as-primary-protagonist + first Krieg (planet) + Octarius / Octarius War + Hive Arathron surface forms**. Inquisition-consistency: Inquisitorial observers on-page assessing Korps loyalty — Inquisition listed at supporting role per constraint (no Inquisitor character POV, so supporting not primary). No flags. No specific named Korps POV surfaced via source coverage — `characters[]` left empty rather than invent one (Korps register is collective by design).
  - **W40K-0118 *Catachan Devil* (Woolley, 2022):** Standalone Catachan-Jungle-Fighters novel. Colonel Aldalon's 57th retake Outpost Four on Gondwa VI; three-POV structure with Catachan-veterans + outsider-Skadi-survivor-trial + Ork-kommando-parallel. **First authority-layer Catachan-Jungle-Fighters-as-primary-protagonist + first Catachan 57th + Aldalon + Torvin + Skadi Second Infantry + Gondwa VI + Ork-kommando-POV (Nogrok) surface forms**. Pov_side `dual` (Imperium + Ork). No flags.
  - **W40K-0119 *Helbrecht: Knight of the Throne* (Collins, 2022):** Standalone Black-Templars novel; Marc Collins's debut Black-Library work. Post-Shrine-Worlds-Crusades + post-Rubicon-Primaris Helbrecht penitent-pilgrimage to Hevaran for relic of Rogal Dorn; small-cast journey + character-study; faith / wrath / skill spine. **First authority-layer Black-Templars-as-primary-protagonist + first Helbrecht + Hevaran + Rubicon-Primaris-as-explicit-plot-event + relic-of-Rogal-Dorn surface forms**. No flags.
  - **W40K-0120 *Witchbringer* (Fischer, 2022):** Standalone Astra-Militarum-Primaris-Psyker novel; Steven B. Fischer's debut. Glavia Aerand transitions from Cadian-900th captain to Primaris Psyker via the Scholastica Psykana, sent back to Visage to investigate psychic artefact + missing mentor + treacherous commander. **First authority-layer Astra-Militarum-Primaris-Psyker-POV + first Scholastica Psykana + Glavia Aerand + Cadian 900th + Visage (planet) surface forms**. Protagonist_class `guardsman` (closest available — no `psyker` value in the facet catalog; Aerand is a former Cadian captain whose Psykana sanctioning is mid-book). No flags.
- **value_outside_vocabulary** (candidates surfaced by this batch, none promoted):
  - `assassin` — protagonist_class still has no `assassin` value. Workaround for *Assassinorum: Kingmaker*: `multi` (three different Temple registers — Vindicare + Callidus + Vanus). A dedicated `assassin` value would map the Officio-Assassinorum vocation cleanly; with three Brooks-style standalone Chaos-protagonist novels + dual-Necron-protagonist + Ork-protagonist + Adepta-Sororitas-protagonist + Genestealer-Cult-protagonist all surfaced in the last 30 books, the protagonist_class vocabulary is increasingly stressed.
  - `psyker` / `sanctioned_psyker` — protagonist_class has no `psyker` value. *Witchbringer* workaround used `guardsman` (closest — Aerand is a former Cadian captain). The Scholastica-Psykana vocation is sufficiently distinct that a `psyker` value would map cleanly; same gap as `commissar` / `navigator` / `hospitaller` raised in prior batches.
  - `tank_crew` — *Steel Tread*'s register (entire novel inside one Leman Russ Demolisher's crew compartment) isn't well captured by `guardsman` + planetary-scope + war-story alone. A `vehicle_crew` or `tank_crew` sub-tag would map the close-quarters-crew-procedural register (analogous to the `chapter_serf` / `hospitaller` / `navigator` candidates raised earlier).
  - `cult_pov` / `genestealer_cult_pov` — *Day of Ascension*'s genestealer-cult-from-the-inside register (Brood + faith-in-the-Coming-of-the-Star-Children frame) isn't well captured by `multi` protagonist_class + `xenos` pov_side; the Tchaikovsky-style cult-as-religion register is distinct from prior Chaos-cult registers. A `xenos_cult_pov` or `genestealer_cult` faceted sub-tag would tighten this.
  - `outsider_author` / `crossover_author` — Tchaikovsky's first Black-Library entry is qualitatively different from typical Black-Library house-author entries; the SF-translator-into-40K register (background SF-genre awareness brought into the setting) is a meta-tag worth tracking. Not a synopsis-content tag but a publishing-context tag; flag preserved for value-outside-vocabulary tracking.
  - `pilgrimage` / `penitent_quest` — *Helbrecht* + *Ephrael Stern* (ssot-w40k-011) + *Mark of Faith* (ssot-w40k-011) all anchor in pilgrimage / penitent-quest structures; `journey` is the closest plot_type but doesn't capture the religious-pilgrimage frame distinctly. A `pilgrimage` plot_type would tighten this; would also have applied to *Honour Guard* (ssot-w40k-003) and several others.
  - `tank_register` / `armoured_company` — *Steel Tread* + the Death-Korps-of-Krieg siege register in *Krieg* both lean armoured-warfare; no faceted tag captures the armoured-company / tank-doctrine vocation.
  - `noble_house_succession` — *Volpone Glory* (Royal Volpone noble-officer-caste) + *Assassinorum: Kingmaker* (House Dominion succession) + *Rites of Passage* (House Brobantis succession in ssot-w40k-011) all anchor in Imperial-noble-house succession dynamics; not a court_intrigue subset cleanly, more a faction-shape tag.
  - `funerary_procession` / `relic_carrier` — *The Triumph of Saint Katherine*'s mobile-shrine register (the Triumph itself is both a unit and a ritual-march) isn't well captured by `war_story + journey + character_study` alone. A `procession_register` or `relic_carrier` plot/structure tag would tighten this; analogous to *Honour Guard*'s pilgrim's-way-with-relics register.
  - `outpost_recapture` — *Catachan Devil*'s 'retake Outpost Four' structure is a recurring Astra-Militarum sub-structure not currently tagged; would apply to many regiment-novels.
- **Notable surface-form frequencies within this batch:**
  - *Factions (canonical-resolver match, returning):* Astra Militarum / Imperial Guard ×5 primary (Volpone Glory + Steel Tread + Krieg + Catachan Devil + Witchbringer — five Astra-Militarum sub-genre entries in one batch, the densest such cluster in the authority layer), Adepta Sororitas ×1 primary (Triumph of Saint Katherine — fourth authority-layer Sororitas-primary entry after ssot-w40k-010's *Celestine* + ssot-w40k-011's *Mark of Faith* + *Ephrael Stern* + *Requiem Infernal*), Adeptus Astartes ×2 primary (Huron Blackheart [Heretic-Astartes-tier] + Helbrecht [loyalist-Black-Templars-tier]), Adeptus Mechanicus ×1 primary (Day of Ascension), Officio Assassinorum ×1 primary (Kingmaker), Chaos ×6 antagonist (Volpone Glory + Steel Tread + Triumph + Krieg + Helbrecht + Witchbringer), Inquisition ×1 supporting (Krieg — observers, no on-page Inquisitor POV; constraint doesn't trip), Orks ×2 antagonist (Krieg + Catachan Devil), Tyranids ×1 antagonist (Krieg). Imperial Knights ×1 secondary (Kingmaker — Knight-suit-bodyguard set-piece).
  - *Factions (new surface forms in this batch):* **Volpone Bluebloods** + **Royal Volpone** + **Blood Pact**-as-primary-antagonist ×1 each (Volpone Glory — Volpone-Bluebloods first authority-layer entry as primary protagonist faction; Blood Pact previously surfaced antagonist-tier in Gaunt's Ghosts cluster). **Cadian Shock Troops** primary ×2 (Steel Tread + Witchbringer — first authority-layer entries with Cadian Shock Troops as primary protagonist faction;   - *Characters:* All POV characters in this batch are first-appearance surface forms (none recur from prior batches): Hadeya Etsul (Steel Tread), Gammat Triskellian (Day of Ascension), Sister Avra + Saint Katherine + Saint Dominica + Saint Silvana + Saint Mina + Saint Arabella + Saint Lucia (Triumph — single book introduces seven named-saint character surface forms; the six Matriarchs are Spirit-bearers in-text but listed at supporting role since they are present-as-Spirits not present-as-flesh), Huron Blackheart (Huron Blackheart — series-iconic but first authority-layer POV surface form), Absolom Raithe + Sycorax + Avaaris Koln (Kingmaker — three POVs), Haskell Aldalon ('Hell Fist') + Trooper Torvin + Nogrok (Catachan Devil — three POVs, Imperium + Ork sides), Helbrecht (Helbrecht — series-iconic but first authority-layer POV surface form; Rogal Dorn + Roboute Guilliman mentioned-tier), Glavia Aerand (Witchbringer).
- **Notes:**
  - **First-authority-layer-as-primary-faction density continues.** Six entries this batch introduce a faction as primary-protagonist for the first time in the authority layer: Genestealer Cults (Day of Ascension), Red Corsairs (Huron Blackheart), Officio Assassinorum (Kingmaker — team-mission frame distinct from prior solo-Assassinorum entries), Death Korps of Krieg (Krieg), Catachan Jungle Fighters (Catachan Devil), Black Templars (Helbrecht). Plus the Triumph-of-Saint-Katherine entry's six Sororitas Major-Order surface forms which fill out the Sororitas vocabulary near-completely. Resolver-brief surface-form pile keeps growing.

W40K-0113 *Day of Ascension*'s Mechanicus character is Genetor Gammat Triskellian (Lexicanum + Black-Library product page confirmed). All three caught by WebSearch + folded into the synopsis before commit; no `low_confidence` flags needed since corrections were applied.
  - **No `data_conflict` flags this iteration.** All ten roster entries are standard novel-length per Black Library + Lexicanum + publisher-product-pages. *Day of Ascension* at ~200 pages is on the short end (`length_tier=short` rather than `standard`), but the SSOT format=`novel` is correct per all sources; no flag needed.
  - **No `low_confidence` flags this iteration.** All ten entries have strong 2021-2022 Black-Library coverage: Lexicanum + Track-of-Words + Unseen Library + At Boundary's Edge + Goonhammer + Grimdark Magazine + WH40k Book Club + Warhammer-Community + publisher product pages + author Rapid-Fire interviews.
  - **Inquisition-consistency constraint** (Brief 061): triggered cleanly for zero entries this batch. W40K-0117 *Krieg* has Inquisitorial observers on-page but no Inquisitor POV-character; Inquisition listed at supporting role (constraint doesn't trip without an Inquisitor character POV). W40K-0102 *Requiem Infernal* precedent from ssot-w40k-011 applies here.
  - **Astra-Militarum-cluster density.** Five of ten entries are Astra-Militarum primary (Volpone Glory + Steel Tread + Krieg + Catachan Devil + Witchbringer), making this batch the densest Astra-Militarum-sub-genre cluster in the authority layer. The 2021-2022 Black-Library editorial direction visibly pushed Astra-Militarum standalones across multiple regimental registers (Volpone / Cadian-tank / Death-Korps / Catachan / Cadian-Primaris-Psyker). Female-POV density is mid-tier this batch (3 of 10: Hadeya Etsul + Sister Avra + Glavia Aerand) — well below ssot-w40k-011's 5-of-10 high-water mark but maintaining 30%+ female-POV continuity.
  - **Outsider-author entry.** W40K-0113 *Day of Ascension* is Adrian Tchaikovsky's first Black-Library work — Tchaikovsky is best known for *Children of Time* (Arthur C. Clarke Award winner) and *Shadows of the Apt*. The SF-translator-into-40K register (background SF-genre awareness brought into the setting, particularly the cult-as-religion frame from a non-grimdark-house perspective) is qualitatively distinct from typical Black-Library house-author entries; flagged in `value_outside_vocabulary` as a publishing-context-tag candidate.
  - **Surface-form treue compliance.** "Astra Militarum" used over "Imperial Guard" as the primary surface form across all five Astra-Militarum entries (Volpone Glory + Steel Tread + Krieg + Catachan Devil + Witchbringer — all 2021-2022 publication-era, firmly post-rename); "Imperial Guard" also tagged as parallel surface form per ssot-w40k-011 precedent (the four post-rename entries there double-tagged both). "Adepta Sororitas" + named Major-Orders (Our Martyred Lady / Ebon Chalice / Argent Shroud / Bloody Rose / Sacred Rose / Valorous Heart) all use canonical Black-Library forms. "Red Corsairs" + "Heretic Astartes" + "Black Templars" + "Death Korps of Krieg" + "Catachan Jungle Fighters" + "Scholastica Psykana" all canonical. "Officio Assassinorum" + "Vindicare Temple" + "Callidus Temple" + "Vanus Temple" canonical Black-Library forms (vs colloquial "Vindicares" etc which would appear in dialogue but not in the authority-layer factions list). "Huron Blackheart" + "Tyrant of Badab" + "Master of the Maelstrom" all canonical. "Rubicon Primaris" + "Primaris Psyker" + "Shrine-Worlds Crusades" canonical Black-Library forms.
  - **Synopsis-length elasticity.** Range 1165–1660 chars; eight of ten sit at or above the 1200-char soft cap.
