*Da Big Dakka* is the actual Ufthak sequel; *Warboss* has a separate multi-clan-succession cast**), W40K-0129 *Pilgrims of Fire* (confirm Justin-D-Hill-author + Order-of-Our-Martyred-Lady + Fleet-Quintus-'Cursed-Fleet'-Indomitus-Crusade + dual-timeline-bracketing-Cicatrix-Maledictum + Helewise-Sister-Superior + ancient-pilgrimage-route + Saint-Katherine-step-retracing + Cion-shrine-world + Sister-Repentia-arc + Arco-flagellants + Penitent-Engines on-page via Black-Library product page + Simon-&-Schuster + Warhammer-Community-Hill-interview + Amazon + At-Boundary's-Edge + Goodreads), W40K-0130 *The Lion: Son of the Forest* (confirm Mike-Brooks-author + Lion-El'Jonson-awakens-in-forest-with-no-memory + ten-thousand-years-in-Warp-stasis + Caliban-fragments-out-of-Warp + Fallen-Angels-as-redeemable-allies + Zabriel-Chaos-warband-traitor + Watchers-in-the-Dark + Lord-of-Shadowed-Paths + Guilliman-revelation-at-novel-close via Lexicanum + Goodreads + TV-Tropes + Fluffenhammer + Warhammer-Community + Simon-&-Schuster + Black-Library product page + Fandom — **roster-title-mismatch confirmed: canonical title is *Son of the Forest* (singular), roster has *Sons of the Forest* (plural); `data_conflict` flag set with field=title, suggestion='The Lion: Son of the Forest'**).
- **Per-book bullets:**
  - **W40K-0121 *Outgunned* (Flowers, 2022):** Standalone Aeronautica-Imperialis dual-POV. Flight-Commander Lucille von Shard (arrogant misanthropic fighter ace) + Propagandist Kile Simlex (sent to film her as Imperial hero) on Bacchus vs Orks. Propaganda-machine-cynicism is the load-bearing spine; aerial-combat-attrition is the action register. **First authority-layer Aeronautica-Imperialis-as-primary-protagonist + first Lucille von Shard + first Kile Simlex + first Bacchus surface forms**. Training-data correction caught: Bacchus war is anti-Ork, not anti-Tau (Unseen Library + Simon-&-Schuster + At-Boundary's-Edge confirmed Orks; my pre-search model wrongly held Tau; folded into synopsis pre-write). No flags.
  - **W40K-0122 *Awakenings* (Mann, 2022):** Standalone Inquisition novel. Inquisitor Astor Sabbathiel awakens in an Ecclesiarchy stronghold a hundred years after being shot-and-warp-stormed-into-stasis in the Calaphrax Cluster, owing her resurrection to Magos Metik; summoned to Hulth by Ordo-Hereticus Inquisitor Heldren and pulled into a conspiracy involving corrupt Inquisitors + Navigator Houses + the Custodes. Slow-burn mystery + political-thriller register. **First authority-layer Inquisitor-Astor-Sabbathiel-POV + first authority-layer Ordo-Hereticus-as-primary-protagonist + first authority-layer single-named-Inquisitor-as-primary-POV-novel + first Magos Metik + first Inquisitor Heldren + first Calaphrax Cluster + first Hulth + first Custodes-as-conspiracy-target surface forms**. **Major training-data correction caught**: Awakenings is an Inquisition novel, NOT a Dark-Angels-Lazarus-from-coma novel (Lexicanum + At-Boundary's-Edge + Simon-&-Schuster confirmed Sabbathiel; my pre-search mental model wrongly held the Dark-Angels frame; folded into synopsis pre-write). No flags.
  - **W40K-0123 *Shadowsun: The Patient Hunter* (Kelly, 2022):** Standalone T'au-Empire-primary novel. Commander Shadowsun in the Chalnath Expanse + Fourth-Sphere-Expansion vs a Death-Guard armada whose ancient warp-tearing tech and daemonic patrons defy the logical Tau worldview; surprise Startide-Nexus attack + civil-war pressure among Tau-allies. **First authority-layer T'au-Empire-as-primary-protagonist + first Commander-Shadowsun-POV + first Kauyon-doctrine + first Mont'ka-counter-doctrine + first Chalnath-Expanse + first Fourth-Sphere-Expansion + first Startide-Nexus + first Death-Guard-as-Tau-antagonist surface forms**. Training-data correction caught: Shadowsun's antagonist here is Chaos (Death Guard), NOT residual Damocles-Crusade Imperial forces; folded into synopsis pre-write. No flags.
  - **W40K-0124 *Void King* (Collins, 2022):** Standalone Rogue-Traders novel — the first true Rogue-Trader-as-primary Black-Library entry in a long time, with the Davamir Compact (Proud Lamertine + Fierce Helvintr + Cunning Radrexxus) tasked by Guilliman with finding a Rift-crossing route during the Indomitus Crusade; Erastus Lamertine heir rises through tragedy-and-betrayal. Court-intrigue + political-thriller + journey register. **First authority-layer Rogue-Traders-as-primary-protagonist + first Davamir Compact + first House Lamertine + first House Helvintr + first House Radrexxus + first Erastus Lamertine surface forms + first 'modern-timeline-Rogue-Trader' frame**. **MAJOR training-data correction caught**: Void King is a Rogue-Traders novel, NOT an Imperial-Knights / House-Tan-Draconis novel (Lexicanum + At-Boundary's-Edge + Black-Library product page + Simon-&-Schuster + Goodreads + Marc-Collins-author-page all confirmed Rogue Traders + Davamir Compact; my pre-search mental model wrongly held an Imperial-Knights frame; folded into synopsis pre-write). No flags. Cowork-relevant note: this is the densest single training-data correction in the batch and a useful precedent for the resolver-brief on author-debut-attribution.
  - **W40K-0125 *Kasrkin* (Albert, 2022):** Standalone Astra-Militarum Kasrkin novel. Captain Bharath Obeysekera + squad on Dasht i-Kevar recover a downed Astra-Militarum-general from the deep desert; T'au-Empire-pressed war + Kroot-kinband-under-Shaper-Tchek-pursuit + ancient-buried-entity in the dunes. ~400-page register flagged as `doorstopper`. **First authority-layer Kasrkin-as-primary-protagonist + first Bharath Obeysekera + first Dasht i-Kevar + first Shaper Tchek + first Kroot-kinband-on-page-antagonist surface forms**. The Kasrkin frame is a Cadian-elite-derivative distinct from the broader Cadian Shock Troops surface form already in the authority layer (ssot-w40k-012's Steel Tread + Witchbringer). No flags.
  - **W40K-0126 *Wrath of the Lost* (Forrester, 2023):** Standalone Flesh-Tearers novel. Chapter Master Gabriel Seth dispatches Chaplain Dumah + Apothecary Barachiel back to silent-garrison Cretacia post-Primaris-influx; the brothers must battle Chaos AND the eponymous Wrath-of-the-Lost gene-curse (Flesh-Tearers' homegrown Blood-Angels-curse analogue). Character-study + war-story + journey-home register; the Chaplain's spiritual-stewardship and the Apothecary's gene-seed-stewardship are the dual spines. **First authority-layer Flesh-Tearers-as-primary-protagonist + first Gabriel Seth + first Chaplain Dumah + first Apothecary Barachiel + first Cretacia + first 'Wrath of the Lost'-as-Flesh-Tearer-gene-curse surface forms**; first authority-layer Blood-Angels-successor-Chapter-curse register; second authority-layer Primaris-integration-as-plot-event after ssot-w40k-012's Helbrecht. No flags.
  - **W40K-0127 *Angron: The Red Angel* (Guymer, 2023):** Standalone Daemon-Primarch novel. Angron returns to Imperium Nihilus + lights a beacon for his scattered XII Legion; three interleaved POV strands — Kossolax-the-Foresworn lord-regent aboard the World-Eaters flagship, Ortan-Leidis-of-Angels-of-the-Grail marooned on a worthless moon, and Grey-Knight Graucis-Telomane executing six-centuries-in-the-making plans to eradicate Angron. Dense Primarch-psychology + Legion-politics + Grey-Knight-counter-strike register. **First authority-layer Daemon-Primarch-Angron-POV + first authority-layer World-Eaters-as-primary-protagonist + first Kossolax the Foresworn + first Ortan Leidis + first Angels-of-the-Grail-warband + first Graucis Telomane surface forms + second-authority-layer Grey-Knights entry after *The Emperor's Gift* (ssot-w40k-008)**. POV_side `dual` (chaos + imperium). No flags.
  - **W40K-0128 *Warboss* (Brooks, 2023):** Standalone Ork-clan-succession-thriller ensemble. Warboss Gazrot Goresnappa dies under a decapitated Gargant-head; Da-Genrul (Blood Axes), Speedboss Zagnob Thundaskuzz (Evil Sunz), Big-Boss Mag Dedfist (Goffs), and Snaggi-Littletoof (grot uprising) all race for a prophesied gate beneath a human city that the one-true-Warboss will use to turn the galaxy green. Satirical + war-story + political-thriller register from inside the greenskin perspective. **First authority-layer Blood-Axes + Evil-Sunz + Goffs-as-primary-clan + Grot-uprising-as-primary-faction surface forms + first Gazrot Goresnappa (mentioned-dead) + Da Genrul + Zagnob Thundaskuzz + Mag Dedfist + Snaggi Littletoof + Gretchin-revolutionary-frame surface forms**. **Training-data correction caught**: *Warboss* is NOT a direct sequel to *Brutal Kunnin* (Ufthak Blackhawk does not appear); *Da Big Dakka* is the actual Ufthak sequel (Warhammer-Community + At-Boundary's-Edge + Black-Library product page confirmed; my pre-search mental model wrongly conflated *Warboss* with the Ufthak-sequel slot; folded into synopsis pre-write). Brooks's second authority-layer Ork-novel after *Brutal Kunnin* (ssot-w40k-011) but with a separate cast. Protagonist_gender `ensemble` (no single primary Ork-POV among the four claimants). No flags.
  - **W40K-0129 *Pilgrims of Fire* (Hill, 2023):** Standalone Adepta-Sororitas novel — third-consecutive-batch Sororitas-primary entry. Order of Our Martyred Lady Sister-Helewise leads Sisters aboard the Indomitus-Crusade's Fleet-Quintus 'Cursed Fleet'; dual-timeline structure bracketing the Cicatrix-Maledictum arrival; pilgrimage retracing Saint Katherine's ancient route to liberate the shrine-world Cion in the daemon-infested sectors beyond the Cicatrix; Sister-Repentia arc as spiritual spine + Arco-flagellants + Penitent Engines on-page. **First authority-layer Helewise + Cion + Sisters-Repentia-as-on-page-arc + Arco-flagellants-on-page + Penitent-Engines-on-page surface forms + second authority-layer Fleet-Quintus surface form** (after *Indomitus* in ssot-w40k-011 — same Crusade fleet, cross-reference); third authority-layer Order-of-Our-Martyred-Lady appearance. No flags.
  - **W40K-0130 *The Lion: Son of the Forest* (Brooks, 2023):** Standalone Lion-El'Jonson novel — second authority-layer Primarch-resurrection event after Roboute Guilliman. Lion awakens in a vast forest with no memory + ten-thousand-years-in-Warp-stasis + Caliban-fragments-out-of-Warp; Fallen Angels nearby (some redeemable, some lost-to-Chaos including Zabriel-as-Chaos-warband-leader); Watchers-in-the-Dark intercede; Guilliman-revelation at novel close. Journey-of-self-rediscovery in Caliban-mythic register. **First authority-layer Lion-El'Jonson-POV + first Caliban-in-the-Warp / Forest-Caliban + first Zabriel + first Watchers-in-the-Dark + first Fallen-Angels-as-on-page-cast + first 'Lord of Shadowed Paths' surface forms + first authority-layer Primarch-resurrection-as-plot-event for the I Legion**. **`data_conflict` flag set**: roster lists *The Lion: Sons of the Forest* (plural) but canonical title across Black-Library + Lexicanum + Simon-&-Schuster + Goodreads + Warhammer-Community + Fluffenhammer + TV-Tropes is *The Lion: Son of the Forest* (singular); roster-mistag-cleanup deferred to Maintainer Excel-SSOT workflow; book stays in this batch to keep the slot covered.
- **value_outside_vocabulary** (candidates surfaced by this batch, none promoted):
  - `aerial_combat` / `fighter_pilot` / `aeronautica` — same gap raised by *Double Eagle* (ssot-w40k-009) revives here for *Outgunned*. Aerial-combat-attrition + fighter-ace register is still not well captured by `war_story + action_heavy`; protagonist_class has no `pilot` value. Workaround used: `multi` (dual Shard-pilot + Simlex-propagandist register) + planetary scope. A dedicated `pilot` or `aeronautica` sub-tag would clarify the cockpit-as-stage register.
  - `propagandist` / `imperial_propaganda` — *Outgunned*'s propaganda-machine-as-load-bearing-spine is a register that has now surfaced multiple times (Volpone Glory ssot-w40k-012 + Outgunned here); a `propaganda` or `propagandist` plot/protagonist-class value would map cleanly.
  - `rogue_trader` — protagonist_class has no `rogue_trader` value. *Void King* workaround: `civilian` (Erastus Lamertine is technically civilian-but-empowered-with-Warrant-of-Trade). A `rogue_trader` value would map a recurring 40K-protagonist archetype that the catalog doesn't currently capture distinctly from generic civilian.
  - `primarch` — protagonist_class has no `primarch` value. *Angron* + *The Lion* both workaround with `space_marine`, which loses the Primarch-distinct register. With Primarch-resurrection events accelerating (Guilliman in the Cawl trilogy + Lion here + Mortarion in HH books + Magnus in HH + Angron-as-Daemon-Primarch here + future Lion / Lion / Sanguinor returns presumably coming), a `primarch` value is increasingly load-bearing.
  - `daemon_primarch` — sub-value of `primarch` for the chaos-side; *Angron* is the first authority-layer Daemon-Primarch-POV. Currently maps to `space_marine + chaos pov_side` which loses the daemon-incarnation-as-protagonist register.
  - `inquisitor_pov` granularity — *Awakenings* is the first authority-layer single-named-Inquisitor-as-primary-POV-novel. `inquisitor` exists in protagonist_class but the catalog doesn't distinguish Ordo-Hereticus / Ordo-Malleus / Ordo-Xenos-flavored Inquisitor protagonists. A sub-tag (`inquisitor_hereticus` / `inquisitor_malleus` / `inquisitor_xenos`) would tighten this.
  - `gretchin` / `grot_uprising` / `xenos_clan_war` — *Warboss*'s grot-uprising-leader register isn't well captured by `pc_xenos`; a `gretchin` sub-tag would distinguish grot-protagonists from Ork-protagonists.
  - `kasrkin` / `cadian_elite` — Kasrkin is an Astra-Militarum-elite-sub-formation register distinct from generic Cadian Shock Troops; a faction-shape sub-tag would tighten the gap (analogous to the Officio-Assassinorum-Temples gap raised in ssot-w40k-012).
  - `pilgrimage` / `penitent_quest` — same gap raised in ssot-w40k-012 (*Helbrecht*) revives for *Pilgrims of Fire*; Hill's pilgrimage-as-load-bearing-spine register would map cleanly to a `pilgrimage` plot_type.
  - `primarch_resurrection` / `primarch_return` — *The Lion* is the second authority-layer Primarch-resurrection-as-plot-event (after the Cawl-trilogy Guilliman-return). A plot-event-tag would map this recurring 40K-meta-plot-frame distinctly from generic `journey + character_study`.
  - `gene_curse` / `chapter_curse` / `genetic_madness` — Flesh-Tearers' Wrath-of-the-Lost + Blood-Angels' Black-Rage + Red-Thirst + Space-Wolves' Wulfen-curse + World-Eaters' Butcher's-Nails are all gene-curse / chapter-curse registers that recur across many Astartes novels. A `chapter_curse` theme-tag would tighten this.
  - `multi_clan_war` / `succession_crisis` — *Warboss*'s six-clan succession-thriller register isn't quite captured by `political_thriller`; an `intra_faction_war` or `succession_crisis` plot_type would tighten this.
- **Notable surface-form frequencies within this batch:**
  - *Factions (canonical-resolver match, returning):* Imperium ×10 primary (every entry, expected); Adeptus Astartes / Space Marines ×3 primary (Flesh Tearers + Angron-multi-Astartes + Lion-Dark-Angels); Astra Militarum / Imperial Guard ×2 primary (Outgunned-Aeronautica-Imperialis-Navy-derivative + Kasrkin); Chaos ×6 antagonist (Shadowsun + Void King + Wrath of the Lost + Angron-primary + Pilgrims of Fire + The Lion); Adepta Sororitas / Sisters of Battle ×1 primary (Pilgrims of Fire — third consecutive batch with a Sororitas-primary entry); Inquisition ×1 primary (Awakenings — first authority-layer single-Inquisitor-POV-primary); T'au Empire / Tau Empire ×2 (Shadowsun-primary + Kasrkin-antagonist); Heretic Astartes ×3 (Shadowsun-antagonist-Death-Guard + Angron-World-Eaters-primary + The Lion-antagonist-warband); Grey Knights ×1 primary (Angron — second authority-layer entry after *The Emperor's Gift* ssot-w40k-008); Orks ×2 (Outgunned-antagonist + Warboss-primary); Indomitus Crusade ×2 secondary (Void King + Pilgrims of Fire).
  - *Factions (new surface forms in this batch):* **Aeronautica Imperialis** primary ×1 (Outgunned — first authority-layer entry as primary protagonist faction; Imperial-Navy-aviation-arm distinct from Imperial-Navy-ship-arm). **Ordo Hereticus** primary ×1 (Awakenings — first authority-layer single-Inquisitor-POV-primary; Ordo-Hereticus appeared as parent-tier in ssot-w40k-009/011 but not as on-page-primary). **T'au Empire / Tau Empire / Fire Caste** primary ×1 each (Shadowsun — first authority-layer entry as primary protagonist faction; previous Tau appearances were antagonist-tier in ssot-w40k-008-010). **Death Guard** antagonist ×1 (Shadowsun — second authority-layer Death-Guard appearance after ssot-w40k-010's *Lords of Silence* but first as Tau-antagonist). **Rogue Traders** + **Davamir Compact** + **House Lamertine** + **House Helvintr** + **House Radrexxus** primary ×1 each (Void King — five first authority-layer Rogue-Trader surface forms in one entry; first authority-layer Rogue-Traders-as-primary-protagonist + first Indomitus-Crusade-Rogue-Trader-tasking frame). **Kasrkin** primary ×1 (Kasrkin — first authority-layer entry as primary protagonist sub-formation; distinct from generic Cadian Shock Troops surface form). **Kroot** antagonist ×1 (Kasrkin — first authority-layer Kroot-on-page-antagonist; Kroot appeared as Tau-allies-mentioned in prior entries but never as on-page-antagonist kinband). **Flesh Tearers** primary ×1 (Wrath of the Lost — first authority-layer entry as primary protagonist faction; Blood-Angels-successor-chapter register distinct from prior Blood-Angels-primary appearances in ssot-w40k-006 *Devastation of Baal* + ssot-w40k-009 cluster). **World Eaters** + **Khorne** primary ×1 each (Angron — first authority-layer World-Eaters-as-primary-protagonist + first explicit Khorne-as-primary-faction). **Angels of the Grail** primary ×1 (Angron — first authority-layer Chaos-warband surface form). **Blood Axes** + **Evil Sunz** + **Goffs** + **Gretchin** primary ×1 each (Warboss — four first authority-layer Ork-clan-as-primary surface forms; Goffs previously surfaced supporting-tier in ssot-w40k-011 *Brutal Kunnin* but is primary here). **Sisters Repentia** + **Arco-flagellants** + **Penitent Engines** primary/supporting ×1 each (Pilgrims of Fire — three first authority-layer Sororitas-substructure surface forms). **Order of Our Martyred Lady** primary ×1 (Pilgrims of Fire — third authority-layer appearance after ssot-w40k-011 *Mark of Faith* + ssot-w40k-012 *Triumph of Saint Katherine*; resolves into a stable canonical-resolver-target). **Dark Angels** + **Fallen Angels** + **Watchers in the Dark** primary/supporting ×1 each (The Lion — first authority-layer Dark-Angels-as-primary-protagonist + first authority-layer Fallen-Angels-as-on-page-cast + first authority-layer Watchers-in-the-Dark surface forms).
  - *Locations:* Bacchus ×1 (Outgunned — first), Calaphrax Cluster ×1 + Hulth ×1 (Awakenings — two firsts), Chalnath Expanse ×1 + Fourth Sphere Expansion ×1 + Startide Nexus ×1 + Great Rift ×3 secondary (Shadowsun three firsts + Great-Rift returning in Void King + The Lion + Shadowsun), Davamir Compact ×1 (Void King — first; doubles as both a faction-and-location surface form for the dynastic-territory frame), Dasht i-Kevar ×1 (Kasrkin — first), Cretacia ×1 (Wrath of the Lost — first), Imperium Nihilus ×3 (Angron-primary + Pilgrims-of-Fire-secondary + The-Lion-secondary; sixth-through-eighth authority-layer Imperium-Nihilus-frame appearances), Cion ×1 + Fleet Quintus ×1 + Cicatrix Maledictum ×1 (Pilgrims of Fire — three firsts; Fleet-Quintus second authority-layer appearance after *Indomitus* in ssot-w40k-011), Caliban ×1 (The Lion — first authority-layer appearance; the Caliban-in-the-Warp / Forest-Caliban register is distinct from the canonical-Caliban-destroyed-in-Heresy register, but the surface form is `Caliban`). Total: 13 first-appearance locations + 4 returning-location appearances; **Imperium-Nihilus-frame revives** this batch (3 of 10 vs ssot-w40k-012's 1 of 10), consistent with the 2022-2023 cluster's post-Cicatrix / Indomitus-Crusade density.
  - *Characters:* All POV characters in this batch are first-appearance surface forms (none recur from prior batches): Lucille von Shard + Kile Simlex (Outgunned), Astor Sabbathiel + Metik + Heldren (Awakenings), Shadowsun / O'Shaserra (Shadowsun — two parallel surface forms for the same character), Erastus Lamertine (Void King), Bharath Obeysekera + Tchek (Kasrkin), Gabriel Seth + Dumah + Barachiel (Wrath of the Lost), Angron + Kossolax the Foresworn + Ortan Leidis + Graucis Telomane (Angron — four POV characters), Gazrot Goresnappa (mentioned-dead) + Da Genrul + Zagnob Thundaskuzz + Mag Dedfist + Snaggi Littletoof (Warboss — five Ork-clan-claimants), Helewise + Saint Katherine (mentioned) (Pilgrims of Fire), Lion El'Jonson + Zabriel + Roboute Guilliman (mentioned) (The Lion). **Roboute Guilliman** appears mentioned-tier in three entries this batch (Void King + Wrath of the Lost + The Lion) — third authority-layer batch with Guilliman as mentioned-tier ambient-presence, consistent with his post-Cawl-trilogy-Imperium-Regent status.
- **Notes:**
  - **First-authority-layer-as-primary-faction density peaks.** Eight entries this batch introduce a faction as primary-protagonist for the first time in the authority layer: Aeronautica Imperialis (Outgunned), Ordo Hereticus / Inquisition-primary (Awakenings), T'au Empire (Shadowsun), Rogue Traders / Davamir Compact (Void King), Kasrkin (Kasrkin), Flesh Tearers (Wrath of the Lost), World Eaters / Daemon-Primarch-Angron (Angron), and the Dark-Angels / Fallen-Angels / Watchers-in-the-Dark / Lion-El'Jonson-as-Primarch (The Lion). **Densest first-authority-layer-as-primary-faction-debut count of any batch so far** — surpasses ssot-w40k-012's six-debut count. Plus first authority-layer Daemon-Primarch-POV (Angron) and first authority-layer Primarch-resurrection-as-plot-event for the I Legion (The Lion).
  - **Four pre-write training-data corrections caught and folded into synopses.** W40K-0121 *Outgunned* — antagonist is Orks, NOT Tau (Unseen Library + Simon-&-Schuster + At-Boundary's-Edge); W40K-0122 *Awakenings* — Inquisition / Astor Sabbathiel novel, NOT Dark-Angels-Lazarus-from-coma (Lexicanum + At-Boundary's-Edge + Simon-&-Schuster); W40K-0124 *Void King* — Rogue-Traders / Davamir Compact, NOT Imperial-Knights / House-Tan-Draconis (Lexicanum + At-Boundary's-Edge + Black-Library + Simon-&-Schuster + Goodreads + Marc-Collins-author-page); W40K-0128 *Warboss* — multi-clan-succession-thriller distinct from the Ufthak-Blackhawk register, NOT a direct *Brutal Kunnin* sequel (*Da Big Dakka* is the actual Ufthak sequel; Warhammer-Community + At-Boundary's-Edge + Black-Library product page confirmed). All four were caught by WebSearch + folded into the synopsis pre-commit; no `low_confidence` flags needed since corrections were applied. **Densest training-data-correction batch so far** — the 2022-2023 release cluster is the period where my training data is thinnest (publication-year coincides with the model-knowledge-cutoff frontier), and the WebSearch-pass caught all four cleanly.
  - **One `data_conflict` flag this iteration**: W40K-0130 *The Lion: Son of the Forest* — roster title is *Sons of the Forest* (plural), canonical title is *Son of the Forest* (singular). Flag set with field=title, suggestion='The Lion: Son of the Forest'. Roster-mistag-cleanup deferred to Maintainer Excel-SSOT workflow per Brief-061 roster-fehleintrag convention. Ursarkar E. Creed last stand. **First authority-layer Fall-of-Cadia-structural-event-novel + Ursarkar-E.-Creed-POV + 13th-Black-Crusade-on-page + Abaddon-as-on-page-antagonist**. "Lord Castellan", "Avenging Son", "Cicatrix Maledictum", "Indomitus Crusade", "Cadian Gate", "Eye of Terror", "Daemon-Primarch", "Pater Mutatis", "Phoenician", "13th Black Crusade" all canonical Black-Library forms.
  - **Synopsis-length elasticity.** Range 1766–2264 chars; all ten entries above the 1200-char soft cap; median ~1947. Higher floor than ssot-w40k-013 (1766 vs 1682), driven by three cross-batch-character-continuity-sequel entries that needed both the new-entry context + the prior-entry cross-reference fitted into one synopsis (Above and Beyond's Outgunned-aftermath frame + Interceptor City's 20-year-post-Enothis frame + Genefather's Great-Work-Pylon-network frame each adds ~300-400 chars of cross-reference scaffolding); plus *Fall of Cadia*'s structural-event-novel-as-multi-POV-ensemble register which absorbs an unusually-large faction roster into one synopsis (4 Imperium-side primaries + 4 Chaos-side antagonists + Eye-of-Terror + Cadian Gate + Cicatrix-Maledictum-genesis).
  - **Resolver-Pre-Note (deferred):** kumulativ ist nach diesem Batch 140. **Die nächste natürliche Resolver-Pause ist bei `cumulativeBefore=150`** (`ssot-w40k-015`, W40K-0141..W40K-0150 — eine Iteration weiter). Cowork-Tendenz aus Brief 061 + früheren Resolver-Pässen: **Resolver-Brief jetzt schreiben oder spätestens bei der nächsten Iteration aktivieren** — Surface-Form-Pile + Authority-Layer-internal-character-continuity-Pile sind beide weiter gewachsen. Aktuelle Pile seit dem ersten Resolver-Pass in 069: ssot-w40k-006..014 = 90 Bücher mit ~170-190 new factions / locations / characters einschließlich diesem Batch's three-faction-debut + twelve-first-appearance-locations + ten-plus-character-debut + drei-cross-batch-character-returns. Wenn Maintainer den Resolver weiterhin verschiebt: nächste natural-stop bei cumulative=150 (eine Iteration weiter).
  - **Brief-071-Vertrag aktiv:** Override-Datei + Status-Log-Append in einem Commit ohne Co-Author-Trailer, keine sonstigen Datei-Edits. Lint/typecheck/brain-lint nicht gelaufen — data-only commit (eine JSON + ein Markdown-Append), keine Code-/Brain-Page-Änderungen, alle drei Lint-Targets nicht betroffen. Per Brief-061-Klausel akzeptabel.

## 2026-05-15 · ssot-w40k-015 · W40K-0141..W40K-0150 · ✅

- **Cumulative books in authority:** 150 / 150 to next resolver pause (140 before this batch + 10 written here) — **next iteration triggers the natural Resolver-Pause-window at cumulative=150 → loud-stop unless `skip-50-stop` marker is set**.
- **CC model:** claude-opus-4-7
- **Pre-check:** Detected existing `manual-overrides-ssot-w40k-001..014.json` (14 files × 10 books = 140 books). W40K max = 14, HH max = 0, cumulative = 140, 140 % 50 = 40 ≠ 0 → no resolver pause. No `skip-50-stop` marker in maintainer prompt (Brief-071-Vertrag governs commit-mechanics, not pre-check). Next batch: `ssot-w40k-015`, slice = W40K-0141..W40K-0150 (10er — unusually-split temporal cluster: seven 2025-2026 publication-frontier releases + the founding Ian-Watson Inquisition-War trilogy 1990-1995).
- **WebSearch:** mean = 1.0 / book, max = 1 (over 10 books). 10 total searches — one obligatory plot-context search per book, no follow-up searches needed thanks to strong coverage across Black-Library + Lexicanum + Goonhammer + At-Boundary's-Edge + Warhammer-Community + Frontline-Gaming + Simon-&-Schuster + Goodreads + Wikipedia + Ian-Watson's-author-site + Noble Knight Games + Gamescape + warmodels.co.uk + Fandom-Warhammer40k-wiki. Lowest mean-WebSearch-count of any iteration so far (ties ssot-w40k-013 and ssot-w40k-014 floor; the founding-Watson-trilogy is well-documented in the secondary-source ecosystem despite being a 30-35-year-old publication-corner, and the 2025-2026 releases are all in current Black-Library product-page coverage).
- **Per-book bullets:**
  - **W40K-0141 *Voidscarred* (Mike Brooks, 2025):** Aeldari-Corsairs novel. Baron Myrin Stormdawn of the Starsplinters allies with exiled Craftworld admiral Taenar Leotharan vs Ork Freebooters. **First authority-layer Aeldari-Corsairs-as-primary-protagonist + Starsplinters + Myrin-Stormdawn + Taenar-Leotharan**. Fourth Mike-Brooks authority-layer entry (after *Rites of Passage* ssot-w40k-011 + *Huron Blackheart* ssot-w40k-012 + *Warboss* ssot-w40k-013). `data_conflict` flag for missing roster author.
  - **W40K-0142 *Tomb World* (Jonathan D. Beer, 2025):** Necron-primary novel. Triarch-Praetorian Khemet, betrayed and imprisoned, dispatched by Necron-Lord Hekasun to awaken tomb-world Orymous (paved over by Astra Militarum). Female-primary-POV. **First authority-layer Triarch-Praetorian-as-primary-POV + Khemet + Hekasun + Orymous**. Second authority-layer Necron-primary appearance after *Indomitus* ssot-w40k-011 but first as single-POV-female-Praetorian. `data_conflict` flag for missing roster author.
  - **W40K-0143 *Vagabond Squadron* (Robbie MacNiven, 2025):** Aeronautica-Imperialis novel. 901st Tactical Wing Valkyrie-squadron on Kanai Tertius vs Orks, with novice-aviator-and-veterans dynamic. **First authority-layer 901st Tactical Wing + Kanai Tertius + Valkyrie-Aeronautica-Imperialis-squadron-as-primary register**. Third authority-layer Aeronautica-Imperialis-as-primary-protagonist entry after ssot-w40k-013 *Outgunned* + ssot-w40k-014 *Above and Beyond* / *Interceptor City* — but first against Orks-as-primary-antagonist (vs prior Chaos / Tau / mixed-secondary-Ork). `data_conflict` flag for missing roster author.
  - **W40K-0144 *Archmagos* (Guy Haley, 2025):** Adeptus-Mechanicus novel — **third book of the canonical Belisarius-Cawl trilogy**. Cawl + retinue cross to a Necron tomb-world trapped on the event horizon of a Black Hole to retrieve control codes for Attilan-Gap-stabilisation. **First authority-layer Attilan Gap + Black-Hole-event-horizon-Necron-tomb-world setting**. Third Belisarius-Cawl appearance — **completes the canonical Cawl-trilogy in the authority layer** (after *The Great Work* ssot-w40k-011 + *Genefather* ssot-w40k-014); first such completed-trilogy-arc milestone. Clean, no flags.
  - **W40K-0145 *Demolisher* (Andy Clark, 2025):** Astra-Militarum-tank-warfare novel — **direct sequel to *Steel Tread* (ssot-w40k-012)**. Hadeya Etsul's Leman-Russ-Demolisher crew on Croatoas after Operation Jotunn fame, fame-as-curse + dysfunctional-crew-dynamic + meat-grinder-tempo. Female-primary-POV (returning). **Second authority-layer Hadeya-Etsul-POV + second Croatoas + second 'Steel Tread' named-vehicle**. First authority-layer Astra-Militarum-tank-warfare-cross-batch-character-continuity-sequel. Clean, no flags.
  - **W40K-0146 *Death Rider* (Rhuairidh James, 2026):** Astra-Militarum-Commissar-and-Death-Korps-of-Krieg novel. Commissar Valian Hesh stranded on Rezlan VI ordered to make the 472nd Siege Regiment of the Death Korps of Krieg withdraw before Exterminatus completes; Krieg-doctrine-vs-retreat tension; Tau-Empire counter-frame. **First authority-layer Valian Hesh + Rezlan VI + Death-Korps-of-Krieg 472nd Siege Regiment + Krieg-Commissar-tension-on-page register**. Second authority-layer Death-Korps-of-Krieg-primary after ssot-w40k-012 *Krieg*. `data_conflict` flag for missing roster author.
  - **W40K-0147 *The Green Tide* (multi-author omnibus, 2026):** Ork-themed-aggregation-omnibus. Collects Brooks's *Warboss* (already in ssot-w40k-013 W40K-0128) + Woolley's *Catachan Devil* (already in ssot-w40k-012 W40K-0117) + Lyons's *Iron Resolve* (novella) + Woolley's *Prisoners of Waaagh!* (novella) + four short stories incl. McNeill's *The Enemy of My Enemy*. Per Brief-061 omnibus-aggregation: facetIds + factions + locations + characters aggregate constituents. **First authority-layer omnibus-that-includes-prior-authority-layer-novels-as-constituents** — both *Warboss* + *Catachan Devil* appear inside. `data_conflict` flag for multi-author roster authors[] gap.
  - **W40K-0148 *Inquisitor / Draco* (Ian Watson, 1990):** Ordo-Malleus-Inquisitor novel — **the literal first Warhammer-40,000 novel ever published**. Inquisitor Jaq Draco dispatched to a hive world for Genestealer-cleanup, uncovers the **Hydra** rogue-Inquisition-cabal-conspiracy. Introduces the trilogy retinue: Callidus-Assassin Meh'Lindi, Navigator Vitali Googol, Squat-engineer Grimm. **First authority-layer Jaq Draco + Meh'Lindi + Vitali Googol + Grimm + Hydra-rogue-Inquisition-cabal + Squat-as-on-page-protagonist-retinue-member + Ordo-Malleus-Inquisitor-as-primary-POV + founding-novel-of-the-Black-Library-publishing-line surface forms**. Inquisition-Konsistenz constraint satisfied: Ordo Malleus + Inquisition at primary. Clean, no flags. Roster releaseYear=1990 confirmed; 2002 retitle to *Draco* is republication, not new entry.
  - **W40K-0149 *Harlequin* (Ian Watson, 1994):** Inquisition-War-trilogy book two — 100 years after *Inquisitor / Draco*. Now-renegade Jaq Draco pursues the Hydra-conspiracy via the Eldar Harlequins' **Ceremony of Cataclysm** on the orbital theatre circling devastated Stalinvast; Space Marines muster to purge the Harlequins; **Black Library of Chaos** + **Book of the Rhana Dandra** introduced. **First authority-layer Harlequins-as-primary-on-page-faction + Stalinvast-as-devastated-Imperial-world + Black-Library-of-Chaos + Book-of-the-Rhana-Dandra + renegade-Inquisitor-on-the-run register**. Second authority-layer Jaq-Draco + Harlequins (after ssot-w40k-011 *Ephrael Stern*-Kyganil-supporting-tier). Clean, no flags.
  - **W40K-0150 *Chaos Child* (Ian Watson, 1995):** Inquisition-War-trilogy conclusion. Draco's survivors escape via the Webway, reach Sabulorb; Thousand Sons arrive for the Book of the Rhana Dandra; Draco enters satori/enlightenment in the Webway; the controversial 'Emperor's Sons' / Star-Children cosmology register surfaces (recorded authoritatively-to-the-novel-without-claiming-canonical-resolution per Brief-061 surface-form-treue). **First authority-layer Sabulorb + Webway-as-on-page-traversal-setting + Thousand-Sons-as-on-page-faction + satori/enlightenment-death-register + Emperor's-Sons-controversial-conspiracy register surface forms**. Third Jaq-Draco appearance — closes the Inquisition-War-trilogy arc in the authority layer. Clean, no flags.
- **value_outside_vocabulary** (candidates surfaced by this batch, none promoted):
  - `commissar` — protagonist_class still has no `commissar` value; recurs with Valian Hesh in *Death Rider*. Workaround: `guardsman`. Sixth authority-layer entry now affected (Cain books ssot-w40k-002/003/004 + Krieg ssot-w40k-012 + Hell's Last ssot-w40k-014 Minka-Lesk + Death Rider this batch).
  - `inquisitor` — protagonist_class has `inquisitor` already, used for the three Watson-trilogy entries. Confirmed working value, no expansion needed.
  - `squat` / `abhuman` — first authority-layer Squat protagonist-retinue-member (Grimm in the Watson trilogy); no existing protagonist_class or faction-shape value. The Squat-as-retconned-in-and-out-of-canon register may need a dedicated value when the resolver pass addresses pre-modern-canon faction surface forms.
  - `corsair` / `aeldari_corsair` — protagonist_class has no `corsair` value; faction-shape similarly lacks. First authority-layer Aeldari-Corsair-as-primary in *Voidscarred*; an `aeldari_corsair` or `corsair` value would distinguish Corsair-band protagonists from Craftworld-or-Ynnari-protagonist registers.
  - `triarch_praetorian` / `necron_lord` — sub-values of Necron-as-primary-protagonist; Khemet in *Tomb World* is a single-POV Triarch-Praetorian, distinct from the Indomitus-Necron-ensemble. A `triarch_praetorian` faction-shape value would distinguish this from generic Necron-protagonist registers.
  - `valkyrie_pilot` / `aeronautica_imperialis_valkyrie` — sub-value of `pilot` (which itself is a still-unpromoted candidate from prior batches); *Vagabond Squadron*'s 901st Tactical Wing is Valkyrie-pilots specifically, distinct from Lightning / Thunderbolt / Marauder fighter / bomber registers. Now five authority-layer Aeronautica-Imperialis-primary entries with no dedicated `pilot` value (*Double Eagle*, *Outgunned*, *Above and Beyond*, *Interceptor City*, *Vagabond Squadron*).
  - `webway_journey` / `eldar_path_traversal` — sub-value of `journey`; the Watson-trilogy Webway-as-on-page-traversal-setting in *Chaos Child* introduces a register distinct from Imperial-warp-jump-journey or planetary-journey. A `webway_journey` value would tighten this.
  - `omnibus_with_prior_constituents` — *The Green Tide* is the first authority-layer omnibus that includes two prior-authority-layer novels as constituents. A `format` sub-tag distinguishing 'fresh-anthology' from 'collection-omnibus-of-prior-authority-layer-works' would tighten the omnibus-aggregation register established by Brief-061.
  - `cabal_inquisition` / `rogue_inquisition` — the **Hydra** in the Watson trilogy is a rogue-Inquisition-cabal pursuing its own agenda outside the Ordo-structure. A `rogue_inquisition` faction-shape would distinguish this from canonical-Inquisition-Ordo registers; relevant for any later Eisenhorn / Ravenor / Bequin resolver pass too where intra-Inquisition factionalism is load-bearing.
  - `cw_canon_divergence` — the Watson trilogy's 'Emperor's Sons' + reincarnation + Hydra cosmology diverges from later codex canon. A meta-tag noting 'canonically-significant-divergence-from-codex' would help readers understand context without forcing the SSOT to recanonise the older novels.

- **Notes:**
  - **Founding-Watson-Inquisition-War-trilogy lands en bloc.** The 1990-1995 Ian-Watson Inquisition-War trilogy (*Inquisitor / Draco* + *Harlequin* + *Chaos Child*) arrives in this batch as a contiguous three-entry block at the end of the roster slice — the literal first three Warhammer-40,000 novels ever published, with *Inquisitor* (1990) being the genesis novel of the entire Black-Library publishing line. **First authority-layer historical-canon-layer** (Squats / Hydra-rogue-Inquisition-cabal / Emperor's-Sons-controversial-cosmology / pre-modern Callidus-Temple register / Sabulorb / Stalinvast / Webway-as-on-page-traversal) that is distinct from modern-codex-canon surface forms — resolver work will need to address this layer separately rather than collapsing it into the modern-canon surface forms. The trilogy-retinue (Jaq Draco + Meh'Lindi + Vitali Googol + Grimm) recurs as primary-retinue across all three entries; surface-form-treue requires preserving each entry's faction list even when it duplicates the prior entry's surface forms.
  - **Completed-trilogy-arc-in-authority-layer milestone.** *Archmagos* (W40K-0144) is the third Belisarius-Cawl novel, completing the canonical Cawl-trilogy in the authority layer after *The Great Work* (ssot-w40k-011 W40K-0103) + *Genefather* (ssot-w40k-014 W40K-0134). **First such completed-trilogy-arc-in-authority-layer milestone** — the Inquisition-War-trilogy also enters complete with all three Watson entries in this batch, so this iteration delivers **two completed-trilogy-arcs simultaneously** (one modern, one founding).
  - **Cross-batch character-continuity peaks again.** Three direct sequels to prior authority-layer entries this batch (Archmagos = Cawl-trilogy-completion after *The Great Work* + *Genefather*; Demolisher = Hadeya-Etsul-book-2 after *Steel Tread*; Green Tide = omnibus-aggregation that includes two prior-authority-layer constituents *Warboss* + *Catachan Devil*). Highest mean of any iteration so far, driven by (a) the Watson-trilogy entries needing both the founding-novel-historical-context + the modern-canon-divergence-note + the retinue-and-Hydra-trilogy-arc-cross-references fitted into each synopsis, (b) the omnibus aggregation requiring constituent-novel-summaries within the single Green-Tide entry, (c) the cross-batch-character-continuity-sequels needing prior-entry-context + new-entry-context (Archmagos's Cawl-trilogy-arc + Demolisher's Steel Tread-aftermath + the implicit constituent-references in Green Tide). Higher floor than ssot-w40k-014 (1879 vs 1766) consistent with the higher first-authority-layer-surface-form-debut count.
  - **Resolver-Pre-Note (HOT):** kumulativ ist nach diesem Batch **150 — die nächste Iteration triggert die natürliche Resolver-Pause** (`cumulativeBefore=150` % 50 == 0 → loud-stop unless `skip-50-stop` marker is set). **Cowork-Tendenz aus Brief 061 + früheren Resolver-Pässen: Resolver-Brief jetzt schreiben** — Surface-Form-Pile seit dem ersten Resolver-Pass in 069 spans ssot-w40k-006..015 = 100 Bücher mit ~190-210 new factions / locations / characters einschließlich diesem Batch's seven-first-authority-layer-faction-debut (Aeldari Corsairs / Starsplinters / Triarch Praetorians / 901st Tactical Wing / Death-Korps-472nd / Hydra / Harlequins-primary) + ten-first-authority-layer-character-debut (Stormdawn + Leotharan + Khemet + Hekasun + Hesh + Jaq Draco + Meh'Lindi + Googol + Grimm + Obispal) + nine-first-appearance-locations + Watson-trilogy-canon-divergence-layer (Squats / Hydra / Emperor's-Sons / Webway-on-page) that resolver work will need to address as a distinct historical-canon-layer separately from modern-codex surface forms. **Two completed-trilogy-arcs-in-authority-layer milestones** delivered this iteration (Cawl-trilogy modern + Watson-trilogy founding) — the resolver-pass-after-this-batch will have an unusually clean trilogy-anchor set to work from.
  - **Brief-071-Vertrag aktiv:** Override-Datei + Status-Log-Append in einem Commit ohne Co-Author-Trailer, keine sonstigen Datei-Edits. Lint/typecheck/brain-lint nicht gelaufen — data-only commit (eine JSON + ein Markdown-Append), keine Code-/Brain-Page-Änderungen, alle drei Lint-Targets nicht betroffen. Per Brief-061-Klausel akzeptabel.

Series-start tier.

Inquisition-consistency: Sternberg is on-page-as-quest-giver → Inquisition tagged supporting (Ordo unspecified in the text).
  - **W40K-0154 *Grey Hunter* (King, 2002):** Series book 3. **Madox** of the **Thousand Sons** has stolen the **Spear of Russ** to open a portal to the **Planet of the Sorcerers** and free **Magnus the Red** into the material realm; Ragnar throws the Spear into the warp-portal to close the gate at the cost of the Chapter's relic, transitioning from Blood Claw to **Grey Hunter** and seeding the Spear-recovery arc that closes in *Wolf's Honour*. **First authority-layer Madox + first authority-layer Spear of Russ + first Garm + first authority-layer Planet of the Sorcerers + first authority-layer Magnus the Red + first authority-layer Thousand-Sons-Space-Wolves-hereditary-enmity register + first authority-layer Grey-Hunter-rank surface forms.** Mid-series tier.
  - **W40K-0155 *Wolfblade* (King, 2003):** Series book 4 and King's final entry. Ragnar dispatched to **Terra** as a member of the **Wolfblade** honour-guard protecting **House Belisarius** of the **Navis Nobilite** — escorting **Lady Gabriela Belisarius**, working alongside fellow Wolfblade **Torin**, navigating a **Paternoval Envoy** succession assassination plot reaching into the depths of the Imperium. **First authority-layer entry where House Belisarius is the primary protagonist faction**; **first authority-layer Wolfblade duty register + first Gabriela Belisarius + first Torin + first authority-layer Paternoval Envoy + first authority-layer Ragnar-on-Terra register surface forms**; second authority-layer Navis-Nobilite appearance after *Rites of Passage* (ssot-w40k-011 W40K-0104) but first as House-Belisarius-specifically + first as Space-Wolves-oath-bound House.
  - **W40K-0156 *Sons of Fenris* (Lightner, 2007):** Series book 5 and Lightner's first contribution after King left. **Hyades** Chaos-incursion brings the Space Wolves to a battlefield where a **Dark Angels** strike force is already on-planet with its own objective; the two ancient-rival Chapters' presence escalates to open inter-Chapter confrontation as Chaos exploits the rift. Russ-Lion-Heresy-feud + Fallen-Angels-question register sub-text. **First authority-layer entry where the Dark Angels Chapter is on-page**; **first authority-layer Hyades + first authority-layer Space-Wolves-Dark-Angels-rivalry register + first authority-layer Russ-Lion-Heresy-feud register surface forms**.
  - **W40K-0157 *Wolf's Honour* (Lightner, 2008):** Series book 6 and conclusion of the King-launched Spear-of-Russ arc. **Thousand Sons** multi-front-offensive against the Space Wolves; Ragnar's lightning-strike counter-attack on the Thousand-Sons' base; **Madox** confrontation; **Spear of Russ** recovery-arc closure. **Series-finale tier for the original-Ragnar-saga** (six-volume original closed; successor Ragnar-arcs in later authority-layer entries TBD); **first authority-layer Spear-of-Russ-recovery-arc closure register + second authority-layer Madox appearance + second authority-layer Thousand-Sons-Space-Wolves-hereditary-enmity climax surface forms**.

Length tier: `doorstopper` (three-novel collection).
  - **W40K-0159 *Space Wolf: The Second Omnibus* (King + Lightner, 2009, omnibus):** Pure-aggregation entry collecting the closing trilogy of the original Ragnar-saga (W40K-0155+0156+0157 this batch — *Wolfblade* by King + *Sons of Fenris* + *Wolf's Honour* by Lightner). Factions / locations / characters / facetIds aggregated from constituent novels per Brief-061 omnibus-constraint. **Authority-layer-internal aggregation** — third omnibus in this batch aggregating same-batch-authored-content. Length tier: `doorstopper` (three-novel collection). **First authority-layer multi-author-omnibus surface form** (King + Lightner co-credit).
  - **W40K-0160 *Krakenblood* (Collins, 2025):** Standalone Space-Wolves novel — Marc Collins's sixth Black-Library novel since 2021 and his pivot from Emperor's Children to Space Wolves. **Ivar Krakenblood**, Wolf Priest of Fenris, takes a relic-recovery quest from **Ulrik the Slayer** himself, gathering a band of warriors to forge his own saga-worthy destiny outside the Ragnar-arc register. Hubris-and-destiny register; Krakenblood-as-mighty-but-complicated-hero — willing to risk his brothers-in-arms for greatness. **First authority-layer Ivar Krakenblood + first authority-layer Ulrik the Slayer + first authority-layer Wolf-Priest-as-primary-POV register + first authority-layer 2025-publication-frontier-Space-Wolves entry surface forms**. Standalone tier — no Ragnar-saga prerequisite reading.
- **value_outside_vocabulary** (candidates surfaced by this batch, none promoted):
  - `wolf_priest` — protagonist_class has no `wolf_priest` value. *Krakenblood* uses Ivar Krakenblood as Wolf-Priest-primary-POV; the Space-Wolves Wolf-Priest vocation (chaplain-equivalent crossed with shamanic-Fenrisian-Rune-Priest-register) is sufficiently distinct from generic `space_marine` that a `wolf_priest` or `chaplain` sub-tag would tighten. Same workaround applied: `space_marine`.
  - `grey_hunter` — within-Space-Wolves Astartes rank tier (Blood Claw → Grey Hunter → Long Fang → Wolf Guard). *Grey Hunter* (W40K-0154) explicitly turns on Ragnar's transition into this rank. No facet captures within-Chapter rank progression; the `space_marine` blanket-class is the workaround.
  - `relic_quest` / `artefact_recovery` — both *Ragnar's Claw* (Talisman of Lykos) and *Krakenblood* (Wolf-Priest-relic-quest) hinge on relic-recovery as the primary plot engine; *Wolf's Honour* + *Grey Hunter* extend this around the Spear of Russ. `journey` covers the structural shape (going-to-the-relic + going-back) but loses the relic-as-MacGuffin specificity. A `relic_quest` or `artefact_macguffin` plot_type sub-tag would tighten.
  - `inter_chapter_conflict` / `chapter_vs_chapter` — *Sons of Fenris*'s Space-Wolves-vs-Dark-Angels confrontation is distinct from the Astartes-vs-Astartes-Heretic register (Heretic Astartes / Chaos Space Marines covers that) — it's two-loyal-Imperial-Chapters at risk of shooting at each other. No facet captures this; `political_thriller` + `war_story` are the closest but neither matches the Imperial-Astartes-internal-frame specifically.
  - `space_wolves_curse` / `gene_seed_flaw` — the Curse of the Wulfen in *Space Wolf* (Kjel's reversion) is the Chapter's signature gene-seed-flaw register; no facet captures Chapter-specific-gene-seed-flaws (analogous to the Black Rage in the Blood Angels register, the Curse of the Flesh in the Iron Hands register, etc.). A `gene_seed_flaw` or `chapter_specific_burden` theme-sub-tag would tighten across multiple Astartes-Chapter-registers — high-priority promotion candidate given the recurrence across batches.
  - `wolfblade_duty` / `oath_bond_inter_faction` — the *Wolfblade* register is the Space-Wolves-House-Belisarius oath-bond as an institutional-on-page structure; no facet captures cross-faction-oath-bond / honour-guard-duty. `loyalty` theme covers the moral register but loses the institutional-structure-specifically.

Length tier `doorstopper` consistently applied to all three.
  - **Space-Wolves-Chapter-as-primary-protagonist-faction debut.** Prior authority-layer Space-Wolves appearances were faction-tier mentions only (generic Astartes-Space-Wolves-faction-tier in ssot-w40k-005's *Salvation's Reach* via Gaunt + ssot-w40k-010's *Eye of Medusa* / etc.); this is the first batch where the Chapter is the primary protagonist faction across nine of ten entries. The Ragnar-Blackmane-saga-six-volume-original + the *Krakenblood* 2025-publication-frontier Wolf-Priest standalone together establish a dense Space-Wolves register the Resolver will need to fold in — including the within-Chapter-rank progression (Blood Claw → Grey Hunter → Wolf-Priest), the gene-seed flaw (Curse of the Wulfen), the Wolfblade-House-Belisarius institutional oath-bond, and the hereditary Thousand-Sons-Space-Wolves enmity.
  - **Inquisition-consistency constraint** (Brief 061): triggered cleanly for one entry — W40K-0153 *Ragnar's Claw* (Inquisitor Ivan Sternberg is on-page quest-giver and supporting POV → Inquisition tagged supporting; Sternberg's Ordo is unspecified in the novel itself, so no specific Ordo Xenos / Malleus / Hereticus / Redactor tag added). The W40K-0151 *The Inquisition War Omnibus* aggregation re-pulls the Inquisition + Ordo Malleus tagging from W40K-0148+0149+0150 (the constituent Watson novels in ssot-w40k-015 where Jaq Draco is primary Inquisitor of the Ordo Malleus). No other entries in this batch have Inquisitor-on-page POVs.
  - **Wolfblade-duty cross-reference.** *Wolfblade* (W40K-0155) establishes the Space-Wolves-House-Belisarius oath-bond as the central plot-structure of the novel; *Sons of Fenris* (W40K-0156) reads as post-Wolfblade-return (the Lightner pickup-point); *Wolf's Honour* (W40K-0157) closes the Wolfblade-tour's strategic-payoff in the form of the multi-front Thousand-Sons-Spear-of-Russ-recovery offensive. The three Lightner-and-late-King books together form a Wolfblade-arc-substructure within the larger Ragnar-saga; *The Second Omnibus* (W40K-0159) aggregates these as a single 2003-2008 volume.
  - **`data_conflict` flags this iteration: none.** All ten roster entries are correctly typed (`omnibus` for the three omnibuses; `novel` for the seven novels). Author attributions match the roster (King solo for 0152-0155; Lightner solo for 0156+0157; King + Lightner co-credit for 0159; Watson for 0151; Collins for 0160). **No author-missing-roster-pattern** (the recent ssot-w40k-014 + ssot-w40k-015 author-missing pattern was 2025-2026-publication-frontier-specific; this batch's only 2025-publication-frontier entry W40K-0160 has Collins correctly attributed in roster).
  - **`low_confidence` flags this iteration: none.** All seven non-omnibus entries have strong 1999-2025 Black-Library coverage (Lexicanum, Fandom, Goodreads, Adventures-with-Peps, TV-Tropes, Black-Library product pages, Risingshadow, Goonhammer-Reviews for Krakenblood, At-Boundary's-Edge for Krakenblood). The three omnibuses are pure-aggregations; no independent-coverage-confidence-assessment applies.
  - **Surface-form treue compliance.** "Space Wolves" used as the primary Chapter surface form across all nine Space-Wolves-entries (no "Vlka Fenryka" Wolves-of-Fenris-Old-Tongue used — the King-Lightner-Collins novels' canonical Black-Library register is "Space Wolves", and the Vlka-Fenryka surface form is Aaron-Dembski-Bowden-era-Horus-Heresy-specific). "Thousand Sons" used over "1KSons" / "Thousand Suns" (the Grey-Hunter search-result-typo "Thousand Suns" is corrected pre-write; the Black-Library + Lexicanum canonical form is "Thousand Sons").   - **Synopsis-length elasticity.** Range 1335–2410 chars; nine of ten sit at or above the 1200-char soft cap; median ~1944. Driven by (a) the omnibus entries' three-novel-aggregation requiring synopsis-coverage of three plot-arcs in a single entry (W40K-0151 at 2410 + W40K-0158 at 1623 + W40K-0159 at 1335 — note W40K-0158 + 0159 are tighter than W40K-0151 because their constituent novels are described in the immediate-preceding same-batch entries, reducing the need to fully restate plots; W40K-0151's constituents are in the prior ssot-w40k-015 batch and benefit from a fuller self-contained restatement), (b) the cross-batch-Ragnar-saga-arc-continuity requiring forward-and-back-references between W40K-0152..0157 entries (each Ragnar-saga novel's synopsis references both predecessors and successors within the same batch).

- **Per-book bullets:**
  - **W40K-0161 *Status: Deadzone* (Gascoigne + Jones eds, 2000, anthology):** Founding Necromunda anthology — 11 stories by 8 authors (Matthew Farrer, Gordon Rennie, Jonathan Green, Alex Hammond, Tully R. Summers, Richard Williams, Neil Rutledge, et al), all set in Hive Primus underhive. Established the line's short-fiction register. Format=anthology per SSOT (correct, no `data_conflict` flag). characters=[] (anthology — too many to enumerate authoritatively without per-story breakdown).
  - **W40K-0162 *Survival Instinct* (Chambers, 2004/2005):** Chambers' debut novel. D'onne 'Mad Donna' Ulanti — Spire-born ex-noble, House Escher gang leader in Hive Primus underhive. Mysterious Guilder triggers exploration of her noble-past. Female POV (only second female-POV in W40K-domain authority-layer after Bequin in ssot-w40k-001/002).
  - **W40K-0163 *Salvation* (Goto, 2004):** Zefer Tyranus, curator at House Ko'iron in the Spire of Hive Primus, descends through the hive to recover an ancient artefact connecting his House to the founding fathers of Necromunda. Three rival pursuers (spy + Redemption-adjacent gang leader + hive librarian). **First authority-layer House Ko'iron.**
  - **W40K-0164 *Blood Royal* (Rennie + McDermott, 2005):** Kal Jerico series-start. Kal — illegitimate son of Lord Gerontius Helmawr — dispatched by his father to hunt Kal's half-brother Armand, who has stolen a House-Helmawr artefact, clad himself in Spyer hunting-rig, and is exsanguinating victims through the Underhive. Nephew Valtin Schemko accompanies as quasi-witness. **First authority-layer Kal Jerico + Lord Gerontius Helmawr + Armand Helmawr + Valtin Schemko + Wotan-the-mastiff (early form).**
  - **W40K-0165 *Junktion* (Farrer, 2005):** Sinden Kass — lamplighter (underhive electrical-supply maintainer) in the small downhive township of Junktion. When the other lamplighters die one by one, Kass becomes the most valuable man in town and a target for Guilders + encroaching gangs. Tight-bounded siege-against-creeping-pressure register; Farrer-noir-claustrophobia signature. **First authority-layer Sinden Kass + Junktion (township).**
  - **W40K-0166 *Fleshworks* (Soulban, 2006):** Uriah Storm — House Delaque secrets-and-shadows agent — descends through Hive Primus to recover top-grade House Van Saar bionic implants from their still-living current owners. Delaque-vs-Van-Saar inter-House espionage + gory surgical-procedural set-pieces + Delaque-internal-politics-as-additional-threat. Setting tilts toward Hive City (more-ordered, claustrophobic-corporate) rather than the deepest Underhive. **First authority-layer Uriah Storm + House-Delaque-as-primary register.**
  - **W40K-0167 *Outlander* (Keefe, 2006):** Quiet stranger of forger-skill arrives at a small abandoned-and-half-reclaimed Underhive settlement during a day-long ash-storm. Local House Cawdor / Redemption-cult congregation tries to coerce his forgery-talents to nefarious purpose; the stranger's hidden revenge-arc unfolds. Deeper-than-typical-Necromunda treatment of House Cawdor / Redemption-cult internal-life. Protagonist deliberately kept unnamed in synopsis mirroring source-material's authorial reticence. **First authority-layer House-Cawdor-as-primary + Redemption-cult-as-fanatic-extortion register.**
  - **W40K-0168 *Back from the Dead* (Kyme, 2006/2007):** Erik Bane — ex-Proctor-General of the Necromunda Hive City Enforcers, expelled, drifted into the Underhive, lost most of his life to addiction — pulled back into operational habits by a fleeing girl pursued by the Razorheads gang. The Neurone Plague (periodic underhive zombie-outbreak infection) sweeps the tunnels; Bane leads a disparate group of survivors against Razorheads + zombies + Redemptionist fanatics + his own addiction-relapse. **First authority-layer Erik Bane + Neurone Plague + Razorheads + Proctor-General-as-Enforcer-rank.**
  - **W40K-0169 *Cardinal Crimson* (McDermott, 2007):** Kal Jerico #2. Kal hauled before crime-boss Nemo to settle debts; bounty contract leads Kal back into the path of his old nemesis Cardinal Crimson (senior Redemptionist demagogue). Cardinal hunts a newcomer-to-the-hive whose secrets could finish him forever; Kal, Wotan (metal mastiff), Scabbs (Ratskin-mutant partner), and Yoland (Escher gang-fighter) become the obstacle. **First authority-layer Cardinal Crimson + Nemo + Scabbs + Yoland; first Wotan-as-named-companion.**
  - **W40K-0170 *Lasgun Wedding* (McDermott, 2008):** Kal Jerico #3 / series-finale. Lord Gerontius Helmawr assassinated; Kal coerced into the Helmawr seat as figurehead-ruler. Kal becomes target of every spire-noble-assassin, and noble Houses maneuver him into a politically-engineered marriage with a high-Spire heiress. Kal begins to suspect his elevation is not luck but the climax of a long-running plot. Tone-shift toward court_intrigue. **First authority-layer Helmawr-assassination + Kal-as-pretender-to-Necromunda's-throne register.**
- **value_outside_vocabulary** (candidates surfaced by this batch, none promoted):
  - `bounty_hunter` / `ganger` / `fallen_noble` — protagonist_class has no Necromunda-specific values. Kal Jerico (bounty hunter), D'onne / Mad Donna (Spire-born ex-noble turned ganger), Sinden Kass (lamplighter-civilian-pressed-into-fighter), Zefer Tyranus (curator-turned-questing-protagonist) all forced into `civilian` as closest available. The Necromunda novel-line's protagonist-typology is its own distinct register that the catalog does not cover.
  - `anthology` — format-field. SSOT-roster correctly tags W40K-0161 as `anthology`, but facet catalog `format` taxonomy lists only `book` / `audiobook` / `animation` / `live_action` / `audio_drama` / `podcast`, so facetIds use `book` and the SSOT-format-field carries the anthology disambiguation separately.
  - `underhive` / `spire` / `hive_city` — no `setting` or `scope` value captures the vertical-tier split within a single hive world. `planetary` is used uniformly but the Necromunda novel-line's central structural distinction is which-tier-of-the-hive the action is in (Spire vs Hive City vs Underhive vs Sump).
  - `lamplighter` / `enforcer` / `proctor_general` — specialist Necromunda profession-and-rank vocabulary (Junktion's lamplighter trade; Back-from-the-Dead's Proctor-General Enforcer rank). Not in the protagonist_class taxonomy.
  - `neurone_plague` / `underhive_zombie_outbreak` — Back from the Dead's specific horror-vector register; not captured by `cosmic_horror` alone (which is more Lovecraftian than zombie-plague-specific).
  - `mafia_extortion` / `faith_racket` — Outlander's House-Cawdor-Redemption-cult-as-mafia-style-extortion register; no theme/plot_type captures the religious-extortion combination.

Next batch: `ssot-w40k-018`, slice = W40K-0171..W40K-0180 (continuation of the Necromunda cluster — now into the **modern-imprint relaunch era**, 2018-2021, tied to the 2017 specialist-game re-release that revived the line after a ~10-year gap following the 2008 *Lasgun Wedding* finale in ssot-w40k-017).

  - 1 obligatory plot-confirmation search each for: W40K-0171 *Wanted: Dead* (Jarene + Wild Cats + outlawed-Escher-gang frame via Goodreads / Track-of-Words / Black-Library / Lexicanum), W40K-0172 *Sinner's Bounty* (Kal Jerico modern-imprint revival + Desolation Zoon Redemptionist target + Venators via WH40k-Book-Club / Track-of-Words), W40K-0173 *Terminal Overkill* (Brielle + Wild Hydras + Goliath Fettnir + Dim Zone + Red Tori via Goodreads / WH40k-Book-Club / Track-of-Words), W40K-0174 *Low Lives* (Caleb Cursebound + Iktomi-the-ratskin + Hope's End + Orlock-gang-antagonist via Goodreads / Track-of-Words / Civilian-Reader), W40K-0175 *Underhive Anthology* (full table-of-contents — 1 novella + 9 shorts by Brooks/Harrison/Hinks/Reynolds/Haley/MacNiven/Kyme — via Amazon / Black-Library / Goodreads), W40K-0176 *Road to Redemption* (Zeke + Floodgrave + lapsed-Cawdor-redemption frame via Black-Library / At-Boundary's-Edge / Track-of-Words), W40K-0177 *Soulless Fury* (D'onne / Mad-Donna + Scrutinator-Servalen + KB-88 cyber-mastiff + Dog-the-ogryn + dual-POV-manhunt via Goodreads / Track-of-Words / Lexicanum), W40K-0178 *Uprising* (multi-author anthology: Annandale/Kloster/Hill/Flowers/Green/Brooks/McDermott/Wiltgren/Rath — confirmed via Amazon TOC / Lexicanum / Simon-&-Schuster), W40K-0179 *Fire Made Flesh* (Tempes Sol + Guild of Light + Lord Silas Pureburn + Fallen Dome of Periculus via Goodreads / Black-Library / Unseen-Library / At-Boundary's-Edge), W40K-0180 *Spark of Revolution* (Breaker Brass + ogryn-POV + House of Chains Goliath civil war via Goodreads / Track-of-Words / Black-Library / Lexicanum). No conditional follow-ups needed — modern-imprint coverage uniformly mid-tier-or-better.
- **Per-book bullets:**
  - **W40K-0171 *Wanted: Dead* (Brooks, 2018):** ⚠ **`data_conflict` flag — format**. Black Library Novella Series 1 #6 — a **novella**, not a novel as the SSOT-roster lists. Jarene-of-Wild-Cats Escher procedural; outlawed-after-Guilder-killing inversion. Subsequently reprinted as the opener of W40K-0175 *Underhive Anthology* (this batch — the anthology has its own entry, so the novella has a single-source-of-truth even though the text appears twice in the roster). **First authority-layer Jarene + Wild Cats (Escher gang).**
  - **W40K-0172 *Sinner's Bounty* (Reynolds, 2019):** Kal Jerico modern-imprint revival — Reynolds takes over the series-baton from Rennie/McDermott. Notable as a **second authority-layer Kal Jerico surface form** sitting alongside the 2005-2008 Rennie/McDermott trilogy from ssot-w40k-017 (W40K-0164 + W40K-0169 + W40K-0170); the Resolver-Brief should consolidate the canonical Kal-Jerico-character-id once across both eras. **First authority-layer Desolation Zoon (Redemptionist antagonist) + first Venators-as-faction-class register.** Clean.
  - **W40K-0173 *Terminal Overkill* (Hill, 2019):** Hill's grim-Escher coming-of-age, single-POV-with-oral-retelling-frame, several-year arc. Brielle / Red Tori / Fettnir / Wild Hydras / Dim Zone all **first authority-layer surface forms**. Tonally darker and slower-paced than the rest of the batch — closer to the somber-grim register of ssot-w40k-017's *Survival Instinct* than to the action-comedy modern-Kal-Jerico revival. **Second-ever W40K-authority-layer female-POV from an Escher viewpoint** after ssot-w40k-017 W40K-0162 (Mad Donna / D'onne Ulanti).
  - **W40K-0174 *Low Lives* (Flowers, 2019):** ⚠ **`data_conflict` flag — format**. Black Library Novella Series 2 #9 — a **novella**, not a novel as the SSOT-roster lists. **First authority-layer Caleb Cursebound + Iktomi-the-ratskin + Hope's End + Ratskins-as-faction-class.** Caleb / Iktomi return as the **framing-piece** of W40K-0178 *Uprising* later in this batch (the Cursebound saga continues across both entries; the saga's continuation thread into W40K-0179 *Fire Made Flesh* is tonal/setting rather than POV-continuous — Tempes Sol replaces Caleb as POV).
  - **W40K-0175 *Underhive: A Necromunda Anthology* (Black Library, 2019):** Format `anthology` correct in roster — no flag. Aggregated factions/locations across all ten constituent pieces (1 novella + 9 shorts); story-list from Amazon TOC + Goodreads. Notable contributor stable: Brooks, Harrison, Hinks, Reynolds, Haley, MacNiven, Kyme — sets the modern-imprint short-fiction authorial-bench for the line's relaunch era.
  - **W40K-0176 *Road to Redemption* (Brooks, 2020):** Brooks' second Black-Library novel, swapping Navigator Houses for Necromunda. **First authority-layer Zeke + Floodgrave + modern-imprint Cawdor-as-primary-protagonist-and-internal-critique register.** Brooks targets the Cawdor / Redemption religious-extremism complex from within — the protagonist is a lapsed Cawdor, not an external critic. Pairs as faction-counterweight to W40K-0167 *Outlander* in ssot-w40k-017 (which approached the same Cawdor / Redemption material from an external-stranger viewpoint). Tonal-register: grim-redemption-quest.
  - **W40K-0177 *Soulless Fury* (McDermott, 2020):** Dual-POV (Mad Donna + Scrutinator Servalen) manhunt-procedural. **Surface-form revival of D'onne Ulanti / Mad Donna from ssot-w40k-017 W40K-0162** *Survival Instinct* — fifteen publication-years between the two appearances. The Resolver-Brief should consolidate the canonical name (D'onne Ulanti vs Mad Donna vs Donna Ulanti) across both entries; both surface forms are listed in this batch's character-list to preserve source-fidelity. **First authority-layer Scrutinator Primus Servalen + KB-88 cyber-mastiff + Dog the ogryn + modern-imprint Necromunda Enforcer Scrutinator-rank register.** Lord-Helmawr-as-living-throughline in modern continuity (in contrast to the assassinated-in-2008 Lord Gerontius Helmawr from W40K-0170 *Lasgun Wedding*) — the modern-imprint relaunch is best read as a soft-reboot continuity, **noted for future Resolver-pass-character-consolidation**.
  - **W40K-0178 *Uprising* (Black Library, 2020):** ⚠ **`data_conflict` flag — format**. Multi-author short-fiction collection (nine Black-Library authors: Annandale + Kloster + Hill + Flowers + Green + Brooks + McDermott + Wiltgren + Rath — confirmed via Amazon table-of-contents listing), framed by Denny Flowers' Caleb Cursebound material. SSOT-roster lists `novel`; **suggestion: `anthology`**. Notable: Caleb Cursebound + Iktomi return as the recurring-frame; structurally a sequel-of-sorts to W40K-0174 *Low Lives* in this batch even though the anthology itself contains nine other authors' shorts.
  - **W40K-0179 *Fire Made Flesh* (Flowers, 2021):** Flowers' debut full-length novel after his Caleb-Cursebound shorts and novella. POV shifts to **Tempes Sol of the Guild of Light** — first authority-layer Guild of Light + Tempes Sol surface forms — vs **Lord Silas Pureburn**, the Keeper of the God-Emperor's Eternal Flame (a Redemptionist demagogue). Setting: **Fallen Dome of Periculus**, a re-discovered lost-dome with archeotech + rage-affliction + flesh-feasting horrors. Tonal-register: grimdark archeotech-horror with religious-extremism subtext, distinct from the rest of the batch — closer to the cosmic-horror tag-register than to Underhive-noir. Cursebound-saga continuation thread is tonal/setting only (the Periculus-arc was seeded earlier in Flowers' work; not a direct POV-sequel).
  - **W40K-0180 *Spark of Revolution* (Kloster, 2020):** Black Library Novella Series 3 #5. Roster `format=novella` correct — no flag. **First authority-layer Breaker Brass + House of Chains (Goliath sub-faction) + ogryn-as-protagonist-POV register + Necromunda-servitor-revolt register.** Notable as a **rare ogryn-POV** with a hopeful tonal-register — the only `hopeful` tag in the entire ssot-w40k-017+018 Necromunda block (twenty entries combined). Goliath-civil-war frame is structurally distinct from the gang-vs-gang inter-House register that dominates the rest of the Necromunda authority-layer.
- **value_outside_vocabulary** (candidates surfaced by this batch, none promoted):
  - `novella` — format-field is its own SSOT-format-field value, but the facet catalog `format` taxonomy doesn't separately model it (only `book`); used-as-workaround `book` + tagged `short` for length_tier. Three entries in this batch are technically novellas (W40K-0171, W40K-0174, W40K-0180) — pattern is repeated enough across the Black-Library Novella-Series imprints (Series 1-#6, Series 2-#9, Series 3-#5 all in this batch) that a `novella` length-tier or format-tier value warrants Cowork attention.
  - `bounty_hunter` — protagonist_class — Kal Jerico (modern-imprint, this batch) + Caleb Cursebound (this batch) + Mad Donna (this batch) + Jarene (this batch) + the entire Venator-class in W40K-0172 + W40K-0178 all sit closer to `bounty_hunter` / `ganger` / `mercenary` than to the catalog's `civilian` workaround. Already raised in ssot-w40k-017 — repeated here.
  - `ratskin` — Iktomi (W40K-0174 + W40K-0178) is a ratskin, a Necromunda-specific class (mutant-Underhive-natives). No catalog value exists.
  - `ogryn-protagonist` — Breaker Brass (W40K-0180) is an ogryn; Dog (W40K-0177) is an ogryn supporting-companion. No catalog value captures the ogryn-POV register as distinct from human-civilian.
  - `coming_of_age` — used as-tagged on W40K-0173 (the catalog has this tag); flagged here to confirm it landed as the right semantic match for Brielle's years-spanning growth arc.
- **Notable surface-form frequencies within this batch:**
  - *Factions (Necromunda Houses + cult/guild register):* House Cawdor ×5 (W40K-0172 antagonist + W40K-0176 primary + W40K-0177 antagonist + W40K-0178 primary + W40K-0179 antagonist), Redemptionists ×6 (every entry from W40K-0172 onward except W40K-0173 + W40K-0180), Guilders ×9 (near-ubiquitous, only W40K-0180's foundry-frame skips), House Escher ×3 (W40K-0171 primary + W40K-0173 primary + W40K-0175 anthology primary), House Goliath ×3 (W40K-0173 antagonist + W40K-0175 anthology + W40K-0180 primary), House Orlock ×3 (W40K-0174 antagonist + W40K-0175 anthology + W40K-0178 primary), House Helmawr ×3 (W40K-0172 supporting + W40K-0177 supporting + W40K-0180 supporting), Necromunda Enforcers ×3 (W40K-0171 antagonist + W40K-0175 anthology + W40K-0177 primary), House Ulanti ×1 (W40K-0177 primary — **modern-imprint revival of the ssot-w40k-017 W40K-0162 Mad-Donna surface form**), Venators ×2 (W40K-0172 + W40K-0178 — **first authority-layer**), House of Chains ×1 (W40K-0180 primary — **first authority-layer Goliath sub-faction**), Guild of Light ×1 (W40K-0179 primary — **first authority-layer Necromunda Guild-of-Light**), Corpse Guild ×1 (W40K-0178 primary — **first authority-layer**), Ratskins ×2 (W40K-0174 + W40K-0178 — **first authority-layer Ratskins-as-faction-class**), House Delaque ×1 (W40K-0175 anthology), House Van Saar ×1 (W40K-0175 anthology), Spyrers ×1 (W40K-0175 anthology), Imperium ×10.
