  - *Characters:* Caleb Cursebound ×2 POV/supporting (W40K-0174 + W40K-0178 framing), Iktomi ×2 (W40K-0174 + W40K-0178 framing), Mad Donna / D'onne Ulanti ×1 POV + double-listing (W40K-0177 — **modern-imprint revival of the ssot-w40k-017 W40K-0162 surface form**), Jarene ×2 (W40K-0171 POV + W40K-0175 anthology supporting), Kal Jerico ×1 POV (W40K-0172 — modern-imprint; **separate from the 2005-2008 trilogy Kal in ssot-w40k-017**), Desolation Zoon ×1 (W40K-0172 antagonist), Brielle ×1 (W40K-0173 POV), Red Tori ×1 (W40K-0173 supporting — deceased mother), Fettnir ×1 (W40K-0173 antagonist), Zeke ×1 (W40K-0176 POV), Scrutinator Primus Servalen ×1 (W40K-0177 POV), Lord Helmawr ×1 (W40K-0177 supporting — **modern-continuity, distinct from the assassinated Gerontius Helmawr in ssot-w40k-017 W40K-0170**), KB-88 ×1 (W40K-0177 supporting), Dog ×1 (W40K-0177 supporting — ogryn companion), Tempes Sol ×1 (W40K-0179 POV), Lord Silas Pureburn ×1 (W40K-0179 antagonist), Breaker Brass ×1 (W40K-0180 POV), Yar Umbra ×1 (W40K-0178 supporting — Venator framing-piece POV).
- **Notes:**
  - **Modern-imprint Necromunda cluster — direct continuation of ssot-w40k-017.** Publication-era jumps from 2008 (*Lasgun Wedding*) to 2018 (*Wanted: Dead*), a ten-year gap that maps to the Black-Library Necromunda-imprint-hiatus between the original 2000-2008 specialist line and the 2017-onwards relaunch tied to the new specialist-game-edition. Continuity-wise: the modern imprint is best read as a **soft-reboot** that keeps the geographical / factional / cultural backdrop while resetting load-bearing character-state — most notably, **Lord Helmawr is alive again** (appears in W40K-0177 + W40K-0180 framing), in clear contrast to the assassinated Lord Gerontius Helmawr at the close of ssot-w40k-017's W40K-0170 *Lasgun Wedding*. Surface-form-treue compliance kept "Lord Helmawr" as the modern-imprint name (consistent with Black-Library copy) and reserved "Lord Gerontius Helmawr" for the 2005-2008 trilogy; Resolver-Brief should explicitly mark the two as distinct entities.
  - **Three `data_conflict` flags — all format-field**. W40K-0171 + W40K-0174 (`novel` → `novella` — both are Black-Library Novella-Series entries) + W40K-0178 (`novel` → `anthology` — multi-author short-fiction collection). All three are robust source-confirmed errors in the SSOT-roster: the Novella-Series numbering is public (#6, #9, #5 across the three series) and the *Uprising* anthology's nine-author TOC is on Amazon. **Excel-SSOT correction needed** (parallels the *Death or Glory* roster-typo correction in ssot-w40k-002): without correction in the upstream `Warhammer_Books_SSOT.xlsx`, `import-ssot-roster.ts` will regenerate these three format errors on the next roster-rebuild.
  - **Long-tail specialist-imprint discipline applied** (Brief 061 OQ): WebSearch confirmed plot-shape on all ten entries (mean 1.0 / book, max 1 — well within the 5-per-book soft cap); modern-imprint coverage was uniformly mid-tier-or-better, no `low_confidence` flags raised. Synopses run 1300-2000 chars (slightly longer than ssot-w40k-017's 941-1614 range) — the modern-imprint coverage allows more concrete plot-detail than the early/mid-2000s cluster, but synopsis-length-elasticity stayed away from speculative-subplot-elaboration.
  - **Inquisition-consistency constraint** (Brief 061): not triggered. No on-page Inquisitor POVs in any of the ten; closest are the Scrutinator-Primus-Enforcer-rank (W40K-0177) and the Cawdor / Redemption religious-extortion register (faith-extremism, not Inquisition-derived). No `Inquisition` faction tagged on any entry — correct per source coverage.
  - **Surface-form revival cross-batch.** Mad Donna / D'onne Ulanti is the **first cross-batch character revival** in the authority layer (W40K-0162 in ssot-w40k-017 → W40K-0177 in ssot-w40k-018), with a fifteen-publication-year gap (2004 → 2020). Both batch's character-lists preserve both surface forms ("D'onne Ulanti" + "Mad Donna" as separate entries with POV role) — Resolver-Brief should consolidate into a canonical-character entry that captures both surface forms as aliases of one entity. Kal Jerico is the **second cross-batch character revival** (W40K-0164 + W40K-0169 + W40K-0170 in ssot-w40k-017 → W40K-0172 in ssot-w40k-018), with a soft-reboot ambiguity: modern-imprint Kal may or may not be the same character-instance as the 2005-2008 trilogy Kal (the modern imprint doesn't explicitly continue the trilogy's storyline, but the character name + setting + class are continuous). Resolver decision needed: one Kal-Jerico canonical entity with multi-era surface forms, or two distinct entities with shared name.
  - **Tag-count discipline.** Range 20-27 tags per entry (median 23.5), slightly above the Brief-061 "typisch 15-20 IDs" target — driven by the modern-imprint cluster's better coverage allowing more confident assertion of secondary themes (`vengeance`, `redemption`, `cw_socio_political`, `cw_mental_health`, `cw_risky_behaviour`) than the early/mid-2000s long-tail entries supported. Not a blocker — within the 20-25 range that ssot-w40k-016 Space-Wolves cluster also occupied.
  - **Synopsis-length elasticity.** Range ~1100-2100 chars; mode in the 1300-1700 range; modestly longer than ssot-w40k-017's 941-1614. Driven by (a) modern-imprint coverage allowing more concrete plot-detail; (b) cross-batch-arc-continuity-restatement (multiple entries reference the Caleb-Cursebound saga progression W40K-0174 → W40K-0178 → tonal continuation W40K-0179, the Mad-Donna fifteen-year revival, the Kal-Jerico Reynolds-takes-the-baton transition); and (c) the format-compliance `data_conflict` flag notes that warrant in-synopsis explanation for the three affected entries.
  - **Resolver-Pre-Note:** kumulativ ist nach diesem Batch 180. **Die nächste natural Resolver-Pause ist bei `cumulativeBefore=200`** (`ssot-w40k-021`, W40K-0201..W40K-0210), two iterations away. Surface-form-Pile seit dem ersten Resolver-Pass in 069 spans ssot-w40k-006..018 = 130 Bücher. Pile is now ~16% larger than at the most-recent skip-50-stop deferral in ssot-w40k-016. **Cowork-Empfehlung aus ssot-w40k-017 verstärkt:** the modern-imprint Necromunda cluster (this batch) introduces multi-era surface-form-revival (Mad Donna / D'onne Ulanti across 15 publication-years; Kal Jerico across 13 publication-years; soft-reboot Lord Helmawr in modern continuity vs assassinated Lord Gerontius Helmawr in classic continuity) — these are exactly the resolver-class problems the canonical-entity-consolidation pass is designed to address. **Resolver-Brief jetzt schreiben** (out-of-band, before the natural cumulative=200 pause), or accept that the next two iterations will land on top of an unresolved Necromunda-cluster surface-form-pile.
  - **Brief-071-Vertrag aktiv:** Override-Datei + Status-Log-Append in einem Commit ohne Co-Author-Trailer, keine sonstigen Datei-Edits. Lint/typecheck/brain-lint nicht gelaufen — data-only commit (eine JSON + ein Markdown-Append), keine Code-/Brain-Page-Änderungen, alle drei Lint-Targets nicht betroffen. Per Brief-061-Klausel akzeptabel.

## 2026-05-16 · ssot-w40k-019 · W40K-0181..W40K-0190 · ✅

- **Cumulative books in authority:** 190 / 200 to next resolver pause (180 before this batch + 10 written here)
- **CC model:** claude-opus-4-7
- **Pre-check:** Detected existing `manual-overrides-ssot-w40k-001..018.json` (18 × 10 = 180 books). W40K max = 18, HH max = 0, cumulative = 180, 180 % 50 ≠ 0 → no resolver pause. Next batch: `ssot-w40k-019`, slice = W40K-0181..W40K-0190 (5 Last Chancers + 3 Gothic War + 2 Soul Drinkers). No skip-50-stop marker in the maintainer eröffnungs-prompt — would be moot anyway (180 is not on the 50er-grid).
- **WebSearch:** mean ≈ 0.5 / book, max = 1 (over 10 books). 5 total searches.
  - 1 search each: W40K-0182 *Kill Team* (confirmed Tau-commander assassination + diplomatic-delegation cover), W40K-0183 *Annihilation Squad* (confirmed Armageddon / Acheron-hive setting + Overlord von Strab antagonist + Kage's emerging psychic potential + Lorii reappearance; **corrected pre-write assumption** that Coritanorum was the current setting — Coritanorum is referenced as Kage's prior-mission flashback, current setting is Armageddon), W40K-0185 *Armageddon Saint* (confirmed Kage-as-the-Burned-Man saint-cult premise + Schaeffer hunting his errant charge + pre-Cicatrix-Maledictum timing), W40K-0186 *Execution Hour* (confirmed Captain Leoten Sempter as POV + cruiser Lord Solar Macharius + Planet-Killer plot spine + Inferno!-magazine origin), W40K-0190 *The Bleeding Chalice* (confirmed Inquisitor Thaddeus POV + Teturact as daemon-prince Chaos-pole + Sarpedon's gene-stability quest + Mechanicus-facility quest target).
  - 0 searches: W40K-0181 *13th Legion* (well-covered series-opener), W40K-0184 *Last Chancers Omnibus* (aggregation from W40K-0181..0183), W40K-0187 *Shadow Point* (direct sequel to *Execution Hour*, naval-continuation), W40K-0188 *Gothic War Omnibus* (aggregation from W40K-0186..0187, contents from earlier search), W40K-0189 *Soul Drinker* (well-covered Soul Drinkers series-opener — Soulspear dispute, Sarpedon's rebellion, arachnid-Marine mutation premise).
- **Per-book bullets:**
  - **W40K-0181 *13th Legion* (Thorpe, 2001):** Last Chancers #1, series-opener. Colonel Schaeffer + Lieutenant Kage + 13th Penal Legion attritional war on Typhos Prime against Orks. Establishes the Dirty-Dozen-in-space penal-legion premise + cynical first-person memoir voice. Clean, no flags.
  - **W40K-0182 *Kill Team* (Thorpe, 2001):** Last Chancers #2. Heist-procedural — Schaeffer / Kage / fresh Last Chancers pose as Imperial diplomatic delegation on a Tau world to assassinate a Tau commander. **First Tau-Empire-as-antagonist** in the Last Chancers line. Clean.
  - **W40K-0183 *Annihilation Squad* (Thorpe, 2004):** Last Chancers #3, original-trilogy closer. Warp-shredded 40,000-light-year transit to Armageddon to kill Overlord von Strab in Ork-rebel hive Acheron. Kage's emerging psychic potential. Lorii reappears with personal-hatred motives. Ends with Kage's apparent death (resolved sixteen years later in *Armageddon Saint*). Tonal shift to cosmic_horror register. Clean.
  - **W40K-0184 *The Last Chancers Omnibus* (Thorpe, 2006):** Omnibus aggregation of W40K-0181..0183. Length_tier=doorstopper, scope=sector (multi-planet across the trilogy), entry_point=series_start (canonical entry-point omnibus). Aggregation per Brief-061 omnibus-constraint.
  - **W40K-0185 *Armageddon Saint* (Thorpe, 2020):** Last Chancers #4, after a sixteen-year publication gap. Kage returns as "the Burned Man," a saint-figure attracting a cult on Ork-infested Armageddon just before the Cicatrix Maledictum / Great Rift opens. Schaeffer hunts his errant charge; daemonic incursion threatens. Tonal pivot to faith-and-hagiography + philosophical register. **Dual character-listing**: "Lieutenant Kage" + "the Burned Man" as both POV — the saint-cult name is the narrative device. entry_point=requires_context (depends on *Annihilation Squad*). Clean.
  - **W40K-0186 *Execution Hour* (Rennie, 2001):** Gothic War #1, opens the Battlefleet-Gothic-wargame-tie-in naval-combat duology. Captain Leoten Sempter + cruiser Lord Solar Macharius vs Abaddon the Despoiler's 12th Black Crusade in the Gothic Sector. Planet Killer super-weapon as looming threat. Originally compiled from *Inferno!* magazine shorts. Naval-combat register — POV is fleet officers, tagged civilian (no `naval_officer` protagonist_class). Clean.
  - **W40K-0187 *Shadow Point* (Rennie, 2003):** Gothic War #2, direct sequel to *Execution Hour*. Imperial Navy strikes back; campaign converges on Shadow Point chokepoint. Same Sempter / Lord-Solar-Macharius POV cast. Tagged **series_finale** (de-facto) — Rennie's planned third Gothic War novel was never written. Clean.
  - **W40K-0188 *The Gothic War Omnibus* (Rennie, 2010):** Omnibus aggregation of W40K-0186..0187 + a Battlefleet Gothic comic strip from the boxed game. Length_tier=doorstopper. Aggregation per Brief-061 omnibus-constraint; tone-and-plot-type tags inherit the naval-combat register without expansion (no third-novel material).
  - **W40K-0189 *Soul Drinker* (Counter, 2002):** Soul Drinkers #1, series-opener. Sarpedon's rebellion against his Chapter Master over the Soulspear-vs-Mechanicus dispute → Soul Drinkers declared Excommunicate Traitoris → chapter begins mutating (arachnid legs on Sarpedon). Establishes the renegade-loyalist Space-Marine tragedy. Body-horror register (workaround: cosmic_horror tone-tag, no body_horror in catalog). Clean.
  - **W40K-0190 *The Bleeding Chalice* (Counter, 2003):** Soul Drinkers #2. Sarpedon's gene-stability quest + Inquisitor Thaddeus's parallel hunt + daemon-prince Teturact's chaos-pole. **Three-protagonist contrast structure** (Sarpedon renegade-loyalist / Thaddeus Imperial-orthodox / Teturact chaos-malevolent). **Inquisition-consistency triggered** (Thaddeus is POV Inquisitor) — `factions[]` includes `Inquisition` role=antagonist; specific Ordo (likely Hereticus) not source-confirmed, deferred to Resolver.
- **value_outside_vocabulary** (candidates surfaced by this batch, none promoted):
  - `penal_legion` — protagonist_class workaround for the entire Last Chancers cluster (Kage / Schaeffer / 13th-Penal-Legion soldiers); used `guardsman` as closest catalog match.
  - `naval_officer` — protagonist_class workaround for Captain Leoten Sempter + the Imperial-Navy POV cast across the Gothic War cluster; used `civilian` (the same workaround ssot-w40k-018 used for Scrutinator Servalen / Necromunda Enforcers).
  - `psyker` — protagonist_class — Kage's emerging psychic potential in *Annihilation Squad* + *Armageddon Saint* (the saint-cult arc has psychic-prescience undertones); no catalog value, defaulted to `guardsman`.
  - `naval_combat` / `space_combat` / `fleet_action` — plot_type / tone workaround for Battlefleet Gothic ship-combat (no naval-specific plot_type in catalog); used `war_story + siege + last_stand` for the rearguard-action register.
  - `hagiography` / `saint_cult` — theme workaround for *Armageddon Saint*'s saint-cult arc; used `faith + philosophical` as closest.
  - `body_horror` — theme / tone workaround for the Soul Drinkers' mutation arc + Sarpedon's arachnid-leg transformation; used `cosmic_horror` tone-tag as closest. Already raised in ssot-w40k-004 (Lost-arc body-horror register, Brief 061 notes); pattern now repeated across Soul Drinkers cluster.
  - `gene_seed_collapse` / `chapter_decline` — theme workaround for Soul Drinkers' genetic-stability fight; used `doubt + hubris + sacrifice` as closest cluster.
- **Notable surface-form frequencies within this batch:**
  - *Factions:* Imperium ×10 (every entry), Imperial Guard ×4 (Last Chancers cluster except *Armageddon Saint* shares both Imperial Guard + Last Chancers), Last Chancers ×5 (entire Last Chancers cluster), Orks ×4 (W40K-0181 + W40K-0183 + W40K-0184 omnibus + W40K-0185), Chaos ×6 (W40K-0183 + W40K-0184 omnibus + W40K-0185 + W40K-0186 + W40K-0187 + W40K-0188 omnibus + W40K-0189 + W40K-0190 — Chaos-as-antagonist is near-ubiquitous), Black Legion ×3 (Gothic War cluster), Imperial Navy ×3 (Gothic War cluster) + ×1 (W40K-0189 Soul Drinker — as Mechanicus-allied force trying to take the Soulspear), Adeptus Mechanicus ×2 (W40K-0189 antagonist + W40K-0190 supporting), Soul Drinkers ×2 (Soul Drinkers cluster), Tau Empire ×1 (W40K-0182 + W40K-0184 omnibus inheritance), Inquisition ×1 (W40K-0190 Thaddeus — **first Inquisition-consistency trigger of the batch**), Ecclesiarchy ×1 (W40K-0185 saint-cult dynamics).
  - *Locations:* Imperium ×10 (every entry), Armageddon ×3 (W40K-0183 + W40K-0184 omnibus + W40K-0185 — single-world recurrence across three batch entries), Gothic Sector ×3 (W40K-0186 + W40K-0187 + W40K-0188 omnibus), Typhos Prime ×2 (W40K-0181 + W40K-0184 omnibus), Acheron ×2 (W40K-0183 + W40K-0184 omnibus), Shadow Point ×2 (W40K-0187 + W40K-0188 omnibus), Tau Empire space ×2 (W40K-0182 + W40K-0184 omnibus).
  - *Characters:* Colonel Schaeffer ×5 (entire Last Chancers cluster — W40K-0181 + 0182 + 0183 + 0184 omnibus + 0185), Lieutenant Kage ×5 (W40K-0181 + 0182 + 0183 + 0184 omnibus + 0185 — listed under the surface form "Lieutenant Kage" plus the additional "the Burned Man" surface form on W40K-0185), Captain Leoten Sempter ×3 (Gothic War cluster), Abaddon the Despoiler ×3 (Gothic War cluster — antagonist surface form), Sarpedon ×2 (Soul Drinkers cluster), Overlord von Strab ×2 (W40K-0183 + W40K-0184 omnibus), Lorii ×2 (W40K-0183 + W40K-0184 omnibus), Inquisitor Thaddeus ×1 (W40K-0190 POV), Teturact ×1 (W40K-0190 antagonist), the Burned Man ×1 (W40K-0185 alt-surface-form for Kage).
- **Notes:**
  - **Mixed early-2000s Imperial-line cluster — three distinct sub-series in one batch.** Last Chancers (Thorpe, 2001-2020) + Gothic War (Rennie, 2001-2003) + Soul Drinkers opener (Counter, 2002-2003). No prior batch has touched any of these three lines — all surface forms are first-authority-layer. The batch represents three near-simultaneous early-2000s Black-Library debut series, two of which never reached intended completion (Gothic War's planned third book; Last Chancers' sixteen-year hiatus before *Armageddon Saint*).
  - **Two omnibus entries with multi-faction aggregation** (W40K-0184 + W40K-0188). Both tagged length_tier=doorstopper, protagonist_class=guardsman/civilian (single-class across constituents, no need for `multi`), entry_point=series_start (canonical entry-point omnibi). Aggregation per Brief-061 omnibus-constraint: factions / locations / characters unioned with role hierarchies preserved.
  - **One de-facto series-closer** (W40K-0187 *Shadow Point*). Rennie planned a third Gothic War novel — set at the war's end — that was never written. Tagged `series_finale` despite the original trilogy intention; the resolver may want to mark this with a `series_status` flag indicating "incomplete-trilogy-closed-by-default" once that vocabulary lands.
  - **Inquisition-consistency** triggered on **W40K-0190 *The Bleeding Chalice*** only — Inquisitor Thaddeus is a POV character per the Goodreads / Lexicanum plot summary. `factions[]` includes `Inquisition` with role=antagonist (≥ supporting per the Brief-061 constraint). Specific Ordo (Ordo Hereticus likely, given Soul Drinkers' Excommunicate-Traitoris quarry) not explicitly named in available source summaries; deferred to Resolver. **Not triggered** on the Last Chancers cluster (Kage / Schaeffer are Imperial Guard / Officio Prefectus penal-legion command, not Inquisition), the Gothic War cluster (naval-officer POVs, no Inquisitor POVs), or *Soul Drinker* W40K-0189 (Sarpedon is Space Marine Librarian, the chapter-vs-Mechanicus dispute is intra-Imperium; no on-page Inquisitor in the first novel).
  - **Surface-form treue.** "Imperial Guard" (over "Astra Militarum" — publication era 2001-2020 spans both naming conventions, but the source Black-Library copy and Track-of-Words / Lexicanum coverage uses "Imperial Guard" for the Last Chancers line, including the 2020 *Armageddon Saint*). "Tau Empire" (over "T'au" — publication era pre-9th-edition; the 2001 *Kill Team* uses "Tau"). "Imperial Navy" (consistent across the Gothic War cluster). "Black Legion" (over "Sons of Horus" — Gothic War is M41, post-Black-Legion-naming). "Adeptus Mechanicus" (consistent).
  - **Last Chancers dual character-listing** on W40K-0185. The narrative device is that the saint-cult knows the figure as "the Burned Man" while Schaeffer knows him as Kage. Both surface forms are listed with role=pov, mirroring the ssot-w40k-018 W40K-0177 *Soulless Fury* dual-listing of "D'onne Ulanti" + "Mad Donna" as both POV. Resolver-Brief should consolidate into a canonical-character entry with alias-tracking — a third cross-entry alias-consolidation case in three consecutive batches (after Mad Donna in ssot-w40k-018 and Kal Jerico in ssot-w40k-017→018).
  - **No format-compliance `data_conflict` flags raised** — SSOT roster classifications (novel/novel/novel/omnibus/novel/novel/novel/omnibus/novel/novel) match Black-Library + Lexicanum + Goodreads classifications across the slice. Unlike the modern-Necromunda cluster in ssot-w40k-018 (three format conflicts), the early-2000s Black-Library line predates the Novella-Series imprints, so format-classification is uniformly correct.
  - **Tag-count discipline.** Range 22-30 tags per entry (median 25); two omnibus entries push to 30 tags (length_tier=doorstopper + multi-faction aggregation + cross-trilogy tone-tag union). Slightly above the Brief-061 "typisch 15-20 IDs" target but within the established range for omnibus + Last-Chancers-style multi-mission narratives.
  - **Synopsis-length elasticity.** Range ~1100-1700 chars; mode in the 1200-1400 range; lower than ssot-w40k-018's 1300-2000 range — early-2000s coverage is less plot-detailed than modern-imprint coverage, so synopses default to tighter plot-spines without speculative-subplot-elaboration. The *Armageddon Saint* synopsis pushes toward the upper bound because the saint-cult premise + sixteen-year publication-gap require more context to land.

- **Per-book bullets:**
  - **W40K-0191 *Crimson Tears* (Counter, 2005):** Soul Drinkers #3, first-trilogy closer. Tellos re-emerged after apparent death on Stratix Lumine, now wholly Chaos-corrupted. Sarpedon hunts him. Faction-breadth peak of the trilogy — Chaos + Dark Eldar + Imperial Guard + Crimson Fists all on-page. Body-horror / cosmic_horror tone register continues. Clean.
  - **W40K-0192 *The Soul Drinkers Omnibus* (Counter, 2006):** Omnibus aggregation of W40K-0189..0191. Length_tier=doorstopper, scope=sector, entry_point=series_start (canonical entry-point omnibus). Aggregation per Brief-061 omnibus-constraint — factions/locations/characters unioned across the three constituent novels.
  - **W40K-0193 *Chapter War* (Counter, 2007):** Soul Drinkers #4, opening second-half-arc. Vanqualis Ork-invasion as redemption-attempt for the chapter; internal factions move against Sarpedon toward Chaos (chapter-civil-war brewing); Howling Griffons arrive as Imperial reinforcements that target the renegades. Three-front conflict. Internal-traitor character not source-named in available coverage, kept unnamed in synopsis. Clean.
  - **W40K-0194 *Hellforged* (Counter, 2009):** Soul Drinkers #5. Chapter flees to galactic rim, encounters Necrons + Mechanicus-pursuit + sustained damage to the Brokenback (their captured Chaos-cruiser-hulk). Three-faction battle. First authority-layer Necrons in the Soul Drinkers line. Clean.
  - **W40K-0195 *Daenyathos* (Counter, 2010):** Soul Drinkers prequel-novella, set between *Hellforged* and *Phalanx*. Centuries-spanning life of Chaplain Daenyathos (Second Siege of Terra → dreadnought-interment → mysterious disappearance), with the Catechisms Martial revealed as a long-game corruption scheme he engineered to turn the chapter against the Imperium. Major series-twist novella. Length_tier=novella, entry_point=requires_context. Clean.
  - **W40K-0196 *Phalanx* (Counter, 2012):** Soul Drinkers #6, series finale. Imperial Fists capture the chapter and put them on trial on the Phalanx star-fort with multi-faction audience (Inquisitors + Sisters of Battle + Mechanicus + multiple Chapters). Iktinos's faithful break under interrogation → reveal Daenyathos's Selaaca vault → Daenyathos brought to Phalanx for trial. Sarpedon's final actions; bittersweet end. Tonal pivot to court_intrigue + character_study. **Inquisition-consistency triggered** (Inquisitors on-page as trial-audience). Clean.
  - **W40K-0197 *Soul Drinkers: Annihilation Second Omnibus* (Counter, 2013):** Omnibus aggregation of W40K-0193 + 0194 + 0196 + shorts. Length_tier=doorstopper, entry_point=requires_context (second-half-arc, not series-start). Inquisition surface form propagates via Phalanx constituent. Aggregation per Brief-061 omnibus-constraint.
  - **W40K-0198 *Traitor by Deed* (Counter, 2020):** Soul Drinkers post-Cicatrix-Maledictum Primaris-reboot novella. Indomitus-Crusade era. Primaris Soul Drinkers (bearing the name and heraldry of the chapter lost at Phalanx) sent to Kepris to break the cult of arch-heretic Yeceqath the Voice of All. Ancient-enemy conspiracy in the background. Length_tier=novella, entry_point=standalone (Primaris-reboot continuity). **Soft-reboot continuity question** for Resolver: Firstborn vs Primaris Soul Drinkers — same name, same heraldry, different gene-seed-tier-cohort, fifteen-year publication gap, post-Cicatrix continuity. Clean.
  - **W40K-0199 *Crossfire* (Farrer, 2003):** Shira Calpurnia #1. Calpurnia (female, arbiter senioris of the Adeptus Arbites) transferred to Hydraphur, investigates assassination attempts on herself. Lord Medell of a great noble house behind the scheme — uses an Arbites-officer-assassination as cover for festival-grounds security tightening. Bell-tower climax during religious festival; Sister killed by Medell's servitor; Calpurnia gravely injured. **First non-Necromunda female-POV in the W40K authority layer + first Adeptus Arbites primary-faction + first procedural-mystery / political-thriller plot-type concentration.** Tonally orthogonal to the surrounding Space-Marine grimdark. Clean.
  - **W40K-0200 *Legacy* (Farrer, 2004):** Shira Calpurnia #2, direct sequel to *Crossfire*. Rogue Trader Hoyyon Phrax has died; his Charter of Trade (Emperor-signed, holy-relic-dimension) must be ceremonially passed to his heir at Hydraphur. Calpurnia administers the legal process. Rival heirs go to arms; ambitious Ecclesiarchy clerics form a secondary threat-thread. Plot-type drift from *Crossfire*'s mystery toward court_intrigue. Clean.

Slightly above Brief-061 "typisch 15-20 IDs" target but within the established range for omnibus + series-finale entries.
  - **Synopsis-length elasticity.** Range ~1294-2140 chars; mode in the 1400-1700 range; comparable to ssot-w40k-018's 1300-2000 range. Two longest entries: *Phalanx* (2140 chars — series-finale with trial-mechanism + Daenyathos-reveal + multi-faction audience requires substantial context to land); *Traitor by Deed* (1906 chars — Primaris-reboot continuity needs explicit framing as soft-reboot relative to *Phalanx*'s firstborn-chapter closure). Shortest: *Chapter War* + *Hellforged* (~1295 chars — single-faction-antagonist-driven war-stories without omnibus / reveal / reboot framing).
  - **Resolver-Pre-Note:** kumulativ ist nach diesem Batch 200. **Die nächste Iteration (`ssot-w40k-021`, W40K-0201..W40K-0210) trifft den natürlichen 50er-Stop** — `cumulativeBefore=200`, `200 % 50 == 0`, **Resolver-Pause loud-stop garantiert** unless `skip-50-stop` marker im Maintainer-Prompt. Dies ist der letzte sauber-produzierte Batch vor der Pause. Surface-form-pile seit dem ersten Resolver-Pass in 069 spans nun ssot-w40k-006..020 = 150 Bücher und enthält fünf resolver-class problems waiting to crystallise: (1) Mad Donna / D'onne Ulanti (ssot-w40k-017 W40K-0162 + ssot-w40k-018 W40K-0177); (2) Kal Jerico classic vs modern-imprint (ssot-w40k-017 + ssot-w40k-018); (3) Lord Helmawr / Lord Gerontius Helmawr soft-reboot (ssot-w40k-017 + ssot-w40k-018); (4) Lieutenant Kage / the Burned Man dual-listing (ssot-w40k-019 W40K-0185); (5) Soul Drinkers Firstborn vs Primaris (ssot-w40k-019 + ssot-w40k-020 W40K-0189..0197 vs W40K-0198). Plus the new Adeptus-Arbites + Hydraphur + Phrax-Charter + Hoyyon-Phrax + Lord-Medell + Shira-Calpurnia first-authority-layer Calpurnia-cluster surface-forms. **Cowork-Empfehlung verstärkt:** Resolver-Brief jetzt schreiben — the natural cumulative=200 pause is exactly the maintainer-trigger this loop-brief was designed to surface.
  - **Brief-071-Vertrag aktiv:** Override-Datei + Status-Log-Append in einem Commit ohne Co-Author-Trailer, keine sonstigen Datei-Edits. Lint/typecheck/brain-lint nicht gelaufen — data-only commit (eine JSON + ein Markdown-Append), keine Code-/Brain-Page-Änderungen, alle drei Lint-Targets nicht betroffen. Per Brief-061-Klausel akzeptabel.

## 2026-05-16 · ⏸ Resolver-Pause bei 200 Büchern

- **Cumulative books:** 200 (in 20 batches: ssot-w40k-001..ssot-w40k-020). W40K max = 20, HH max = 0.
- **Pre-check:** Detected 20 existing `manual-overrides-ssot-w40k-001..020.json` (20 × 10 = 200 books). `cumulativeBefore = 200`, `200 % 50 == 0` und `> 0` → **natural Resolver-Pause-Schwelle erreicht, loud-stop ausgelöst**. Next batch wäre `ssot-w40k-021` (W40K-0201..W40K-0210), NICHT geschrieben. Dies ist die **vierte natural-50er-Schwelle** seit Loop-Start (50 / 100 / 150 / 200) und die **zweite tatsächlich respektierte Resolver-Pause** im Pause-Block-Sinne — die 50er-Schwelle bei cumulative=50 hat den ersten echten Resolver-Pass in Brief 069 ausgelöst; die 100er-Schwelle wurde via `skip-50-stop`-Marker übersprungen (ssot-w40k-011); die 150er-Schwelle wurde mit Pause-Block-only-Commit gehandhabt + danach via `skip-50-stop`-Marker fortgesetzt (ssot-w40k-016, kein Resolver-Brief dazwischen geschrieben); 200er-Schwelle hier ist die nächste echte Pause ohne Skip-Marker.
- **Skip-marker?** none detected in maintainer prompt — Loop hat den 50er-Stop respektiert. Brief-071-Vertrag explizit auf 50er-Loud-Stop-Pfad gesetzt (Acceptance-Bullet auf Brief-061-Zeile 131 = Wahrheit; Brief-061-Constraint-Note auf Zeile 79 überschrieben für den Pause-Pfad: KEINE Override-Datei, aber Status-Log-Pause-Block committed). Vorherige Iteration (ssot-w40k-020) hat diese Pause exakt vorhergesagt im Resolver-Pre-Note ("Die nächste Iteration trifft den natürlichen 50er-Stop — Resolver-Pause loud-stop garantiert unless `skip-50-stop`-Marker im Maintainer-Prompt").
- **Action required:** Maintainer schreibt **zweiten echten Resolver-Brief** (OQ4 + OQ5). Surface-Form-Crystallization für ssot-w40k-006..020 = 150 Bücher seit dem ersten Resolver-Pass in 069 (akkumulierte Pile über die letzten fünfzehn Iterationen). Aus der ssot-w40k-020-Resolver-Pre-Note bereits konsolidiert — **fünf cluster-class resolver problems** stehen in scharfer Form: (1) Mad Donna / D'onne Ulanti dual-surface-form (ssot-w40k-017 W40K-0162 + ssot-w40k-018 W40K-0177); (2) Kal Jerico classic vs modern-imprint dual-canonicity (ssot-w40k-017 + ssot-w40k-018); (3) Lord Helmawr / Lord Gerontius Helmawr soft-reboot (ssot-w40k-017 + ssot-w40k-018); (4) Lieutenant Kage / the Burned Man dual-listing (ssot-w40k-019 W40K-0185); (5) Soul Drinkers Firstborn vs Primaris cohort-distinction (ssot-w40k-019 + ssot-w40k-020 W40K-0189..0197 vs W40K-0198). Plus die Last-Chancers / Gothic-War / Soul-Drinkers-Subset aus ssot-w40k-019. Loop pausiert bis Resolver-Brief geschrieben + Apply-Sweep durchgelaufen ist (Brief 060 idempotent re-applied gegen 001..020 nach Resolver-Crystallisation).
- **Maintainer-Trigger zum Fortsetzen:** (a) nächste CC-Session mit Resolver-Brief (Cowork-Tendenz — pile ist nun das doppelte der Pile-Größe bei der ssot-w40k-011-skip-deferral; weiter zu verschieben verschärft das Resolver-Problem ohne Vorteil), oder (b) Loop-Brief mit explizitem `skip-50-stop`-Marker im Eröffnungs-Prompt (verschiebt Resolver weiter nach hinten; nächste natural-stop bei `cumulative=250` mit ssot-w40k-026, W40K-0251..W40K-0260).

## 2026-05-17 · ⏭ Pilot Synopsis-Rewrite ssot-w40k-020 (Brief 080)

- **Trigger:** Maintainer-Review der Public-`/buch/[slug]`-Seite am 2026-05-17 zeigte Markdown-Sterne + SSOT-IDs + Brief-Refs + "authority layer"-Vokabular + "surface form"-Tails durchgängig in Welle-2/3/4-Batches. Brief 080 schließt die Lücke zwischen kodifizierter Discipline (Brief 061 § Public-Synopsis-Discipline, forward-only ab `ssot-w40k-021`) und Apply-Layer-Enforcement. **Pilot:** Rewrite der 10 Synopsen im pollutedsten Batch (020) als Voice-Kalibrierung, bevor Folge-Brief 081 die restlichen 110 Bücher in 11 Iterationen abarbeitet.
- **Track A — Synopsis-Rewrite:** 10 / 10 Bücher (W40K-0191..W40K-0200). Nur `overrides.synopsis` pro Buch geändert; alle anderen Felder byte-identisch (facetIds + factions[] + locations[] + characters[] + flags[] + Top-Level $schema/batch/createdBy/createdAt/model/rationale). Re-Apply-Lauf (`npm run db:apply-override -- --batch=ssot-w40k-020`) grün, 10 `works.synopsis`-Rows updated, kein Guard-Throw.
- **Pre lengths:** ~1294–2140 chars, median ~1500 (curation-chrome dense: Markdown-Bold um jeden Property-Namen, SSOT-IDs in Cross-Refs, "First authority-layer X surface forms"-Audit-Tails).
- **Post lengths:** min 412 (`hellforged`), max 556 (`the-soul-drinkers-omnibus`), mean 475 chars (Standalones 412–487, Omnibi 546–556). Korridor: 200–500 mit Soft-Cap 600 für Omnibi, mean-Soll 300–400 laut Brief.
- **Mean-Diskussion:** 475 liegt **über** dem Brief-Soll 300–400, **innerhalb** des Korridors 200–500 (Soft-Cap 600). Empirischer Voice-Korridor aus den von Brief 080 referenzierten clean batches 001..008 (Eisenhorn / Ravenor / Pariah) sitzt bei 456–478 chars — meine Standalones (mean 464) treffen exakt diesen Korridor. Cowork kann für Folge-Brief 081 entscheiden: (a) härter trimmen auf 300–400-Soll, oder (b) den 450–480-Empirie-Korridor akzeptieren als de-facto-voice. Brief-Soll und Empirie-Korridor stimmen heute nicht überein; ein Sentence von Maintainer-Feedback klärt das eindeutig.
- **Omnibi-Begründung:** beide Omnibi (W40K-0192 `the-soul-drinkers-omnibus` 556 chars; W40K-0197 `soul-drinkers-annihilation-second-omnibus` 546 chars) liegen ~50 chars über dem Standalone-Cap. Drei-Sätze-Formel (Setup-Sentence + Arc-Spanning-Sentence + Tonality-Sentence) brauchte beide Bögen — bei W40K-0192 die Rebellion + die Mutations-Tragödie; bei W40K-0197 die zweite Hälfte (Chapter-War + Hellforged + Phalanx) in einem Bogen. Soft-Cap 600 nicht erreicht.
- **Banned-pattern Re-Mess (per Brief § Notes mess-Befehl):** `**` = 0, `authority-layer` = 0, `Brief-NNN` = 0, `W40K-NNNN` = 0. Alle vier Pattern-Klassen sauber.
- **Voice notes for follow-up loop 081:**
  - **Opening pattern:** ~6/10 premise-first ("Years after his apparent death on Stratix Lumine, Tellos…" / "The Soul Drinkers have been taken alive by the Imperial Fists…" / "The death of a rich and ancient Rogue Trader…"); ~4/10 setup-first ("Bloodied from chapter-civil-war…" / "An Indomitus-Crusade reconquest sends…" / "Newly promoted to arbiter senioris, Shira Calpurnia…" / "A prequel-novella told across centuries…"). Beide Forms tragen Calpurnia und Sarpedon gut; premise-first ist die Mehrheit weil die meisten Bücher einen klaren character-act oder event als Eröffnungs-Hook haben.
  - **In-universe Vokabular-Level:** "Astartes" / "Arbites" / "Excommunicate Traitoris" / "Indomitus Crusade" / "Cicatrix Maledictum" / "Ecclesiarchy" / "Mechanicus" werden ohne Glossierung verwendet (Reader-übliche Faction-Kürzel; nicht "Space Marines of the Imperium"). Eigennamen wie "Brokenback" / "Catechisms Martial" / "the Phalanx" tragen kurze Inline-Erklärung wenn nicht selbsterklärend ("the chapter's captured Chaos-cruiser fortress"). Soul-Drinkers-Faction-Name + Sarpedon-Charakter-Name werden nicht erklärt (load-bearing series identity).
  - **Tonality-Marker als Prose:** "A character-study of command under unbearable cost, and the close of the first Soul Drinkers trilogy." / "The procedural shades into court-intrigue." / "A tight standalone novella that re-establishes the chapter for the post-Maledictum era." — jeweils im closing sentence, keine standalone audit-tags wie "Tonal pivot from war_story to court_intrigue" mehr.
  - **Omnibus-Formel:** kein per-constituent walkthrough. Beide Omnibi nutzen 3-Sätze: (1) Setup (was die Series ist), (2) Arc-spanning (was passiert über die Bücher hinweg), (3) Tonality-Closer (warum der Reader das lesen sollte). Wirkte natürlicher als die 1-Satz-Reset-Form; rechtfertigt die ~550-char-Länge.
  - **Daenyathos-Twist:** **bewahrt** (centuries-long Catechisms-Martial-Korruptions-Scheme als reveal). Die existing polluted synopsis spoilte den twist bereits voll; partial obfuscation wäre erfunden gewesen. Cowork entscheidet, ob Folge-Brief 081 eine general "twist-protection"-Klausel braucht oder ob spoilers in synopses gegen Reader-Erwartung OK sind (Lexicanum + Goodreads spoilen frei).
  - **Faction-Name-Choices:** "Dark Eldar" (period-treue für 2005 era Crimson Tears, nicht "Drukhari" der 8th-edition). "Imperial Guard" (2005, nicht "Astra Militarum"). "Sisters of Battle" (2012, beide Begriffe live aber Black-Library copy bevorzugt). "Adeptus Mechanicus" + "Imperial Fists" + "Necrons" konsistent. Period-Treue über strikte Konsistenz priorisiert — die Synopsen-Voice soll period-eigen lesen.
- **Track B — Apply-Layer-Forward-Guard:** separater Commit (siehe Repo-Log Brief-080-Track-B). Pure Helper `scripts/apply-override-synopsis-lint.ts` analog 077-Skip-Helper-Pattern; Pattern-Liste in `scripts/seed-data/synopsis-banned-patterns.json` (32 Pattern-Einträge nach Review-Fix für Footnote-Style-Marker); hard throw in `scripts/apply-override.ts` als batch-level pre-pass (alle Bücher mit Treffern in einem Throw aggregiert), report-only in `scripts/apply-override-dry.ts` (Per-Batch-Telemetrie für Folge-Brief 081). `scripts/test-synopsis-lint.ts` 14/14 grün.
- **Dry-Run-Telemetrie (Pre-Mess-Baseline für Brief 081, post-Track-A re-mess):** ssot-w40k-001..004 clean (0 hits); ssot-w40k-005 = 1 hit / 1 book; ssot-w40k-006 = 2 hits / 2 books; ssot-w40k-007 = 31 hits / 5 books; ssot-w40k-008 = 7 hits / 6 books; ssot-w40k-009 = 18 hits / 9 books; ssot-w40k-010 = 110 / 10; ssot-w40k-011 = 243 / 10; ssot-w40k-012 = 239 / 10; ssot-w40k-013 = 309 / 10; ssot-w40k-014 = 321 / 10; ssot-w40k-015 = 369 / 10; ssot-w40k-016 = 476 / 10; ssot-w40k-017 = 350 / 10; ssot-w40k-018 = 499 / 10; ssot-w40k-019 = 384 / 10; **ssot-w40k-020 = clean** (post-Pilot). Total post-Pilot: 3359 hits in 123 books. Folge-Brief 081 fasst 11 Iterationen (`ssot-w40k-009..019`). Erwartung pro Pilot-Token-Verbrauch: jede Iteration sollte unter 50k Tokens bleiben.
- **Unerwartete Finding (Pre-Mess-Telemetrie):** Brief 080 § Context-Tabelle erwartet 001..008 als clean; tatsächlich zeigen 005..008 je 1-31 Treffer. Vermutlich seltene Edge-Cases (z. B. typografische cross-refs wie `*Crossfire*` oder authority-layer-Vokabular in den frühen audit-tails). **Nicht in 080 gefixt** — out-of-scope. Cowork sollte für Folge-Brief 081 entscheiden, ob diese auch rewriten oder als Pattern-Justierung in der banned-patterns.json behandeln.
- **Maintainer-Bedienung als nächstes:** (a) Public-Review der 10 Pilot-Synopsen auf `/buch/<slug>` — empfohlen: `crossfire` / `legacy` / `the-soul-drinkers-omnibus` / `phalanx` als repräsentativen Querschnitt; (b) Voice-Feedback an Cowork für Folge-Brief 081; (c) Folge-Brief 081 schreiben (Standing-Loop für ssot-w40k-009..019, 1 Batch pro `/clear`-Subsession, kein WebSearch, Voice-Konvention aus dem Pilot oder maintainer-präzisiert).
- **Brief-080-Vertrag aktiv:** Track B + Track A in separaten Commits ohne Co-Author-Trailer (Track B first so the guard is live when Track A lands); Re-Apply Batch 020 grün; smoke 3 Slugs (legacy + the-soul-drinkers-omnibus + daenyathos) DB-direkt verifiziert (DetailPanel rendert plain `{book.synopsis}` ohne Markdown-Parser — DB-Text = page-output). Maintainer caught it. - **Voice notes:** Premise-first for the four hooks that carry their own gravity (0072 Iron-Father-quest, 0073 Sahaal-resurfaces, 0076 class-war-thriller, 0080 first-person Grey-Knights retrospective); setup-first for the two where the world IS the hook (0074 episodic Iron-Snakes culture, 0075 isolated-Kaelor → Naois). 4/6 premise vs 2/6 setup — slightly more premise-leaning than the 6/10 Pilot ratio because the book-line here skews to character-driven 40K standalones rather than ensemble-piece omnibi. Period-treue 2004–2012 register held: Iron Hands, Iron Snakes, Night Lords, Grey Knights, Space Wolves, Imperial Navy, Inquisition, Dark Eldar (for 2005 Lord-of-the-Night + 2007 Brothers-of-the-Snake, period-correct), Eldar (not Aeldari, for the 2007 Goto novel), Slaaneshi (lowercase-adjective form). Tonality closings as prose: "a Mechanicus-theological quest novel" / "where the legion's primarch-orphaned politics weigh as much as the manhunt itself" / "oath and hospitality and kin-debt ethics threaded through every tale" / "a dense interior Eldar-politics piece rather than a wider-40K war-story" / "Ship-as-society at full scale." / "incorruptible but not infallible, the moral cost is the load-bearing spine."
- **Touched clean books?** none — W40K-0071/0077/0078/0079 left byte-identical (clean per detector, reader-dense already; no Voice-Drift pressure inside this batch since the rewrites and the originals coexist comfortably for the Iron-Father/Sahaal/Priad/Naois/Becket/Hyperion line-up).
- **`low_confidence`-/Twist-Policy-Calls:** none. The pre-existing W40K-0075 `low_confidence` flag (thin secondary-character coverage for Eldar Prophecy) and the W40K-0074 `data_conflict` flag (novel-vs-fix-up format question) are byte-identical — pre-existing scope, not 081's. The rewritten 0075 synopsis already stays at the Naois + Houses + Slaanesh-implication level so it never leans on uncertain secondary-character names that the flag warns about. No twist obfuscation needed — the Months-of-Shame frame for 0080 is widely-known canon, Acerbus for 0073 is the named engine of the chase, and Slaanesh-implication for 0075 is openly hedged in the source.
- **Iteration time / token estimate:** ~30k–40k tokens. Detection via loop-log-tail grep was crisp (one-shot); the bulk went to drafting + length tuning (eldar-prophecy needed three passes to land in the 500–620 standalone band).
- **Carry-over notes:** (a) Standalone-band 500–620 holds tightly for single-POV books with a single focal arc (0072 at 568, 0075 at 523). Books with dual focal characters (0073 Sahaal+Mita at 682, 0076 Becket+Ward at 674) or episodic linked-story structure (0074 Priad+squad at 641) or first-person-with-secondary-Inquisition-anchor (0080 Hyperion+Annika at 749) naturally drift into the 620–750 multi-POV band even though publishers list them as single-volume standalones. Either widening the standalone band for dual-focal/episodic structures or formally counting these as multi-POV would match practice — same observation as batch-007's Bildungsroman/tie-in note. (b) Detection-algorithm-Variante-B (Codex liest tail des loop-logs) worked cleanly this time: `grep "Synopsis-Rewrite ssot-w40k-" sessions/ssot-loop-log.md | tail` returned 005/006/007, so 008 was unambiguous. The batches-worktree branch (`codex/ingest-batches-synopsis-005-019`) was correctly aligned with `66407ea` (batch 007) at session start, so no cross-branch-confusion this time. (c) Next iteration: `ssot-w40k-009` (9 books with hits, 18 total — last warm-up batch before the Welle-3 voll-getroffen wall at 010+ which jumps to 110 hits / 10 books).

  - W40K-0484 Vaults of Obsidian: anthology aggregated across ~12 stories / ~10 authors per the §6 omnibus rule. `audiobook` tag deliberately omitted — could not confirm a Black Library audiobook edition from sources; left at `book` only.
  - W40K-0485 Ascension: tagged `series_finale` — Blackstone Fortress novel arc is a 2-book Hinks set (BSF + Ascension); the anthology sits between them but doesn't continue Draik's POV thread. The Archivist mapped to `antagonist` per source's "duplicitous alien" framing.
  - W40K-0486 Attack of the Necron: middle-grade Warhammer Adventures conventions applied throughout the next 5 entries — `civilian`, `ensemble`, `short`, `cw_parental_guidance`. Mekki's Martian/Mechanicus origin is backstory only this volume; not added to `factions`.
  - W40K-0487 Claws of the Genestealer: `locations` left empty — synopsis names only an unnamed "remote ice world"; refused to invent a place name. Genestealer mapped to `Tyranids` faction (canonical parent).
  - W40K-0488 Secrets of the Tau: `T'au Empire` carried as primary (apostrophe surface form per current BL canon; book title drops the apostrophe). Captain Harleen Amity tagged supporting under `Rogue Traders` — synopsis calls her a "pirate" but Black Library positions her as a rogue trader captain.
  - W40K-0489 War of the Orks: added `satirical` tone for the Ork tribal warfare framing. Amity again under `Rogue Traders`.
  - W40K-0490 Plague of the Nurglings: `Adeptus Mechanicus` primary (forge world Aparitus), `Inquisition` supporting (Jeremias, Ordo unspecified — kept generic), `Chaos Daemons` + `Nurgle` both `antagonist`. Per §7 Inquisition-Konsistenz, Jeremias is supporting not POV so this is just safe coverage.
- **value_outside_vocabulary:** []
- **Notable surface-forms (within this batch):** Ziasuthra (craftworld surface — post-Great Rift introduction in Ghost Warrior), Saim-Hann (canonical hyphenation), Ynnari (canonical), T'au Empire (apostrophe form vs book title's apostrophe-less "Tau"), Adeptus Mechanicus (full canonical name preferred over short "Mechanicus"), The Archivist, Inquisitor Jeremias.

  - HH-0048 (The Burden of Loyalty): true multi-author anthology; left `characters` thin and added a `low_confidence`/`characters` flag — only the Wolf King and Sigillite POVs surfaced cleanly from external coverage.
  - HH-0049 (Wolfsbane): single-novel; included Belisarius Cawl as a supporting character per his first-fiction appearance (notable for later 40k continuity), Mechanicum supporting via the Trisolian forge fleet.
  - HH-0050 (Born of Flame): Salamanders anthology; aggregates Promethean Sun, Scorched Earth and the Sons of the Forge novel; antagonist tags Word Bearers + Night Lords come from the Isstvan V / Nocturne arcs covered by the constituent works.
